Wele gug qocna Anut uqa sao mahaca ifanen .
Odocob maha eu ihulahal tanac gauc nijen . Wa ben tatacan tu ahulec cilehdu nijen . Odocob Anut uqana kis eu wa tatacan jojoi cobon .
Odocob Anut madeceb , “ Camajac calagale , ” eceb camajac calen .
Anut camajac me bahic eu fimei waug ceelen . Odimei Anut camajac tuca filiganalen .
Camajac eu Anut uqa ijan “ Cahineg ” qon . Tu eu ijan “ Witic ” qon . Odocob witic mimei cojagen . Eu deel matu .
Odocob Anut madeceb , “ Wa ohisdecca wa mahanadecca filiganalecnu qagojoc oso calagale , ” eceb eu odi calen .
Qagojoc eu Anut uqa ifanen eu wa mahanadecca wa ohisdecca filiganalen .
Odocob Anut qagojoc eu ijan “ Sao ” qon . Odocob witic mimei cojagen . Eu deel lecis doc .
Odocob Anut madeceb , “ Wa sao bisalu eu cudun osahicna gabandocob cudun galalec caleiale , ” eceb eu odi calen .
Odocob Anut cudun galalec eu ijan “ Maha ” qon . Odocob wa cudun osahicna gabandon eu ijan “ Macas ” qon . Anut eu me bahic fimei waug ceelen .
Odocob Anut madeceb , “ Mahana celumca na sihul filfil me qonaca cehelo gug filfil aig qonaca caleigale , ” eceb eu odi calen .
Eunu mahana celumca na sihul filfil me qonaca cehelo gug filfil aig qonaca eu odi calein . Anut eu me bahic fimei waug ceelen .
Odocob witic mimei cojagen . Eu deel ijed doc .
Odocob Anut madeceb , “ Cahineg witicca filiganalecnu cabi saenca deelca cabi gelca gadac mecnu fulacdoc saona caleigale .
Fulacdoc i age maha fulacdoc utuqagannu saona tawoqagan , ” eceb eu odi calen .
Oodon Anut uqa fulacdoc benben lecis mudalen . Fulacdoc ben bahic eu cahineg cofdocnu muden . Fulacdoc nag eu witic cofdocnu muden . Uqa malaqaha mudaden .
Anut uqa maha fulacdoc utuqagannuca cahineg witicca cofdocnuca fulacdoc tuca filiganalecnuca fulacdoc i age saona maden . Anut eu me bahic fimei waug ceelen .

Odocob witic mimei cojagen . Eu deel wal oso doc .
Odocob Anut madeceb , “ Wana ceteteh cunug cebac nijuqagan eu fulusdoigale . Euha maha ohisnaca sao bisalunaca man fululec fululi coboigale , ” eceb eu odi calen .
Odimei Anut macasnadec dool benben ifanen . Ceteteh cunug cebac cobogina agena sihul filfil toodudu wana am ben . Man fululec sihul filfil cunug euha ifanen . Anut eu me bahic fimei waug ceelen .
Odimei Anut eeladi maaden , “ Fulusdumeig mati bahic caleigale . Macas cunug ihoc leigale . Mahana man fululec fulusdumeig mati bahic calimeig maha cunug ihoc leigale , ” aden .
Odocob witic mimei cojagen . Eu deel ebum oso doc .
Odocob Anut madeceb , “ Mahana dool gug filfil mananca cusca benca nagca caleigale , ” eceb eu odi calen .
Odimei Anut uqa mahanadec dool manan sihul filfilca dool cus sihul filfilca ceteteh mahana cobogina sihul filfilca mudaden . Anut eu me bahic fimei waug ceelen .
Odocob Anut maden , “ Ege dana cajaca mudalecnu . Ege ihocomige qumeb ege cinigwe mudalecnu . Odocob ale dool wanadecca man fululec saonadecca dool mananca maha cunugca ceteteh cunug mahana cobogina eu cofadowasin , ” en .
Odimei Anut uqadodoc ihocon qu dana cajaca ifanalen . Manahal aidca uqa ifanalen .
Odimei Anut eelali maalen , “ Mel basimesi fulusdosiale . Odimesi maha cunug ihoc limesi ilo bilesiale . Macasnadec doolca saonadec man fululecca ceteteh cunug mahana cebac cobogina eu cunugnu ale ilo bilesiale , ” alen .
Odimei uqa maalen , “ Fesia ! Celum aig qona gug filfilca cehelo aig qona gug filfilca ija wele alem euqa maha olana ihoc leia nijia . Cehelo eu age agena aig eu alena sab biligian .
Qa mahanadec dool cunugca saonadec man fululec cunugca ceteteh cunug mahana cebac coboginaca eu age celum gigica cunug eu agena sab adiga , ” alen . Odocob eu odi nijen .
Odimei Anut ceteteh cunug uqa mudaden eu me bahic fimei waug ceel bahic en . Odocob witic mimei cojagen . Eu deel eben gic osahicca doc .
Aria sao mahaca ceteteh cunug ifanen . Eu uqana cabi hedon .
Deel eben naha gic lecisca qee ihoc lec Anut uqana ifanec cabi cunug hedon . Odimei jaen muden .
Oodon Anut uqa ifanec cabi cunug hedumei jaen muden eunu deel eben naha gic lecisca eu eeldumei qagu fil men .
Je i saen Anut sao mahaca ifanalennu je . Tibud Anut uqa maha saoca ifanalen saen euna
uqa mahana wa qee suldol . Dana cabi cehecnu ha qee mudel . Eunu gigi o celum oso mahana qee cajec nijen .
Qa wa tut gaid mahanadec cajimei maha cunug wa utoloi .
Odocob Tibud Anut uqa colig mahanadec umei dana oso muden . Odimei mede gigil ocna kis cebac eu fuldutocob dana cebac men .
Aria Tibud Anut cabi oso cam tobi becna isec Iden ono cehen . Odimei dana uqa ifani mudon eu ono muden .
Odocob Tibud Anut uqa odocob mahanadec na cunug fecnu galeca sabnu me bahic eu cajein . Cabi gemo na lecis tawesin . Oso uqa na aig jifei cebac biligian . Oso uqa aig eu jifei doc meca me qeeca ugian .
Aria wa tut oso Idendec boloi . Eu cabi wa utoloi . Odimei eunadec wa eu batac qu wal oso don .
Wa batac matu eu ijan Pison . Wa eu nuimei Hawila hatu eu cunug taldona . Hatu euna gol nijina .
Hatu eunadec gol eu me bahic . Ono na oso nijina eu uqana gilic eu dedeman me bahic . Eu ijan deliam . Euna ha meen oso nijina . Eu ijan oniks .
Wa oso , eu ijan Gion , eu nuimei Kus hatu eu cunug taldona .
Wa oso ijan eu Taigris . Eu Asiria cam tobi becna isec nuina . Wa oso ijan eu Jufretis .
Aria Tibud Anut uqa dana eu umei Iden cabi dunuh muden . Cabi cehigiannuca cofdugiannuca muden .
Odocob Tibud Anut dana dahig hehewi bili je gagadic odi madon , “ Hina na aig cunug cabina nijia eu cois jagale .
Qa doc meca me qeecanu na eu aig cain jagaun . Hina eu jegaqa deel euna himec hina cal megan , ” don .
Aria odocob Tibud Anut maden , “ Dana uqa cuhanuc bilec me qee . Ija uqa cesuldoc oso muditugen , ” en .
Eunu Tibud Anut maha leih cedimei dool mahanadecca man fululec saonadecca cunug mudaden . Odimei dana ijanaga aqeceb figia bili cedadi danaca ehadi len . Odocob dana uqa dool cunug osahicosahic ijanaga qon . Ijanaga qon eu age ijanaga ibuldon .
Oodon dana uqa dool mananca man fululec saonadecca dool cusca eu cunug ijanaga aqen qa uqa cesuldocnu cinigwe oso qee fel .
Eunu Tibud Anut odocob dana uqa us geh men . Odocob uqa cal mecwe nijen . Ninijen Tibud Anut dana qeih teful oso umei teful onna deweg ganacna haun cufa quton .
Odocob Tibud Anut dana qeih teful euna caja oso mudimei danaca ehudi len .
Odocob dana uqa maden , “ Mele bahic . Uqa teful eu ija tefulininadec . Uqa cuhun eu ija cuhuninadec . Uqa dananadec umei mudon . Eunu ija ijan ‘ Caja dugen , ” en .
Eunu dana uqa anag memegca culaleceb uqa aidegca gabandowasan . Odimesi ale dewenela osol mowasan .
Aria dana aidegca ale bical aleqa qee majanala alel .
Aria man sononec uqa fanindocnu du cuhadon . Uqa dool cunug wooladec Tibud Anut maden . Odocob uqa caja sisildon , “ Anut ale cehelo aig cunug cabina nijia eu cain jowasin ec maalen eu melefo ? ” don .
Odocob caja uqa man sononec jejeg hewi madon , “ Cehelo aig osooso cabina nijeiga eu ele jecnu ihocqa
na gemo taweia eunu Anut uqa ale eundec aig eu cain jowasin o cain qududu fowasin . Eu odifesi ale cal mowasan ec malen , ” don .
Odocob man sononec caja madon , “ Qeeo ! Ale qee cal mowasin !
Ale aig eu jifesi alena cisdoc fogo docob ceteteh meca me qeecanu dowasan . Ale Anut cinigwe calowasan . Eu Anut uqa dona . Eunu uqa odi maalen , ” don .
Eunu caja uqa aig eu feceb galeca bahic ameg qon . Eu jecnu me bahic fen . Uqa doc meca me qeeca ocnu ha gale don . Eunu uqa cehelo eundec aig umei jen . Odimei gemug uqaca tawesin euha uteceb jen .
Odocob ale amala fogo don . Odocob ale bical eu dosin . Eunu ale dan bagac gisimesi taqesin .
Aria wesu maha daec saenna Tibud Anut uqa cabina cocobon ale hutan dosin . Odimesi ale cabina na gemo Tibud Anut amegnu jahundosin .
Euqa Tibud Anut dana utadu madon , “ Hina ai ? ” don .
Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija hina cabina cocobogan hutain dugaqa ija bical . Eunu ija cucuiimig jahuniga , ” don .
Odocob Anut uqa sisildon , “ Hina bical ec eu indec maheia ? Hina cehelo aig ale cain jowasin ec mahem eundec u jagafo ? ” don .
Odocob dana jejeg hewi madon , “ Caja ijaca bilewannu item eu uqa cehelo eundec aig iteceb ija jiga , ” don .
Odocob Tibud Anut caja sisildon , “ Eu celnu odoga ? ” don . Odocob caja jejeg hewi madon , “ Man sononec qauteceb ija jiga , ” don .
Odocob Tibud Anut man sononec madon , “ Hina eu odi odoganu dool cunug mananca cusca gemo hina himec gelihigina . Qila hina wawinna dih sononi cobogan . Hina eu odi mahana cocobi li hinana cal mec deelna calegan .
Ija odocomin hina cajaca qocobqocob owasan . Uqana sihulca hinana sihulca gaid cad biluwasan . Hibna caja uqana mel oso uqa ilom tulohdocob hina uqa jaih bisoc qu jegan , ” don .
Odimei uqa caja madon , “ Ija hina mel basecnu dain hec saen eu ben bahic tubduhigen . Hina ben dain heheb mel basegan qa hina gemunnu gale hec eu odi nijigian . Euqa uqa hinana ilo biligian , ” don .
Odimei uqa dana madon , “ Hina aiden jejeg dah mimeg cehelo aig ija cain jowasin ec mahem eu jaga . Hina eu odi odoganu ija maha geldugina . Hina gagadic odocca dain hecnaca u jegan . Eu odi himec oodi li cal megan .
Husca gagalitca hinana cabina cajoqagan . Odocob hina sab bahudec u jegan .
Hina musul heheb sab u jegan . Oodi li haun maha ibuldogan . Hina mahana mihem . Hina maha eunu haun ceseli maha ibuldogan , ” don .
Aria Adam uqa aideg eu uqa dana cajaca cunug agena anaga calen . Eunu uqa ijan Iw qon .
Odocob Tibud Anut uqa dool ganacna lotoc mudimei Adam aidegca aleceb taqesin .
Odocob Tibud Anut maden , “ Qila dana ege oso cinigwe caleia . Ceteteh meca me qeeca dona . Euqa uqa eben mimei cebac bilec na aigha u jimei cebac bileceb catanecdain . Eunu ege cahacdoc bahic cahacdoqan , ” en .
Eunu Tibud Anut uqa dana caja Iden cabinadec ititacalen . Maha dana muden euna sab cehigiannu eunadec malen .
Ititacali hedocob cali lesin . Odimei Iden cabi cam tobi becna isec uqa han qali dana gagadic , ijan Kerub , ono maden . Odimei sigin aig ja belicanca eu hagen cunugna isec walwaldudu tawena euna muden . Eu cebac bilec catanec uqana jic cahacdoc .
Aria Adam uqa aideg Iwca nijimesi uqa melca men . Odimei Ken basen . Odocob uqa maden , “ Tibud cesulteceb ija mel momodo oso ehudiga , ” en . Eunu uqa ijan Ken qon .
Odocob uqa hibna Ken waliag Ebel basen . Odocob Ebel uqa ben mimei dool cofadec dana calen qa Ken uqa ben mimei cabi ceteteh cehec dana calen .
Aria saen osona Ken uqa cabinadec sab leih cedi ahumei Tibud ihandon .
Ebel uqaha Tibud ihandon qa uqa sipsip nag leih hahawan basadec eundec aqi tuqadimei cuhunuga lalonoga eu cedadi ahon . Odocob Tibud uqa Ebelnuca uqana ihanecnuca waug nijen .
Qa Kennuca uqana ihanecnuca Tibud uqa waug qee nijel . Eunu Ken uqa gemag geh bahic ben . Odocob ola gulu qon .
Odocob Tibud uqa Ken madon , “ Celnu hina gemain bena ? Celnu hina olain gulu qona ?
Hina odi cuhadoummi ija wawi hinanu nijoub . Qa hina qee odi cuhadocomfi silail hinana cebecna hagawihecnu saciadoia taweia . Uqa hinanu nalunin meia taweia . Qa hina gagadic mimeg wooldoga , ” don .
Aria Ken waliag Ebel madon , “ Gec beli bahu cobewa , ” don . Odocob belesin . Cocobi bilesi Ken uqa cajimei waliag Ebel qagadocob cal men .
Aria Tibud uqa Ken sisildon , “ Hina walin Ebel ai ? ” don . Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija qee dugina . Ija wali cofdoc danafo ? ” don .
Odocob Tibud madon , “ Hina eeta odoga ? Hina walin golac mahana basedoia eu dana jejeg cinigwe utai mateia ija dah miga .
Qila ija hina gelihigina . Hina walin qagadocom cal meceb uqa golac mahana basedoia . Odimei golac maha dunuh noia eu maha cocawe mimei sugudoia . Eunu maha i hina ceteh cehecnu ihoc qee . Eunu ija hina maha inadec ititachigina .
Saen hina maha ina sab cehegaqa hina sab me qee cajiheian . Hina jehen osoca qee . Hina odi mahamaha loldudu cobogan , ” don .
Odocob Ken uqa Tibud madon , “ Ijana me qee odoc ameg eu ben bahic . Ija gahidocwe qee .
Faga ! Hina qila deel ina maha inadec ititactagana . Odocom ija hina amennu bisachi nuigen . Ija jehenca qee mahamaha loldudu cobigen . Odi cocobomin in oso guluctigiaqa qagateceb cal migen , ” don .
Qa Tibud jejeg hewi madon , “ Eu odi qee . Dana oso Ken qagadocob cal migiaqa ija dana eu ameg culumen eben naha gic lecisca wadacdugen , ” don . Odocob Tibud uqa Kennu gaga oso men . Eunu dana oso Ken gulucdugiaqa uqa gaga eu fimei uqa qee qagadoiaun .
Odocob Ken uqa Tibud amegnu bisacdumei caji nuen . Odimei uqa Iden cam tobi becna isec nuimei hatu ono bilen . Hatu eu ijan “ Loldudu Coboc ” .
Aria Ken aidegca nijimesi uqa melca men . Odimei Inok basen . Saen euna Ken uqa taun ben oso cecehi bilei uqa melah ijan Inok eu taun eu ijan qon .
Aria Inok ben mimei caja oso ocob mel basen . Eu uqa ijan Irad qon . Odocob Irad uqa caja oso ocob mel basen . Eu uqa ijan Mehusel qon . Odocob Mehusel ben mimei caja oso ocob mel basen . Eu uqa ijan Metusel qon . Odocob Metusel ben mimei caja oso ocob mel basen . Eu ijan Lamek qon .
Odocob Lamek ben mimei caja lecis cedalen . Oso ijan Eda . Oso ijan Sila .
Odocob Eda uqa Jabal basen . Jabal uqa dana dool manan cofaadi bileig lotoc talahna himec nijegina eu agena asaga calen .
Jabal uqa waliagca , eu ijan Jubal . Uqa dana sihul gita qoginaca cololo fuldoginaca eu agena asaga calen .
Odocob Sila uqaha mel oso basen . Uqa ijan eu Tubal-ken . Tubal-ken uqa bras ainca na cabi teful aigcaca mudec dana calen . Tubal-ken uqa cebinagca , eu ijan Nama .
Odocob Lamek aidegul maalen , “ Eda Silaca ale ija jejeni dah mesia . Ale ijana caja ijana je dah mi cuhadosia . Dana oso uqa ija qiteceb golani necebfi ija qocomin cal migian . Mel oso uqa ija qitecebfi ija qocomin cal migian .
Dana oso Ken qagadocob cal mecebfi wadacdoc ameg eu ben ugian . Qa dana oso ija qagatifei uqa wadacdoc ameg eu culumenca bahic ugian , ” alen .
Odocob Adam haun aidegca nijimesi uqa mel oso basen . Odimei uqa maden , “ Ken uqa Ebel qagadocob cal men . Eunu Anut uqa mel oso haun itia . Eu Ebel hehuldocnu itia , ” en . Eunu ijan Set qon .
Odocob Set uqa caja oso ocob mel basen . Eu uqa ijan Inos qon . Saen euna dana age Tibud ijanna inondudu ihanec sanan mein .
Je jaqoc ina Adamna sihul ijanaga nijia . Anut uqa dana ifanen saen euna uqa dana Anut cinigwe muden .
Uqa manahalca aidca ifanalen . Ifanaalen uqa eelalimei ijanala “ Dana Cajaca ” aqalen .
Saen Adam uqana cabi gel 130 eu odi bibili bilei uqa aideg mel oso basen . Mel eu uqa cinigwe uqa hahun umei cali hon . Odocob uqa ijan Set qon .
Aria Set cali hocob Adam uqa bileceb li uqana cabi gel 800 eu odi calen . Oodon Adam aideg uqa melahul ategulca haun basaden .
Eunu Adam uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 930 . Odocob uqa cal men .
Aria Set uqa bibilen li uqana cabi gel eu 105 eu odi caleceb uqa aideg mel oso basen . Odocob ijan Enos qon .
Odimei Set uqa bibilen li cabi gel 807 on . Oodon uqa aideg melahul ategulca haun basaden .
Eunu Set uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 912 . Odocob uqa cal men .
Aria Enos uqa bibilen li uqana cabi gel 90 ocob uqa aideg mel oso basen . Odocob ijan Kenan qon .
Odimei Enos bibilen li cabi gel 815 on . Oodon uqa aideg melahul ategulca haun basaden .
Eunu Enos uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 905 . Odocob uqa cal men .
Aria Kenan uqa bibilen li uqana cabi gel 70 ocob uqa aideg mel oso basen . Odocob ijan Mahalalel qon .
Odimei Kenan bibilen li cabi gel 840 on . Oodon uqa aideg melahul ategulca haun basaden .
Eunu Kenan uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 910 . Odocob uqa cal men .
Aria Mahalalel uqa bibilen li uqana cabi gel 65 ocob uqa aideg mel oso basen . Odocob ijan Jared qon .
Odimei Mahalalel bibilen li cabi gel 830 on . Oodon uqa aideg melahul ategulca haun basaden .
Eunu Mahalalel uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 895 . Odocob uqa cal men .
Aria Jared uqa bibilen li cabi gel 162 ocob uqa aideg mel oso basen . Odocob ijan Inok qon .
Odimei Jared bibilen li cabi gel 800 on . Oodon uqa aideg melahul ategulca haun basaden .
Eunu Jared uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 962 . Odocob uqa cal men .
Aria Inok uqa bibilen li cabi gel 65 ocob uqa aideg mel oso basen . Odocob ijan Metusela qon .
Odimei Inok uqa cabi gel 300 eu odi Anutca cobosin . Oodon uqa aideg melahul ategulca haun basaden .
Eunu Inok uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 365 .
Aria Inok mahana bibili uqa Anutca cobosin . Oodon Anut uqa ehuden . Eunu uqa jajanu qelen .
Aria Metusela uqa bibilen li cabi gel 187 ocob uqa aideg mel oso basen . Odocob ijan Lamek qon .
Odimei Metusela bibilen li cabi gel 782 on . Oodon uqa aideg melahul ategulca haun basaden .
Eunu Metusela uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 969 . Odocob uqa cal men .
Aria Lamek uqa bibilen li cabi gel 182 ocob uqa aideg mel oso basen .
Odocob uqa maden , “ Maha i Anut wele geuldon eunadec mel i ege cehi jecnu cabi culumenca oqonanu mel i uqa cesulgigian , ” en . Eunu mel eu ijan Noa qon .
Odimei Lamek bibilen li cabi gel 595 on . Oodon uqa aideg melahul ategulca haun basaden .
Eunu Lamek uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 777 . Odocob uqa cal men .
Aria Noa uqana cabi gel 500 hedocob uqa melahul ijedca bilen . Age ijanaga eu Semca Hamca Jafetca .
Aria saen euna dana sihul mahana geh bahic fulusdumeig mel aid basadein .
Mel aid eu age galeca bahic . Eunu Anutna sao mel age dana atagail feciadecebil amaga qon . Odocob age aidagailnu agena gawecnana cedadein .
Odocob Tibud uqa maden , “ Dana cajaca age qee bilecebil cataneiaun . Eunu ijana Kis eu dana cajaca ageca qee bileceb cataneiaun . Qila ija odadecemin age cabi gel 120 himec biluqagan , ” en .
Saen euna hibnaha dana citoec mahana bilein . Aria Anutna sao mel age dana atagail gami ocobocob imeig mel basadein . Mel eu age dana citoec age hannu gelehinigaca calein . Dana eu age age dana weledec age ijanagaca .
Aria Tibud uqa dana cajaca mahanadec agena qisol mec eu ben bahic fen . Agena cisdoc me qeeca golanaga me qeenu sililecca odi nijen .
Uqa dana cajaca ifanadimei mahana mudennu waloc don . Uqa waug ben qon .
Odocob Tibud uqa maden , “ Ija dana sihul cunug ifanadem eu qee madigen . Mahana doolca man fululecca ceteteh cunug mahana cobogina eu qee madigen . Ija ifanademnu waloc tena , ” en .
Qa Tibud uqa Noana odoc fimei Noanu waug tawen .
I Noanu je . Noa uqa dana ititom . Uqa Anut amegna cahuldocca qee . Uqa Anutca cobosin .
Noa uqa melahul ijedca . Age ijanaga eu Semca Hamca Jafetca .
Qa saen euna dana cajaca cunug age Anut amegna qisol mec me qee bahicca . Age cunug han me qee cadein .
Anut uqa dana cajaca mahana cunug bilein age qisol mein eu fen .
Odocob Anut uqa Noa madon , “ Dana cunug agena qisol mec eu maha cunug ihoc len . Eunu ija age cunug qee madigen . Mele bahic ija maha cunug fadaldugen .
Wag ben oso wamena hinadodocnu himec jelega . Wag eu hamol mati bahicca muduga . Odimeg baial dunuhca maha gumuca joudoga .
Hina odi jelegan . Wag eu uqana cecelac eu 133 mita . Uqana bagalan eu 22 mita . Uqana ohis tec eu 13 mita .
Hina jo qab naca qeih naca gemo fufu cebecha qahegan . Fufu cebec uqana ohis tec eu mita naha himec . Odimeg cebec eu wag qeihna qahegan . Wag eu uqana bahim ijed dunuh bacatca mudegan .
Faga ! Ija wa sil mahana suldugen . Ceteteh cunug mahana coboginaca sao bisalunaca cunug fadaladigen . Ceteteh mahana cebac bilegina age cunug cal moqagan .
Qa ija hinaca bal cehec je madewan . Odocob hina wag tobegan . Hinaca hina melemenelca hina aidenca hina melemenel aidagailca toboqagan .
Ceteteh cunug mahana cobogina eundec dool filfil man fululec filfil manahalca cufunecca ehadi ehi li wagna madegan . Odocob age qee cal mowain .

Odocob hina sab gug filfil hinanuca agenuca cedi ehi li megan , ” don .
Aria Noa uqa Anut madon eu cunug toodu odon .
Odocob Tibud uqa Noa madon , “ Saen ina hina himec ija amina dana ititom . Eunu hinaca hinana talaunelca wag dunuh leiga .
Hina dool qagoc eundec gug filfil manahal eben naha gic lecisca cufunec eben naha gic lecisca odi cedadaga . Odimeg hina dool qee qagoc eundec manahal osahic cufunec osahic odi cedadaga .
Odocob man fululec sao bisaludecha manahal eben naha gic lecisca cufunec eben naha gic lecisca odi cedadaga . Eu age hibna haun mahana fulusdoqagan .
Deel eben naha gic lecisca hedocob ija wa ben saonadec suldugen . Odocob wa eu cahineg 40 witic 40 odi hugian . Saen euna ija ceteteh cunug maha ina ifanadem eu fadaladigen , ” don .
Odocob Noa uqa Tibud madon eu cunug toodu odon .
Aria Noa uqana cabi gel eu 600 . Saen euna wa sil cajimei maha cunug ihoc len .
Oodon Noa uqa wa sil cajigiannu uqa melahul gami uqa aidegca uqa melahul aidagail gami age wag dunuh lein .
Dool qagocca qee qagocca manca ceteteh cunug mahana cobogina euha dunuh lein .
Euqa manahalca cufunecca Noa gami wag dunuh lein . Age Anut Noa madon eu odi toodu lein .
Odocob deel eben naha gic lecisca hedocob wa sil mahana cajen .
Saen euna Noa uqana cabi gel eu 600 . Wa sil cajen eu deel 17 jagel lecis docna wa ameg cehec maha dunuhdec eu uqana cebec qajawen . Odocob saonadec cebec cunug hudeceb wa ben nen .
Odocob wa eu cahineg 40 witic 40 odi mahana nen .
Deel euna dih Noaca uqa melahul Sem , Ham , Jafetca ageca uqa aidegca uqa melahul aidagailca age cunug wag dunuh lein .
Dool mananca cusca eundec sihul filfil ceteteh cunug mahana cobogina eundec sihul filfil man fululecca ceteteh cunug hojonogaca sihul filfil eundec age cunug Noa gami wag dunuh lein .
Age cunug Noa gami lein . Dool cunug cebac cobogina age lecislecis wag dunuh lein .
Dool lein eu manahalca cufunecca odi lein . Age cunug Anut maden odi toodumeig wag dunuh lein . Odocob Anut hibilimega jic cebec menen .
Aria mahana wa sil tubca cacaji ninijen deel 40 leceb wag u suldocob basai cobon .
Odocob wa ben bahic cajimei mahana wa gudoc calen . Odimei wag u suldocob wa lal cobon .
Wa mahana ben bahic ihoc timei aluh benben sao bisalu eu cunug jahuladen .
Odimei wa 7 mita ohis aluh cunug u jebucaden .
Odocob ceteteh cunug mahana cobogina age cal mein . Man fululec cunug dool mananca dool cusca cunug mamanig cunug mahana cobogina euca dana cunugca cal mein .
Ceteteh cunug mahana cocobi medemegana siwogina eu cunug cal mein .
Ceteteh cunug mahana cebac cobogina danaca doolca mamanigca man fululec saonadecca eu cunug Anut uqa mahanadec qee maden . Odocob Noa uqaca uqana sihulca age himec wagna bilein .
Odocob deel 150 odi wa sil mahana caji nijen .
Qa Anut uqa Noaca dool cusca dool mananca wagna bileinnu dahig qee celel . Eunu uqa odocob fufu oso mahana hon . Odocob wa sil seleldon .
Odocob wa ben cehec maha dunuhnadecca saonadecca eu calena cebec eu cufa qon . Odocob wa sao ohisdec nen eu gatidon .
Wa mahana nijen eu cebitnana seleldon . Odocob deel 150 hedocob wa toni non .
Deel 17na jagel eben naha gic lecisca docna wag eu Ararat aluh osona toni bilen .
Odocob wa haun cebitnana seleldodon li jagel eben nahanahaca on . Odocob jagel eu uqana deel sanan mecna aluh agena igoc camasac mein .
Odocob deel 40 hedocob Noa fufu cebec uqa muden eu huden .
Odimei uqa alog oso u suldocob nuen . Nuimei qa qee ceseli hol . Uqa fululi cocobon li wa mahana cunug sidon .
Oodonqa Noa uqa cuhudid oso umei suldocob nuen . Uqa wa mahana seleldonfo qeefo eu dugiannu suldon .
Qa wa maha cunugna nijen . Eunu cuhudid eu cudun oso hewi bibili jaen mudecnu qee fimei uqa haun wagna ceseli hon . Odocob Noa eben maha gumu leceb uqana cuhudid u wag dunuh ehi li muden .
Odocob Noa uqa deel eben naha gic lecisca haun wa seleldugiannu sumuden . Odocob uqa cuhudid wagnadec haun u suldon .
Wesu memen cuhudid eu ceseli uqaca hon . Uqa cona na oso , ijan oliw , eu bagac cebac u qada qu ahon . Odocob Noa uqa wa wele hidon eu don .
Odocob Noa uqa deel eben naha gic lecisca hedocob uqa cuhudid haun suldon qa cuhudid eu uqaca qee ceseli hol .
Saen Noa uqana cabi gel 601na jagel sanan mec eu uqana deel sanan mecna wa mahana cunug hidu qee men . Odocob Noa uqa wag ohis jahuldoc eu qosocdon . Noa meciimei maha tatacdec eu galalec ninijen fen .
Saen deel 27na jagel lecis docna maha galal bahic en .
Odocob Anut Noa madon ,
“ Wag culimeig caleiga . Hinaca hina melemenelca hina aidenca hina melemenel aidagailca caleiga .
Ceteteh cunug mahana cebac coboginaca man fululecca doolca mamanig cunug mahana coboginaca age agena sihul eu mahana geh bahic fulusdoqagannu cedadecem hina gami maha gumu caleiga . Odimeig maha cunug ihoc loqagan , ” don .
Eunu Noa uqa maha gumu calen . Uqaca uqa melahulca uqa aidegca uqa melahul aidagailca age maha gumu calein .
Dool cunug mamanig cunug man fululec cunug ceteteh cunug mahana cobogina eu cunug agena sihulnana qagocqagoc wag dunuhdec calein .
Odocob Noa uqa Tibud ihandugia bili meenna ihanec cabal oso gualen . Odimei uqa dool qagoc eundecca man fululec qagoc eundecca osahicosahic cedadimei ihanec cabal euna Tibud ihandudu bili manen .
Odocob Tibud uqa dedeman eu tinca don . Eunu uqadodoc waugna maden , “ Dana age melnadec agena qisol cisdoc eu gaid odi nijina . Eunu hibna ija dananu maha haun qee geldugaun . Ceteteh cunug mahana cobogina eu qila fadaladiga odiwe haun qee fadaladigaun .
Mahana saen eu odi nijigian cehec saenca sab oc saenca duan saenca cam saenca san saenca wa saenca cahinegca witicca eu cunug qee qee meiaun , ” en .
Odocob Anut uqa Noaca uqa melahulca eelaadi bili maaden , “ Age aig qumeig fulusdoigale . Odimeig maha cunug ihoc leigale .
Dool cunug saonadec man fululec cunug wanadec dool cunug mamanig cunug mahana cobogina eu age cunug agenu cucuii teleloqagan . Ceteteh eu age cunug age ebenegana migina .
Weleca ija celum himec jecnu adem . Qila ceteteh cunug mahana cebac cobogina euha agena sabnu adigina .
Euqa golac eu cebac silig . Eunu age dool golacca cain jowain .
Dana oso uqa oso qagadocob golac toni basecdocob cal mecebfi ija dana eu wadacdoc utigen . Dool oso uqa dana oso qocob cal mecebfi ija uqa wadacdu qocomin cal migian .
Ija ihoconi qumig dana ifanem . Eunu in oso dana oso qocob cal mecebfi uqadodocha dana age qocobil cal migian .
Qa agenu eu odi age aig qumeig mati bahic caleigale . Age fulusdu mati bahic calimeig maha cunug ihoc leigale , ” aden .
Odocob Anut uqa Noaca uqa melahulca ha maaden ,
“ Aria feiga ! Ija qila ageca agena sihul hibna cali hoqagan eucanu bal cehec je madigina .
Euha man fululecca dool mananca dool cusca ceteteh cunug wagnadec cali hoiga euca ceteteh cunug mahana cebac cobogina eu ageca wagna bileiga eu agenu ha bal cehec je madigina .
Ija bal cehec je i edi madigina , ‘ Ija ceteteh cunug mahana cebac cobogina eu wa sil haun qee fadaladigaun . Wa sil oso maha i haun qee bahic fadaldoiaun , ’ igina .
Bal cehec je i ijaca ageca ceteteh cunug mahana cebac cobogina euca gemo biligiannu migina . Bal cehec je i bileceb catanigian . Eu uqana gadac eu i hen .
Ija taenna wal cehegina . Euqa bal cehec je ija mahaca gemo biligiannu migina eu uqana gadac .
Ija taenna maha jahuldocomin wal saona caligian saen euna
ija wa sil oso ceteteh cunug mahana cebac cobogina eu haun qee fadaladeiaun ec ageca dool cunugca maadiga eu cisdugen .
Saen wal taenna caligian fimig ija bal cehec je ijaca ceteteh cunug mahana cebac cobogina euca gemo bileceb catanigian eunu cisdugen .
Bal cehec je ijaca ceteteh cunug mahana cebac cobogina euca gemo biligiannu uqana gadac eu hen , ” aden .
Aria Noa uqa melahulca wagnadec cali hoin eu age ijanaga eu Sem , Ham , Jafetca . Ham uqa Kenan memeg .
Mel ijed eu age Noa melahul . Odocob dana eu agenadec dana cajaca cunug sabijimeig fulusdocobil maha cunug ihoc len .
Aria Noa uqa jehen cabi oc dana . Eunu uqa wain halu cabina cehimei aig cedimei wain wa muden .
Saen osona wain wa muden eundec naha jimei dalul qon . Odocob uqa uqana lotoc tacec hulimei bical uqana lotoc talahna nijen .
Ham , uqa Kenan memeg , uqa memeg Noa bical ninijen fimei maha gumu cali limei waliagul lecis maalen .
Qa Sem Jafetca ale lotoc oso umesi qatomolana huleldu hewimesi bicbic limesi memela jahuldosin . Ale memela bical nijen eunu qee felesin . Ale amala abes nuen .
Odocob hibna Noa uqa wain jen eu dalul qoc hedocob uqa melah subig odudon eu wele don .
Odocob uqa madon , “ Hina melem , Kenan , geldugina . Uqa waliagul agena cabi dana biligian .
Tibud Uqa Semna Anut . Eunu binan waseiale . Kenan uqa Semna cabi dana biliale .
Anut uqa Jafetna sihul hatu ben utiale . Age Sem asagaca bileigale . Kenan uqa Jafetna cabi dana biliale , ” don .
Aria wa sil hedon eu Noa uqa cabi gel 350 odi bilen .
Eunu Noa uqa mahana bilen eu cabi gel 950 eu hedocob uqa cal men .
Aria Noa melahul Sem , Ham , Jafetca agena sihul je i edi . Wa sil cajen eu hedocob melamagail eu age aidagail mel haun basadein .
Jafet melahul eu Gome , Megog , Madai , Jawan , Tubal , Mesek , Tirasca .
Gome melahul eu Asigenas , Rifat , Togamaca .
Jawan melahul eu Elisa Tasisca . Dana sihul i age Kit Dodanica ageha Jawannadec .
Sihul eunadec dana age bilisadumeig age lannaca nuinaca belein . Age bilisadumeig agena jobon medeh filfilnana hatu filfilnana je filfilnana qaguqagu belein .
Ham melahul eu Kus , Isip , Put , Kenanca .
Kus melahul eu Seba , Hawila , Sabta , Rama , Sabtegaca . Rama melahul eu Siba Dedanca .
Aria Kus uqa melah oso ijan eu Nimrod . Nimrod mahana han cadecnu gelehinca calen .
Uqa Tibud amegna dool qocnu ijanca calen . Eunu je oso odi madegina , “ Nimrod cinigwe dool qoc dana ijanca Tibud amegna , ” egina .
Hahawan bahic uqa taun benben hewaden eu Sina mahana taun eu Bebel , Erek , Akadca .
Maha eunadec uqa cajimei Asiria nuen . Odimei uqa ono Niniwa , Rehobot-ia , Kala ,
Resenca cehaden . Resen eu Niniwa Kalaca gemo bilen . Kala eu taun ben bahic .
Isip uqa dana sihul Lud , Anam , Lehab , Naftu ,
Patrus , Kaslu , Kaptoca asaga calen . Filistia age Kaptona sihulnadec calein .

Hiwi , Aki , Sini ,
Awad , Sema , Hamatca . Agena sihul age asagail calein . Hibna Kenan uqana sihul age jobon medeh filfilnadec age bilisadumeig belein .
Odocob Kenan agena maha gadac eu Saidondec sanan mimei nui Gasa gadac eu Gera isec euha Sodom , Gomora , Atma , Seboimca leceb Lasa gadac .
Aria eu age Ham melahul . Age agena sihulnana agena jenana agena mahanana agena hatunana odi qaguqagu bilein .
Sem ha melahulca . Uqa waliag matu eu Jafet . Hibru dana cunug age asaga eu Sem .
Sem melahul eu Ilam , Asur , Apaksad , Lud , Aramca .
Aram melahul eu Us , Hul , Geta , Masca .
Sela memeg eu Apaksad . Ebe memeg eu Sela .
Ebe uqa melahul lecisca . Oso ijan eu Peleg . Uqana saenna maha gadac qatani mati bahic calen . Eunu ijan odi qon . Uqa waliag ijan eu Joktan .
Joktan melahul eu Almodad , Seleb , Hasamawet , Jera ,
Hadoram , Usal , Dikla ,
Obal , Abimel , Siba ,
Ofia , Hawila , Jobabca . Dan eu age eu Joktan melahul .
Maha age bilein eu Mesa sanan mimei leceb Sefa gadac . Eu hatu aluh mati bahic cam tobi becna isec .
Aria dana eu age eu Semna sihul . Age agena sihulnana agena jenana agena mahanana agena hatunana odi qaguqagu bilein .
Aria eu age eu Noana sihul . Agena jobon medeh filfil . Age agena sihulnana agena hatunana odi qaguqagu bilein . Wa sil hedocob Noana sihulnadec dana cajaca mahana cunug bilegina eu calein .
Aria weleca Nimrod bilen saenna mahamaha cunug agena je madec eu osol himec . Eu filfil qee .
Dana cajaca eu age bili u cocobi bileig cam tobi becna isec belein . Bebeleig maha asou osona calein . Eu Sina agena hatu . Odimeig age ono bilein .
Odocob age madocobmadocob imeig madein , “ Gec , maha agam cedimeb jana manocomun gagadic mimei brik caligian , ” ein . Age simen baial mimeig brik fagdudufagdudu nuein .
Odocob age madein , “ Gec hoiga . Ege egena taun ben oso cehecnu . Ege jo oso ohis bahic cehecnu . Uqana qab eu sao qududugian . Eufi ege qatani filigandumeb mahamaha cunug qee ihoc loqaun qa ege ijanigeca bilecnu , ” ein .
Odocob Tibud uqa dana eu age taun ben jo ohis bahic cecehegin tena eu figia bili nen .
Odimei uqa maden , “ Feiga ! Dana i age age sihul osol . Age cunug je osolca . Age cabi i odoqagannu sanan mi odogina eu odoqagan . Age qila cel oso odoqagannu nalug mifeig age odocobil ihoc himec ligian .
Age odi odowainnu ege ono numeb agena je ihulduadecnu . Eufi age agena je madec eu docobdocob qee owain , ” en .
Eunu Tibud uqa filiganadeceb age onodec bilisadumeig mahamaha cunug ihoc lein . Odimeig age taun ben eu cehec culein .
Odocob ono Tibud uqa mahamaha cunug agena je qu ihulahalduadimei filiganadeceb age bilisadumeig mahamaha cunug ihoc lein . Eunu jobon eu ijan Bebel doin .
Semna sihul agena je eu odi . Aria wa sil hedocob cabi gel lecis nueceb Sem uqana cabi gel eu 100 eu odi ihoc leceb uqa aideg mel oso basen . Uqa ijan Apaksad qon .
Odimei Sem bibilen li haun cabi gel 500 bilen . Oodon Sem aideg melahul ategulca haun basaden .

Odimei Ebe bibilen li haun cabi gel 430 bilen . Oodon Ebe aideg melahul ategulca haun basaden .

Aria Neho uqa bibilen li uqana cabi gel eu 29 eu odi ihoc leceb uqa aideg mel oso basen . Uqa ijan Tira qon .

Aria Tira uqa bibilen li uqana cabi gel eu 70 eu odi ihoc leceb uqa melahul ijedca . Ijanaga eu Ebram , Neho , Haranca .
Aria Tirana sihul agena je eu odi . Tira uqa melahul ijedca . Eu Ebram , Neho , Haranca . Haran uqa Lot memeg .
Aria Tira cebac bibilen Haran uqa cal men . Uqa anag basen maha euna cal men . Eu ijan Ur .
Aria Ebram Nehoca ale caja cedesin . Ebram aideg ijan eu Sarai . Neho aideg ijan eu Milka . Milka uqa Haran ateg . Iska uqaha Haran ateg .
Odonqa Sarai uqa goud . Uqa melca qee .
Odocob Tira uqa melah Ebramca Haran melah uqa asag Lotca Ebram aideg Saraica ehadeceb age Kaldia hatu ijan Ur eu culimeig Kenan hatuna beloqagannu belein . Belimeig li age Haran hatuna calein . Odimeig age ono bilein .
Odocob Tira uqa Haran ono cal men . Uqana cabi gel cunug eu 205 odi .
Aria Tibud uqa Ebram madon . “ Hina memenca hinana sihulca hinana hatuca culimeg hatu ija ihachigen euna nuuga .
Odocom ija odocomin hinana sihul eu mati bahic caloqagan . Ija eelhigen . Ija binainca mihigen . Odocob hina binainnu mati bahic age eeldoc oqagan .
Dana hina eelhigian eu ija eeldugen . Qa in oso hina gelihigian eu ija geldugen . Hinanu himec mahamaha sihul cunug age eeldoc oqagan , ” don .
Ebram uqa Anutna je dah men saen euna uqana cabi gel eu 75 . Aria Ebram uqa Anutna je toodumei uqa aideg Saraica uqa waliag melah Lotca uqana cabi dana Haran ono cedaden euca uqana ceteteh cunug ono ceden euca cunug cedimei Haran hatunadec culimei Kenan hatuna nuen . Uqa jicna niji u nui Kenan hatuna calen .

Odocob Ebram uqa Kenan hatuna calimei cocobi bili u nui maha oso ijan Sekem ono calimei More uqana na ben gun oso gugna calen . Aria saen euna Kenan dana age maha euna bibilegin uqa ono calen .
Odocob Tibud uqa ono Ebram amegna camasac mimei madon , “ Maha i hinana sihul adigen , ” don . Odocob uqa ono Tibud camasac menna uqa Tibud ihandocnu meen cabal oso gualen .
Odimei uqa onodec haun cajimei cam tobi becna isec aluh oso Betel cemenug nijia euna nuen . Uqa cudun euna uqa lotoc talah cehen . Betel eu cam toni nocna isec ninijen Ai eu cam tobi becna isec nijia . Uqa gemo euna Tibud ihandocnu meen cabal oso gualen . Odimei uqa Tibud ijan u bili ihandon .
Uqa onodec haun cajimei cocobi bili nui Negew isec nuen .
Aria saen euna maha euna cahel saen ben calen . Eunu Ebram uqa Isip biligiannu onoca nuen .
Nuimei Ebram uqa Isip calecnu dodoldudu bili uqa aideg Sarai madon , “ Faga ! Hina caja jaca eu ija dugina .
Saen Isip dana age hina mecihimeig age i uqa aideg ec cisdoqagan . Odimeig age ija qagatimeig hina oihuqagan .
Eunu hina uqa ija cebinami ec odi maadagale . Hina eu odi maadecemfi ija culitimeig me eeltoqagan , ” don .
Odocob Ebram Isip ono caleceb Isip dana age aideg mele uqa caja jaca bahic eu fein .
Odocobil Fero uqana cabinu ilo dana age caja eu fimeig Fero caja eu galeca bahic madocnu lein . Eunu caja eu ehudi Ferona jona lein .
Fero uqa Sarainu dumei uqa Ebram eeldu cuhadon . Odimei uqa sipsipca memeca bulmakauca cesel manahal cufunecca cabi dana cajaca kamelca cedadi Ebram uton .
Oodonqa Fero uqa Sarai on eunu Tibud uqa hag me qee me qee suldon . Odocob Feroca dana caja cunug uqana jona bilegina euca age hag me qee eu hewaden .
Odocob Fero Ebram utadocob hocob madon , “ Celnu kobol i oditem ? Celnu hina uqa hina aiden ec qee matelem ?
Celnu hina uqa ija cebinami ec matem ? Ija uqa aideninu imig om eu celnu qee cahactelem ? Aria hina aiden i hen . Umeg nuuga , ” don .
Odimei uqana dana maadeceb age Ebramca uqa aidegca uqana ceteteh cunugca odi ehadi ehi nui maha gadacna culadein .
Aria ono Ebram uqa cehewan ben bahicca . Uqa sipsipca memeca bulmakauca golca silwaca . Odocob Ebram uqa aidegca Lotca uqana ceteteh cunugca cedimeig Isip culimeig Negew tein .

Onodec uqa Negew culimei cocobicocobi nui Betel ono calen . Maha euna uqa hahawan lotoc talah cehennu euqa Betel Aica gemo .
Cocobi li uqa hahawan ihanec meen cehenna ono calen . Odimei cudun euna uqa Tibud ijan u binan sulen .
Aria Lot uqa Ebramca belesin . Uqaha sipsipca memeca bulmakauca uqana cabi danaca .
Qa ale alena ceteteh eu mati bahic eunu maha eu ale osoben gabandu bilecnu ihoc qee .
Eunu Ebramna dool cofadec danaca Lotna dool cofadec danaca gemo fee dadanec calen . Aria saen euna Kenan danaca Peres danaca age maha euna bilein .
Odocob Ebram Lot madon , “ Odi cain . Ele cotigcotig . Eunu ele fee dadan ecebeceb qee owaun o ijana dool cofadec danaca hinana dool cofadec danaca ageha qee fee dadanowain .
Maha cunug eu me himec nijia fagana . Eunu cois ele filigandowan . Ansecna isec nuecemfi ija meulana isec nuigen . Qa hina meulana isec nuecemfi ija ansena isec nuigen , ” don .
Odocob Lot ameg suli umei Jodan maha asou leceb Soa maha eu cunug fen . Maha eu cunug wa uti cuhadoc nijen . Maha eu Tibudna cabi cinigwe eu Isip agena maha cinigwe . Saen euna Tibud uqa Sodom Gomoraca qee fadalalec ninijen . Eu ale ihoc nijesin .
Eunu Lot uqa uqadodocnu Jodan maha asou cunug nesilen . Odocob uqa cam tobi becna isec nuen . Ale eu odi filigandosin .
Ebram uqa Kenan mahana bilen . Oodon Lot uqa jobon benben maha asou euna nijegina ono age gemo nui bilen . Odocob uqa li Sodom cemenug uqana lotoc talah cehen .
Aria Sodom dana age qisol jaumadec . Age Tibud amegna silail dana bahic .
Saen Lot Ebram culdi nueceb Tibud uqa Ebram madon , “ Amen suli umeg cudun hina tawaganadec hagen cunugna isec meciecem nuia .
Ija hinaca hinana sihulca maha cunug fagana eu adigen . Agena gaid biligiannu adigen .
Odocob ija odocomin hinana sihul eu bobos cinigwe fulusdugian . Eunu in oso bobos saniecnu ihocfi hinana sihulha saniecnu ihoc .
Cajaga . Maha i ija hina ihigen eu cocobi nui cunug faga , ” don .
Eunu Ebram uqana lotoc talah wagalimei cocobi nui Mamri uqana na benben gugna calen . Ono Hebron cemenugca bilen . Odimei uqa ono ihanecnu meen cabal gualen .
Aria saen euna dana ben oso bilen uqa ijan Kedoleoma . Uqa Ilam agena king . Wele Kedoleoma uqa king ebum oso cadadimei ilo bilen . King ebum oso i age eu odi . Sodom agena king Beraca Gomora agena king Birsaca Adma agena king Sinabca Seboim agena king Semebaca Bela agena kingca . Kedoleoma uqa cabi gel 12 eu odi king ebum oso agena ilo bilen . Odocob cabi gel 13 docna king eu age Kedoleoma feedoin . Odocob cabi gel 14 docna Kedoleoma uqana danah king ijedca gami gabandoin . King ijed i age eu odi . Sina agena king Amrafelca Elasa agena king Ariokca Goim agena king Tidalca . Kedoleoma king ijedca agena han dana cedadimeig jicna bebeli bileig Refaim dana age Asterot-kanaim ono bibilegin aqadein . Odimeig age Susim dana Ham onoha aqadein . Odimeig Emim dana Kiriataim onoha aqadein . Odimeig Ho dana age Sia agena hatu aluhca jabadi ehi nui El-paran gadac ono aqadein . El-paran eu wadau naca qee cemenug nijia . Odimeig age haun ceselein . Ceseli humeig En-misbat ono calein . En-misbat eu Kades . Odimeig ono han cadimeig Amalek agena hatu eu cunug oin . Odimeig Amo age Hasason-tema ono bilein euha aqimeig hatu eu oin . Aria Sodom agena kingca Gomora agena kingca Adma agena kingca Seboim agena kingca Bela eu Soa agena kingca age wele gabandoin . Age Kedoleomaca uqana han danaca aqadecnu sacia dumeig gabandu Sidim maha asouna ono cali hoin . Sidim eu wa macasca bahic cudun .







Age Ilam agena king wal oso i age han cadoqagannu cajein . Ilam agena king eu Ilam agena king bahic Kedoleomaca Goim agena king Tidalca Sina agena king Amrafelca Elasa agena king Ariokca . Eu king wal oso age king ebum oso gami han cadoqagannu cajein .
Aria Sidim asou eu maha baial . Helo mati bahic euna gag bibi nijen . Odocob Sodom Gomoraca alena king hannu bubusali bilesi helo euna nosin . King ijed ale culadesin euha busalein qa age aluhna belein .
Odocobil king wal oso age Sodom Gomoraca agena ceteteh cunugca agena sab cunugca cedimeig belein .
Ebram melah Lot uqa Sodom ono bilen uqaha ehudimeig uqana ceteteh cunug cedimeig belein .
Aria Ebram uqa Mamri Amodec uqana na benben gugna bilen . Mamrica uqa waliagul Eskol Aneca age Ebramna danah . Odimei Ebram bibilen dana oso hannadec busali humei Hibrudec Ebram madocob don .
Odimei uqa uqana sihul eundec u hewi nueiga ec dah mimei uqa uqana cabi dana 318 eu hannu wele iwaladec eu age uqana jobon bilein cedadeceb age tooadi beli Dan ono calein .
Uqa witic euna uqana dana qataneceb uqa uqana cabi danaca age aqimeig jabadi ehi nui Hoba ono calein . Eu Damaskas taun hagen ono isec .
Odimei Ebram uqa melah Lotca uqana cajaca uqana ceteteh cunugca dana cajaca king wal oso agena ceteteh cedein eu cawaladi cedimei ceselen .
Aria Ebram uqa Kedoleoma king leih uqaca gabandoin eu hanna aqimeig ceselein . Eu hedumei ceseli limei Sawe maha asouna ono calen . Sawe eu ijan oso King Agena Maha Asou . Ono Sodom agena king Ebram gulucdon .
Ono Melkisedek Salemdec king uqaha Ebram gulucdon . Melkisedek uqa Anut Ohis Bahic uqana gemo tawec ihanec dana Ebram eeldoc je madugiannu bret wainca hewimei li gulucdon .
Odimei uqa Ebram eeldudu madon , “ Anut Ohis Bahic uqa sao mahaca ifanen eu Ebram eeldoiale .
Anut Ohis Bahic hina cesulheceb han wooldoga eu binan suleqale , ” don .
Odocob Ebram ceteteh cunug ila meceb li am 10 calen . Odocob 10 eundec osahic eu Melkisedek uten . Odocob Sodom agena king uqa Ebram madon , “ Dana cajaca ija iiteg ceteteh eu hina cedega , ” don .
Odocob Ebram Sodom agena king madon , “ Anut Ohis Bahic uqa sao mahaca ifanen eu uqa amegna wele je cagu madiga .
Ija hinana ceteh oso qee ugaun . Halu wegecfo jaimiga tacec halufo qee ugaun . Hibna hina ija Ebram cehewanca mudem ec madagaun .
Ijadodocnu ija ceteh oso qee ugaun . Ijana dana sab jein eu cois agena ceteteh eu himec ugen . Qa ijana danah Ane , Eskol , Mamrica eu age age mugumuga mec eu himec cois oqagan , ” don .
Odocob ceteteh i hedocob Tibud uqana je ola codocna Ebramca humei madon , “ Ebram hina cain cucuiagaun . Ija hina cofhi cuhadumig hina wadacdoc ameg ben bahic ihigen , ” don .
Qa Ebram jejeg hewi madon , “ O Tibud ijana Ben ija melca qee . Hina adi wadacdoc ameg ben bahic itegan ? Ija cal meceminfi ija cehewani eu Eliesa Damaskasdec ugian .
Mel oso qee itelemnu eunu cabi dana oso ijana jona bilia cehewani eu ugian , ” don .
Odocob Tibud uqa Ebram haun madon , “ Cabi dana i hina cehewain qee oiaun qa hinadodoc melem uqa hina cehewain eu ugian , ” don .
Odimei Tibud uqa Ebram ehudeceb maha gumu cali lesin . Odimei madon , “ Faga ! Saona isec meciimeg malaqa sicanadaga . Hina sicanadecnu ihocfa hinana sihul ha malaqa nijia eu odiwe nijigian , ” don .
Odocob Ebram Tibudna jenu meleen . Eunu Tibud uqa Ebram gale docob uqa dana ititom don .
Odimei uqa madon , “ Ija Tibud . Ija maha i ihecemin hinana biligiannu Ur Kaldia agena hatunadec ehihi ahom , ” don .
Qa Ebram sisildon , “ O Tibud ijana Ben maha i ijana biligian eu adi dugen ? ” don .
Eunu Tibud uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Hina bulmakau osoca meme osoca sipsip manahal osoca agena cabi gel ijed doc eundec cedi ahutuga . Euha cuhudid lecisca eu odi cedi ahutuga , ” don .
Odocob Ebram uqa ceteteh eu age cedimei Anutca ahon . Odimei uqa dool eu cunug qatani lecis aali helen . Odimei uqa nahanaha eu am lecisna mealen . Qa cuhudid eu qee tuqalel .
Odocob alog leih age nimeig cuhun joqaga bili odocobil qa Ebram jabadeceb belein .
Odi oodon am tonen . Oodon Ebram uqa us docob cal mecwe bahic nijen . Uqa eu odi ninijen uqa ceteh ola odocna cinigwe fimei ben bahic cucuien .
Odocob Tibud uqa Ebram odi madon , “ Hina du cuhadogale . Hinana sihul eu age cele agena mahana jag biluqagan . Odimeig age cabi dana gauc biluqagan . Odocobil cele dana age me qee mamadebil li cabi gel 400 ugian .
Qa cele dana eu age kobol eu odi odoqagan ija wadacadigen . Odocomin hina jajainel age hatu eu cuculeig ceteteh mati bahic cedi hewi beloqagan .
Euqa hina bibili li toia mimeg hina wawin bodoecca cal mecem hel cisihuqagan .
Hinana sihul eu maha ina mahuc qee ceseli howain . Amo sihul age maha ina bilegina kobol me qee mati bahic eu qee odi hedoc nijia . Cabi gel 400 leceb age odi hedocobil aria ija age gagadic wadacadimig maha inadec ititacadigen . Odocomin saen euna hina jajainel ene ceseli hoqagan , ” don .
Aria cam casileceb tu gihodon . Oodon hal jaca oso calen . Oodon ceial ja belicanca osoha calen . Odimesi ale dool am lecis aali na naha mealec eu gemo cobosin .
Witic euna himec Tibud uqa Ebram bal cehec je madumei madon , “ Maha i cunug ija hinana sihul adigen . Eu uqana gadac eu Isip agena wanadec nueceb wa ben Jufretis gadac .
Age Ken agena mahaca Kenis agena mahaca Kadmon agena mahaca
Het agena mahaca Peres agena mahaca Refaim agena mahaca
Amo agena mahaca Kenan agena mahaca Girgas agena mahaca Jebus agena mahaca eu cunug adigen , ” don .
Aria Ebram Kenan mahana bibilen cabi gel 10 hedocob Sarai Ebram aideg uqa Ebram mel oso qee basitol . Qa uqa Isipdec cabi caja osoca . Uqa ijan Hega . Eunu Sarai Ebram madon , “ Faga ! Tibud uqa ija mel cain basigaunnu wawi jic menen . Eunu hina ijana cabi cajaca lecem nijesia . Ija mel uqanadec ugenfa , ” don . Odocob Ebram Saraina je don . Odocob Sarai Ebram aideg uqa Hega uqana cabi caja Isipdec ehudi ehi li uqa aideg biligiannu gemug Ebram uten .


Odocob uqa Hegaca nijimesi Hega uqa melca men . Odocob Hega uqa melca fimei uqa culaug ocob Sarai cewudoloi .
Odocob Sarai uqa Ebram madon , “ Hega ija cewitina eu hinana cahuldoc . Ijadodoc ijana cabi caja ihem qa uqa melca mimei uqa cewitina . Ija cahuldomfo qee hina cahuldomfo ? Tibud uqa tem li figian , ” don .
Odocob Ebram uqa Sarai jejeg hewi madon , “ Faga ! Hinana cabi caja eu hina ebenna bilia . Hina adi odudegannu gale hena eu odudoga , ” don . Odocob Sarai uqa galac mecna isec cabi culumencaca uten . Odocob Hega uqa Sarai amegnadec busalen .
Aria odocob Tibudna ensel uqa Hega wadau naca qeena wa tut cemenug bibilen gulucdon . Wa tut eu Sur nuec jicna .
Odimei uqa madon , “ Hega , Saraina cabi caja , hina anadec hoga ? Odeia hina ana nuuguna ? ” don . Odocob uqa maden , “ Ija ijana ben Sarai amegnadec busaligina , ” en .
Odocob ensel uqa madon , “ Ceseli hinana benca nuuga . Odimeg uqa co toodu odoga , ” don .
Odimei uqa haun madon , “ Ija hinana sihul eu odadecemin mati bahic fulusdoqagan . Eu oso sicani madecwe qee .
Faga ! Hina mel oso basegan . Tibud uqa hinana culumennu wawin qajena eu dah meia . Eunu hina uqa ijan Ismal qogan .
Qa uqa cesel cus cinigwe cocobi biligian . Uqa dana cunug cad madigian . Odocob dana cunug age uqa cad muduqagan . Odocob uqa cotugul gami gidod biluqagan , ” don .
Odocob Hega uqa uqadodoc waug maden , “ I mele bahicfo ? Anut ija gaid mecitina eu figaqa ija cebac biliga , ” en . Eunu uqa Tibud ijan Anut Mecitina qon .
Eunu wa tut hunec eu Kedes Beretca gemo nijia age “ Oso Cebac Bilina Uqa Mecitina Uqana Wa Tut , ” ec madegina .
Odocob Hega mel oso basen . Odocob Ebram uqa mel eu ijan Ismal qon .
Saen euna Ebram uqana cabi gel eu 86 odi .
Aria saen Ebram uqana cabi gel 99na Tibud uqa Ebraham amegna calimei madon , “ Ija Anut Gagadic Bahic . Ija amina ititom coboga .
Ijana bal cehec je ijaca hinaca gemo mudigen . Ija odocomin hinana sihul eu gadacca qee fulusdugian , ” don .
Odocob Ebram uqa maha cotadon . Oodon Anut madon ,
“ Bal cehec je eu i edi mudigina . Hina hatu mati bahic age asaga calegan .
Ija hina hatu mati bahic age asaga mihigen . Eunu hina haun ijain Ebram qee howain qa hina ijain Ebraham hoqagan .
Ija odadecemin hinana sihul mati bahic caloqagan . Leih age king caloqagan . Ija odadecemin hinana sihul hatu filfil caloqagan .
Bal cehec je eu bileceb catanecnu mudigen . Euqa ijaca hinaca gemo biligian . Hinana sihul hibna cali hoqagan eu age gemo ha biligian . Bal cehec je eu odi . Ija hinana Anut biligen . Hinana sihul hibna cali hoqagan eu agena Anut ha biligen .
Qila hina Kenan hatuna jag biliga . Qa hatu i cunug eu hinana biligiannu ihigen . Hinana sihul cunug hina toohi cali hoqagan , eu ha agena biligiannu , adigen . Euqa ageca bileceb catanigiannu adigen , ” don .
Odocob Anut haun Ebraham madon , “ Aria hinanu je qa odi . Hina ijana bal cehec je eu hewec bahic hewaga . Hinana sihul hibna hina toohi cali hoqagan eu age ha hewec bahic hewoqagan .
Bal cehec je eu hinaca hinana sihulca biligian eu odi . Hinana sihulna manahal cunug eu mel simca dana cunugca deweg gaga qoc bahic qoqagan .
Hinana sihul hibna cali hoqagan eu manahal cunug eu mel simca dana cunugca deweg gaga qoqagan . Mel sim cunug basecebil deel eben naha gic ijedca hedocob age deweg gaga qoc bahic qoqagan . Hinana jona cabi dana cunug cali hoqagan euca hinana sihul qee hinana begabeg ageca deweg gaga qoqagan . Hina deweg gaga qogan . Euqa bal cehec je ija hinaca gemo bilia eu uqana gadac .

Cel cabi dana hinana jona cali hugian o begabeg age deweg gaga qoc bahic qoqagan . Eunu ijana bal cehec je eu age dewenegana biligian . Eu bal cehec je bileceb catanigiannu gadac .
Odocob manahal oso uqa deweg gaga qee qolfi uqana sihulnadec ijan qetoqagan . Uqa ijana bal cehec je eu qee toodol , ” don .
Odocob Anut uqa Ebraham madon , “ Hina aiden , ijan Sarai , eu haun Sarai qee dogaun qa qila hina uqa ijan Sera dogan .
Odocob ija uqa eeldocomin uqa mel oso basihigian . Odocob Sera uqa hatuhatu age asaga caligian . Dana eu age leih king caloqagan , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa gob cehi bilimei jogoinu olana maha cotadudu bili asalen . Odimei uqa waugna maden , “ Dana ija edec ijana cabi gel 100 ija golaninadec mel oso cali hocnu ihocfo ? Odocob Sera uqana cabi gel eu 90 uqa mel oso basecnu ihocfo ? ” en .
Odocob Ebraham uqa Anut sisildon , “ Ismal uqa ija melami eeldocomin biligian ihocfo ? ” don .
Odocob Anut madon , “ Ao , euqa hina aiden Sera uqa mel oso basihigian . Odocob hina uqa ijan Aisak qogan . Odocob ijana bal cehec je eu uqaca mudigen . Euqa uqana sihul hibna cali hoqagannu mudigen . Bal cehec je eu bileceb catanigiannu mudigen .
Aria Ismalnu je madaga eu ija dah mihiga . Faga ! Ija uqa eeldocomin uqana sihul mati bahic fulusdoqagan . Uqana sihul eunadec hatu ilo 12 caloqagan . Uqana sihul hatu ben oso caligian .
Hina melem , Aisak , saen i edina cabi gel osona Sera basihigian . Euqa ijana bal cehec je eu hina melem Aisakca mudigen , ” don .
Saen Anut uqa Ebrahamca je madi hedumesi uqa culdimei ohis ti nuen .
Odocob deel euna himec Ebraham uqa Anut madon eu toodu odon . Uqa melah Ismalca uqana cabi dana uqana jona cali hoin euca uqana begabeg ageca deweg gaga aqaden . Uqana tal manahal eu cunug deweg gaga aqaden .
Aria Ebraham uqa uqana cabi gel 99na uqa deweg gaga qon .
Uqa melah Ismal uqana cabi gel 13na uqa deweg gaga qon .
Ebraham uqa melah Ismalca ale deel euna himec deweg gaga qosin .
Dana uqana jona cali hoinca begabeg ageca dana cunug Ebrahamca bilein age Ebraham gami deweg gaga qoin .
Aria Tibud uqa Ebrahamca camasac men . Saen euna Ebraham uqa Mamrina na gug benbenna lotoc talah cehi bilen . Cam eu gagadic tatawen Ebraham uqa lotoc talah cebecna bilen .
Bibilen uqa ameg suli umei dana ijed cemenug tatawegin meciaden . Saen Ebraham meciadimei uqa lotoc talah cebec culimei dana ijed gulucadecnu gudugudui len . Odimei uqa gob cehi bilimei jogoi nu maha cotadudu bili
maaden , “ Ijana ben ija age amagana tawecemin gale adenafi agena ewel dana cain wooldu belowain .
Age wa nag oso ahocobil jaimiga cuseigale . Odocob age na salu jaen mudeigale .
Ija sab oso saciaduadigen . Odocob age gagadic odoc umeig coboqagan . Age agena ewel danaca wele hoiga . Eunu ija loo adigennu culiteigale , ” aden . Odocob age madoin , “ Cois hina madaga eu odi odogale , ” doin .
Odocob Ebraham uqa mahucwe lotoc talah dunuh limei Sera madon , “ Hina mahucwe plaua uqana culumen eu 14 kilo odi umeg ibuldumeg managa , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa guguli bulmakau gelna len . Odimei uqa bulmakau nag oso eu uqa cuhun jecnu bodoec umei uqana cabi dana uten . Odocob cabi dana uqa bulmakau eu mahuc bahic cilecnu saciadugia bili nuen .
Odocob uqa bulmakauna su muhuc qagocca su haunca bulmakau nag cili saciadon euca ahu miaden . Odimei age jejegin uqa gesacna na salu meciadi tawen .
Odocob age sisildoin , “ Hina aiden Sera ai ? ” doin . Uqa jejenega hewi maaden , “ Uqa lotoc talah dunuh bilia , ” aden .
Odocob dana oso uqa Ebraham madon , “ Mele bahic saen ina cabi gel oso euna ija hinaca ceseli hugen . Euqa hina aiden Sera uqa mel oso wele basigian , ” don . Aria Sera uqa lotoc talah cebecna dah mimi bilen .
Aria Ebraham Seraca ale wele toia mesin . Alena cabi gel eu mati bahic . Sera uqana jagel qoc saen eu wele hedon .
Eunu Sera uqa uqadodoc waug dunuhna asali bili maden , “ Ija wele toia mem . Gemuni ha wele toia men . Gemunica nijimeu ija wawi migenfo ? ” en .
Odocob Tibud uqa Ebraham madon , “ Eu adi Sera uqa asali bili ija toia bahic eu mele bahic ija mel basigenfo ec madeia ?
Ceteh oso eu ija odocnu ija ihoc qeefo ? Ija cabi gel osona hinaca ceseli hugen . Saen euna Sera uqa mel oso wele basigian , ” don .
Odocob Sera uqa cucuiimei maden , “ Ija qee asalelem , ” en . Odocob uqa madon , “ Qeeo , hina asalaga , ” don .
Aria dana age beloqaga bili cajimeig age Sodom isec meciecebil non . Odocob Ebraham uqa culadeceb beloqaga bili osoben cocobi lein .
Odocob Tibud uqa uqadodoc waug maden , “ Ija ceteh oso odige bili eu Ebraham ameg jahundi odigenfo qeefo ?
Mele bahic Ebraham uqa uqana sihul hatu oso binanca caligian euha gagadic odocca . Odocob Ebraham sihul hatu cunug age eeldoc oqagan .
Ebraham melahulca uqana sihulca Anutna je toodocnu maadigian eunu Ebraham nesiludem . Euha Ebraham age ititom odocnuca me odocnuca dado madigian . Age odi odocobilfi ija Ebrahamnu je cunug madem eu odigen , ” en .
Odocob Tibud uqa maden , “ Sodom Gomoraca qisol ben bahic mesina dah miga .
Eunu ija noc bahic numig Sodom Gomoracanu madegina eu melefo qeefo figen , ” en .
Odocob dana lecis ale waldumesi Sodom isec belesin . Ale bebelesin Ebraham uqa Tibud olana tawen .
Odocob Ebraham uqa Tibud cemenug limei madon , “ Hina dana ititomca qisol mecca osoben tetec golisdocwe golisadeganfo ?
Dana ititom 50 taunna bilecebilfi hina eu cunug tetec golisdocwe golisadeganfo ? Dana ititom 50 bileiga eunu taun qee fadaldogaunfo ?
Hina dana ititom qisol mec danaca gabanadi qee madegafi euqa hinana kobol qee . Eu odi odogaqa hina dana ititom qisol mecca osoben ihocihoc odadegan . Eu odi odoc hinana kobol qee ! Hina mahamaha cunug agena gesilec dana . Hina tutuc gesilgec bahic gesilgaga , ” don .
Odocob Tibud uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija Sodom taun dunuh dana ititom 50 gulucadifig ija taun eu cunug qee fadaldugaun , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham haun madon , “ Ija Tibud je madocnu gauc temduga ijaqa dana mahanadec himec .
Dana ititom 50 qee bileleinfa . Eu 45 himec bileiga . Hina dana ititom 45nu taun qee fadaldogaunfo ? ” don . Odocob Tibud uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija dana ititom 45 gulucadifig ija eu qee fadaladigaun , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa haun madon , “ Dana ititom 40 bileigafa ? ” don . Odocob Tibud uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Dana ititom 40 bilecebilfi ija qee fadaladigaun , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa madon , “ O Tibud hina cain gemain beiaun . Culitecem je madiga . Dana ititom 30 bilecebilfi hina fadaladeganfo ? ” don . Odocob uqa madon , “ Dana ititom 30 ono gulucadifig ija qee fadaladigaun , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa madon , “ Ija Tibud je madocnu temduga . Dana ititom 20 gulucadifeg hina fadaladeganfo ? ” don . Odocob uqa madon , “ Dana ititom 20 gulucadifig ija taun eu qee fadaldugaun , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa madon , “ O Tibud hina cain gemain beiaun . Culitecem haun je madi osahic dugen . Dana ititom 10 himec gulucadifeg hina eu fadaladeganfo ? ” don . Odocob uqa madon , “ Dana ititom 10 bilecebilfi ija qee fadaladigaun , ” don .
Odocob Tibud uqa Ebraham je madu hedodoi ha uqa Ebraham cuculdi nuen . Odocob Ebraham uqa uqana cudunna ceseli nuen .
Aria Tibudna ensel lecis eu ale wesu Sodom ono calesin . Lot uqa taun cebecna bilen . Odocob Lot uqa mecialimei caji gulucaligia bili len . Uqa gulucalimei gob cehi mahana bilimei jogoi nu maha cotadoin .
Odimei maalen , “ Ijana ben lecis ale waldumesi alena ewel danana jona hosiale . Humesi jaimila cusesiale . Odimesi witic ene nijesiale . Odocobil ale uqadec qasil bahic cajimesi belowasan , ” alen . Qa ale jejeg hewi madosin , “ Qeeo , ele maha gemo cegulec cudunna us nijewan , ” dosin .
Odocobil uqa cesuscesusaleceb ale waldumesi uqana jona lesin . Odocobil Lot uqana cabi dana maadeceb age sab tinca oso saciadualein . Odimeig age bret jisca qee qagecebil jesin .
Ale us nijuwasa oodosin taundec dana age jo talildoin . Sodomdec dana toiaca mel haunca eu cunug age jo talildoin .
Age Lot utai sisildoin , “ Dana qila witic hinaca hoiga eu ai ? Ehali cali hocom ege canalecnu , ” doin .
Qa Lot uqa meciadigia bili jic cebecna cali len . Oodon uqa jic cebec hibilohu isec menen .
Odimei uqa maaden , “ Ija cotiel eu odi cain . Qisol mec kobol cain odowain .
Qa feiga . Ija ateniel lecis eu dana gami oso qee nijelesin . Culitecebil ija eu ale ehali ahocomin age agena gawecna odaloqagan . Qa dana eu ale adih oso cain odalowain . Ale ijaca loo hosia . Eunu me cofaligen , ” aden .
Qa age madoin , “ Jag , hina isa quguga ! Ege eeta odocomun cain magagaun . Hina isa quguga . Qeefi hina me qee odiheqan eu wooldoc ale me qee odaleqan , ” doin . Age Lot gagadic bahic sundoin . Odimeig age cebec batawoqaga bili cemenug lein .
Dana lecis dunuh bilesin euqa ebenela hocob Lot hewi didocobil jo hamol len . Odimesi ale jic cebec menesin .
Odimesi ale fulacdocna dana toiaca mel haunca aqesin . Ale fulacdocna amaga afac quadecebil jic cebec walecnu cabi mein .
Odimesi dana lecis ale Lot madosin , “ Ele taun i fadaldowan . Eunu hinana talnadec indec oso melemfo atenfo atenel gemulailfo hinaca taun ene bilecebilfi eu cedadecem taun i culimeig beleiga . Euqa Tibud agena qisol mec eu me qee bahic dah men . Eunu Tibud uqa fadaldocnu sulleia , ” dosin .

Odocobil Lot uqa cali limei dana lecis uqa ategul cedalowasannu je nijen eu maalen , “ Cajesia ! Taun i culdesia ! Tibud uqa taun i fadaldugian , ” alen . Odonqa ale uqa udoc je maalena ec cisdosin .
Odocobil qasil cocojagen ensel lecis ale Lot cesusdudu madosin , “ Cajaga ! Odimeg hina aidenca hina atenel lecisca cedadecem beleiga . Qeefi ageha fadaloqagan ele taun i fadaldowan saenna , ” dosin .
Lot uqa cisdoc lecisca men . Euqa Tibud uqa uqanu waug qon . Eunu dana lecis ale uqa ebenca aideg ebenca uqa ategul ebenelaca hewadi ahu cedimesi ehadi taun gesacna nui madesin .
Odocobil ale ehadi nui taun gesacna madimesi dana eu ale oso maaden , “ Mahuc busaleiga ! Age cal mowainnu busaleiga ! Hibilomoga isec cain meciowain . Maha asouna ha cain tawowain . Aluhna busali beleiga . Qeefi taun i fadaldodohul ageha fadaloqagan , ” aden .
Qa Lot uqa maalen , “ O ijana ben lecis eu ihoc qeeo .
Ale ijanu gale alena . Eu nalug mec kobol ihactesia . Euqa ija cal migaunnu cesultesia . Qa ija aluhna busali nuecwe qee . Ja i ija oiteceb cal migen .
Qa fesia . Taun oso i onoca qee ono busali lecnu eu nag ihoc . Ija culitecem ono busali liga . Ija ono lifig ija qee cal migaun . Eu taun nag bahic , ” alen .
Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madosin , “ Cois . Je madaga eunu ha cois howona . Taun hina madaga eu qee fadalowaun .
Aria mahuc ono busali beleiga . Age ono calecebil himec ele ceteh oso odocnu ihoc , ” dosin . Lot taun eu nag ec maden eunu taun eu ijan Soa dogina .
Aria walag dadanen Lot uqa Soa calen .
Odocob Tibud uqa meen dain gulgulecca jaca osoben saonadec suldocob wa cinigwe Sodom Gomoraca nen .
Tibud uqa taun eu ale eu odi fadalalen . Maha asou eu cunug fadaldon . Dana caja taun bilein euca ceteteh mahana cehec nijen euha cunug fadaldon .
Qa Lot aideg uqa Lot hibilohu isec meciimei si meen ibuldon . Odimei na tutuc cinigwe tawen .
Aria cojageceb Ebraham qasil bahic cajimei ceseli nui cudun uqa Tibud amegna tawen euna len .
Odocob Ebraham uqa mecieceb Sodom Gomoraca isec non . Odimei maha cunug asouna nijen euha fen . Ja casuc ben bahic mahanadec sao ohis teten eu fen . Eu cinim manecebil casuc cajenawe eu odi fen .
Qa Anut uqa taun lecis fadalalen saen euna uqa Ebrahamnu cisdumei Lot fadalec cudunnadec suldocob taun uqa bilen eu culimei busali nuen .
Euqa Lot uqa Soa bilecnu cucuien . Eunu uqa ategul lecis gami Soa culdimeig aluhna timeig age meen hatin osona bilein .
Odocob ateg matu eu milum madon , “ Ele memile uqa toia . Odocob dana oso ele ocnu ene qee bilel . Ele mel oso adi basewan ?
Gec hoga . Memile wain utocohul jimei dalul qocob uqaca nijeqan . Eu odifeu ele melca mewan . Eufi egena sihul gaid biligian , ” don .
Eunu witic euna ale memela wain utecebil jeceb dalul qon . Odocob ateg matu eu leceb memegca nijesin . Odosin memeg uqa ateg leceb nijimesi culdi cajen eu qee dol .
Odocob cojageceb ateg matu eu milum madon , “ Faga . Cum witic ija meica nijuwan . Gec qila witic ha wain utocohul jimei dalul qocob hina lecem uqaca nijuwasan . Eufi egena sihul gaid biligian , ” don .
Eunu witic euna ha ale memela wain utecebil jeceb dalul qon . Odocob ateg milum eu cajimei leceb memegca nijesin . Odosin memeg uqa ateg leceb nijimesi culdi cajen eu qee dol .
Eunu Lot uqadodoc ategul odaleceb ale melca mesin .
Odocob ateg matu eu mel oso basen . Odimei eu ijan Moab qon . Uqa Moab sihul asaga calen . Age qila bilegina .
Odocob ateg milum uqaha mel oso basen . Odimei eu ijan Ben-ami qon . Uqa Amon sihul asaga calen . Age qila bilegina .
Aria Ebraham uqa Mamri culimei Negew hatuna nuen . Odimei jobon lecis gemo bilen . Oso ijan eu Kedes . Oso ijan eu Sur . Hibna uqa Gera bilen .
Gera bibilen Ebraham uqa Seranu uqa ija cebinami ec oso madon . Eunu Gera agena king Abimelek uqa uqana cabi dana suladeceb nui Sera aideg biligiannu ehudi uqaca lein .
Odoinqa witic osona Anut uqa bebelecna Abimelekca humei madon , “ Sera uqa dana wele on . Hina uqa omnu hina cal mega biliga , ” don .
Qa Abimelek uqa Sera cemenug qee lec ninijen uqa Anut madon , “ O Tibud ija qisol mec oso qee odolom . Hina ijaca ijana hatuca fadaldoganfo ?
Faga . Ebraham uqadodoc Seranu ija cebinami ec maten . Seraha Ebrahamnu uqa ija cebinami ec maten . Eunu ija odom eu cisdoc tutuc odom . Ija silail qee melem , ” odi madon .
Odocob Anut uqa bebelecna jejeg madon , “ Hina odom eu cisdoc tutucna odom eu ija dugina . Eunu ija qee culihecemin caja euca lelem . Eunu ija hina cahuldogaunnu cahahahem .
Qilaqa caja eu gemugca suldocom ceseli ligian . Dana eu uqa ijana je hahun madec dana . Eunu uqa inondocob hina qee cal magaun . Qa hina caja eu qee ceseli suldocomfi hinaca hinana dana cajaca age cunug cal moqagan , ” don .
Cojageceb qasil bahic Abimelek uqa uqana cabi dana utaadeceb hocobil ceteh fen eu cunug saadeceb age ben bahic cucuiein .
Odimei uqa Ebraham utadocob leceb madon , “ Hina eetanu kobol eu odi odigem ? Ija hina adi oso cahulhem eunu hina culumen ben i ijaca ijana dana cajaca ege gemo migem ? Kobol eu odi odom eu hina qee oditoum .
Celnu eu odi odom ? ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa madon , “ Dana jobon enedec age Anutnu qee cucuiegina . Eunu age ija aideni ocnu qagatoqagan ec odi cisdom .
Qa Sera uqa ija cebinami eu mele bahic . Ele memile osolnadec qa ele anile eu filfil . Odocob ija uqa aideninu om .
Saen ija meina jona bibiligin Anut uqa oditeceb mahamaha loldudu cocobi bilig Sera edi madom , ‘ Hina ijanu nalunin mec eu i edi ihactoga . Anaana belewan eu hina ijanu uqa ija cebinami ec madagale , ’ dom , ” odi madon .
Odocob Abimelek uqa Sera ceseli suldocob Ebrahamca len . Odimei sipsipca bulmakauca cabi dana cajaca ha cedadi ahu Ebraham uten .
Odimei Abimelek uqa Ebraham madon , “ Maha fagana eu ijana maha . Hina maha ina ana bilegannufi hinana gawecna biligale , ” don .
Odocob Abimelek uqa Sera odi madon , “ Ija qaig uqana ameg eu 1000 silwa eu odi cebinem wele utiga . Eu gadac oso . Agena sihul cunug hinaca bilegina age hina silailca qee doqagan eunu gadac , ” don .
Aria Tibud uqa Sera Ebraham aidegnu caja cunug Abimelekna jona bilegina eu wawaga meniaden . Eunu Ebraham uqa Anut inondocob Abimelek uqa me men . Uqa aidegca uqana cabi cajaca eu wawaga jic hudiaden . Odocob age mel haun basecnu ihoc .

Aria Tibud uqa Seranu maden eu dahig bilen . Eunu uqa Seranu je wele qel qeti maden eu toodu odon .
Saen Ebraham uqa toia cocobon Sera uqa waugca mimei mel oso basiton . Euqa Anut saen gadac menna mel basiton .
Odocob mel Sera basiton eu Ebraham ijan Aisak qon .
Deel eben naha gic lecisca hedocob Ebraham uqa melah Aisak deweg gaga quton .
Aria Sera uqa Aisak basen saen euna Ebraham uqana cabi gel eu 100 gadac .
Odocob Sera uqa maden , “ Anut uqa oditen eunu ija celeboigina . Dana cunug ija celeboigina dah moqagaqa eu ageha ija gami celeboeqan .
In uqa Ebraham odi madoub , ‘ Sera uqa mel basimei su utigian , ’ doub ? Euqa uqa toia bibilen ija melah basituga , ” en .
Odocob mel eu meca mimei su jec culen . Odocob deel euna himec Ebraham uqa mel sim eunu ja qon .
Aria deel osona Ismal Isipdec caja Hega uqa Ebraham basiton eu uqa Sera melah , Aisak , bulamdodon Sera uqa fen .
Eunu Sera uqa Ebraham madon , “ Cabi caja eu uqa melahca ititacalecem belesia . Cabi caja eu uqa melah hina cehewain ija melami Aisaknu muguh biligian eu qee cesawi oiaun , ” don .
Qa Ismal uqaha Ebraham melah . Eunu Ebraham uqa Serana je eu dumei uqa waug culumen don .
Odocob Anut uqa Ebraham madon , “ Hina hinana cabi caja uqa melahca alenu cain jaen qihiaun . Aisak uqana sihulna eu hinana sihul mele bahic . Eunu eeta Sera mahena eu toodu odoga .
Cabi caja melah uqaha ija odocomin uqana sihul eu sihul ben oso caloqagan . Uqaha hina melem , ” don .
Odocob deel oso euna Ebraham uqa qasil bahic cajimei sabca wa leih dool ganacna tacec eu cedadimei uton . Odimei uqa mel Hega qatona mitumei suldocob nuen . Odocob uqa nuimei Biasiba wadau waca qeena lili huhu i cobon .
Odi cocobon wa dool ganacna eu qee men . Odocob uqa mel ehi li na nag oso salafuna muden .
Tawimei cocobi li bilen . Eu onoca qee . Uqa maden , “ Ija mel cal memeb cain figaun , ” en . Uqa ono bibilei co suli umei qajen .
Odocob Anut uqa mel qaqajen dah men . Odocob Anutna ensel saonadec Hega utadudu madon , “ Hega , eetanu qajagana ? Cain cucuiagaun . Anut uqa mel eu odi qaqaji ninijen wele dah meia .
Cajaga . Mel eu eben umeg cesuldocom cajeia . Ija odocomin mel eu uqana sihul eu sihul ben oso caligian , ” don .
Odocob Anut uqa ameg fogo dutocob wa tut oso fen . Odimei uqa limei wa eu dool ganacna wetimei mel uteceb jen .
Aria Anut uqa ameg mel eu cofdodon ben men . Ben memen uqa Paran agena wadauna bilen . Odocob uqa qali dana calen .
Odocob uqa anag Isipdec caja oso uton .
Saen euna Abimelek uqa uqana han dana ilo , ijan Fikol , uqaca belimesi Ebraham madon , “ Hinana odoc cunugna Anut hinaca bilia .
Hina Anut amegna qel qetec je oso madaga . Ija Abimelekca uqana melca uqana sihulca qee qauadigaun ec odi madaga . Ija kobol me bahic odihem . Eunu qel qetec madaga . Ija Abimelek uqana dana cajaca ija gemo biligina euca kobol me bahic odadigen ec madaga , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa madon , “ Hina mataga eu ija toodu odigen , ” don .
Qa Abimelek uqana cabi dana age Ebraham uqana wa tut oso cawaludein . Eunu Ebraham uqa Abimelek gonagona mudon .
Odocob Abimelek uqa madon , “ Indec odeia eu ija qee dugina . Hina oso qee matelem . Ija je oso qee dolom . Qila himec eunu dugina , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham sipsipca bulmakauca cedadimei Abimelek uten . Odocob ale bal cehec je madi cagosin .
Odimei Ebraham uqa sipsip nag cufunec eben naha gic lecisca cedadimei abes meaden .
Odocob Abimelek uqa Ebraham sisildon , “ Sipsip cufunec i age abes madaga eu eetanu odoga ? ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa madon , “ Hina sipsip nag eben naha gic lecisca cedadaga . Cedadecemfi Ebraham uqa wa tut i hunen oqagan , ” don .
Eunu cudun eu ijan Biasiba ein . Dana lecis ale cudun euna bal cehec je madi cagosin eunu .
Aria ale Biasiba ono bal cehec je madi cagocobil Abimelek uqa uqana han dana ilo Fikolca cajimesi Filistia agena mahana ceseli belesin .
Eu hedocob Ebraham uqa na oso , ijan tamaris , Biasiba ono cehen . Odimei uqa Tibud Anut Bilec Catanec binan sulen .
Aria Ebraham uqa odi odimei saen cecelac Filistia mahana bilen .
Aria hibna saen osona Anut uqa Ebraham temdon . Uqa madon , “ Ebraham ! ” don . Odocob Ebraham uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija i hen , ” don .
Odocob Anut madon , “ Hina melem osahic himec , Aisak , eu hina uqanu nalug magana eu ehudecem Moraia hatuna belesia . Odimeg ono aluh oso ija ihachigenna hina mel eu ihantaga , ” don .
Odocob qasil bahic Ebraham uqa cajimei uqana cesel saciadumei ja ihanecnu ha qatani sogon . Odimei uqa uqana cabi dana haun lecisca uqa melah Aisakca ehadeceb age cudun Anut madon euna belein .
Bebelegin deel hedocob Ebraham uqa ameg suli umei cudun Anut madon eu onoca ninijen fen .
Odimei Ebraham uqana cabi dana haun eu maalen , “ Ale ceselca ene bibilebil ija melca ele ono belewan . Ele ono cuha fimeu aleca haun ceseli howan , ” alen .
Odocob Ebraham ihanecnu ja sogonca umei melah Aisak qatona men . Odimei uqa ebenna ja cijecca jaca siginca cedali hewen . Odocob ale osoben cocobi belesin .
Ale odi cocobi bebeli bilesi Aisak uqa memeg Ebraham madon , “ Mei ! ” don . Odocob Ebraham uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Melami , ija i hen , ” don . Odocob Aisak uqa sisildon , “ Faga . Ja cijec jaca i hen . Qa sipsip ihanecnu eu ai ? ” don .
Odocob Ebraham jejeg hewi madon , “ Melami , Anut uqadodoc sipsip ihanecnu iligian , ” don . Eunu ale osoben haun cocobi belesin .
Belimesi ale cudun Anut madon euna calesin . Ebraham ono ihanec meen cabal gualen . Odimei ja sogonca meen cabal tatacan men . Eu hedocob uqa melah Aisak jaih ebenca libimei ja tatacan muden .
Odimei Ebraham uqa eben leceb melah qogia bili sigin on .
Qa Anutna ensel uqa saonadec utadudu madon , “ Ebraham , Ebraham ! ” don . Odocob Ebraham uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija i hen , ” don .
Odocob ensel uqa madon , “ Hina eben eu mel eu oso cain qududoiaun . Hina ceteh oso cain odudogaun . Hina Anutnu cucuiagana qila ija dugina . Hina melem osahic himec eu ija ihantecnu qee cahacdolom , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa falicdu meciimei hibilohu isec sipsip manahal oso uqana tub culilisna hagawen tatawen fen . Odimei uqa li sipsip eu on . Uqa umei uqa melah cudunna sipsip eu ihanen .
Odimei Ebraham uqa cudun eu ijan “ Tibud Uqa Igigian , ” qon . Eunu qila saen ina odi madegina , “ Tibud uqana aluhna uqa igigian , ” egina .
Odocob Anutna ensel saonadec Ebraham haun utadudu
madon , “ Tibud uqa odi madena , ‘ Ija Tibud . Ija ijanina qel qetec je oso migen . Hina melem osahic himec ija ihantecnu qee cahacdolom eunu mele bahic ija hina eelhigen .
Odimig ija odocomin hinana sihul mati bahic fulusdoqagan . Euqa malaqa saona nijiaca lanna cesic nijiaca eu odiwe caloqagan . Odocobil hinana sihul agena cad aqadoqagan .
Hina ijana je toodu odoga . Eunu mahamaha hatu cunug eeladigen eu odiwe hinana sihul eeldugen , ’ ena , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham Aisakca ale ceseli uqana cabi dana haun bilesin euna calesin . Eunadec age cajimeig osoben Biasiba belein . Aria Ebraham uqa ono bilen .
Aria saen osona Milka , uqa Neho aideg , mel basaden eu Ebraham dah men .
Mel matu eu ijan Us . Uqa waliagul ijanaga eu Bus , Kemuel ,
Kesed , Haso , Pildas , Jitlap , Betuelca . Kemuel uqa Aram memeg .
Betuel uqa Rebeka memeg . Mel eben naha gic ijedca eu age Milka uqa Neho basaditon . Neho uqa Ebraham waliag .
Reuma uqa Nehona cabi caja oso uqaha mel basaditon . Ijanaga eu Teba , Gaham , Tahas , Makaca .
Sera uqana mahana coboc cabi gel eu 127 .
Odocob uqa Kenan mahana Hebron ono cal men . Odocob Ebraham Seranu uqa me qadac qajen .
Odocob Ebraham uqa aideg deweg ganac nijen cudun eu culdimei dana Hetna sihul eundecca nuimei maaden ,
“ Ija dana jag . Ija age gemo loldudu cobigina . Aideni hel cisigennu age maha oso idadecnu culiteiga , ” aden .
Odocob age jejeg hewi madoin ,
“ O egena ben dah migigale . Ege gemo hina king melah cinigwe . Eunu hinana gawecna cel meen hatin eu gale hena euna hina aiden deweg ganac hel cisigale . Egena meen hatinnu oso qee cahachoqaun , ” doin .
Eunu Ebraham uqa cajimei age amagana jogoen .
Odocob Ebraham uqa odi maaden , “ Age ija maha ene ijana caja deweg ganac hel cisecnu cois toqaganfi age Efron , Soha melah , ija coni umeig maduteiga .
Eu odi maduteiga , ‘ Ebraham uqa Makpela meen hatin fajecnu gale dona . Makpela meen hatin eu hinana cabi cemenug nijia . Uqa fajecnu coisfo ? Meen hatin eu fajecnu ameg cunug ihigian . Euqa uqana qalqal biligian . Eu fajecnu eu ege amigena odigian , ’ odi maduteiga , ” aden .
Odonqa Efron uqa uqana dana age taun cebecna gabandoin bibilegin uqa age gemo bibili bilei cunug dah memegin uqa Ebraham madon ,
“ Ijana ben , qeeo . Dah mitiga . Ija cabi eu ihigina . Meen hatin cabi euna nijia euha ihigina . Dana caja melamagail amagana ihigina . Aiden deweg ganac euna hel cisiga , ” don .
Qa Ebraham uqa haun maha eunadec dana cajaca amagana jogoen .
Odocob age amagana uqa Efron madon , “ Hina dah mitigale . Ija cabi eu uqana ameg ihigen . Hina cabi eu ameg ocom ija aideni deweg ganac euna hel cisigen , ” don .
Odocob Efron uqa Ebraham jejeg hewi madon ,
“ O ijana ben dah mitiga . Cabi i uqana ameg eu silwa 400 eu odiqa hina eunu cain cisdogaun . Eunu aiden euna hel cisiga , ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa Efronna je dah mimei uqa meen qaig 400 silwa eu odi saniimei uten . Meen qaig ameg eu Ebraham uqa wele dana cajaca Het sihuldec amagana maden . Ebraham uqa idadec doc dana cinigwe meen qaig eu sanien .
Eunu idadec jicna bahic Ebraham uqa Efronna cabi Makpela ono , eu Mamri cemenug , faji on . Cabica meen hatinca na cunug cabi euna tawein euca uqa faji on .
Eunu Het dana age taun cebecna cegulein bibilegin age amagana Ebraham uqa cabi faji on .
Eu cunug hedocob Ebraham uqa aideg Sera meen hatin cabi euna nijia ono hel cisen . Cabi eu Makpela ono Mamri cemenug nijia eu Kenan hatuna nijia .
Eunu cabi meen hatinca eu Ebraham faji on . Euqa idadec jicna Het melahul ebeneganadec qalqalnu faji on .
Aria Ebraham uqa wele toia men . Uqa bibilen cabi gel mati bahic nuen . Ceteteh cunug uqa odon eu Tibud uqa eeldon .
Odocob Ebraham uqa uqana cabi dana matu eu uqana cabi cunugnu ilo eu madon ,
“ Hina ebein ija tucumi gemo mimeg qel qetec je oso madaga . Anut uqa saonaca mahanaca Tibud bilina , hina uqa amegna qel qetec je madaga . Hina melaminu Kenan sihulnadec caja oso qee u togaun .
Qa hina nuimeg caja ijana hatunadec euqa ijana sihulnadec oso u ija melami Aisak uqa aidegnu u togan , ” don .
Odocob cabi dana uqa sisildon , “ Caja eu maha ina tooti hocnu culecebfi ija adi odigen ? Hina melem ehudi ceseli nui maha hina homnadec euna mudigenfo ? ” don .
Odocob Ebraham uqa jejeg madon , “ Batut fagale ! Ija melami ono cain ehudi lagaun .
Anut uqa saonadec Tibud , uqa ija meina jonadec ehiten . Odocob ija meina joca maha ija cali hom euca culem . Odocob uqa bal cehec je matimei je hahun i maten , ‘ Maha i hinana sihul adigen , ’ ten . Eunu Anut uqa uqana ensel aquni suldocob jic qahihigian . Odocob hina ija melami uqana caja onodec u togan .
Qa caja eu hina toohecnu culecebfi hina Anut amegna eu odi odigen aga eunu hina dewenna jeca qee . Qa ceteh oso ija melami ono cain ceseli ehudi lagaun , ” don .
Eunu cabi dana eu uqa eben Ebraham tucuh gemo mimei Ebrahamna je eu toodu odigen en .
Odocob cabi dana eu uqana ben uqana kamel 10 cedadimei nuen . Uqa ceteteh me me leihha uqana ben ebennadec cedimei nuen . Uqa cajimei Neho uqana taun eu Mesopotemia hatuna nijia ono nuen .
Uqa niji u nui wesu memen uqa Neho uqana taun gesacna wa tutna calen . Odocob uqa kamel odadeceb gob qahi bilein . Saen eu caja agena wa wetec saen .
Odocob uqa Tibud Anut inondudu maden , “ O Tibud Anut hina ijana ben Ebraham uqana Anut , ijana ben Ebraham hinana kobol me bahic ihacdoga . Cabi i odocomin tutuc caligiannu cesultaga .
Faga . Ija wa tut gesacna tatawigin taunnadec mel aid age wa wetoqagannu hogina .
Ija caja oso madocomin , ‘ Hinana halon mahana toni mimeg ija wa gab oso itiga , ’ docomin uqa odi matecebfi , ‘ Wa gab jejem ija hinana kamelha wa adigen , ’ tecebfi mel aid eu ijana ben Aisak aidegnu camasac muditiga . Hina eu odi odocomfi hina ijana ben kobol me bahic ihacdogan ija dugen , ” don .
Uqa inondudu qee hedoc Rebeka uqa wa halon qatona bibilen cali hon . Rebeka uqa Betuel ateg . Betuel uqa Neho Milkaca ale melamala . Neho uqa Ebraham waliag .
Rebeka uqa caja taula olaca euqa uqa dana osoca qee nijelesin . Uqa wa tutna numei wa weti hedumei haun ceseli ben .
Odocob Ebrahamna cabi dana uqa mahucwe bahic guguli gulucdugiannu len . Odimei uqa madon , “ Hina hinana halonnadec wa nag itecem jecnu coisfo ? ” don .
Odocob uqa madon , “ Ijana ben gad wa gab jaga , ” don . Odi madudu bilei uqa mahuc bahic wa halonca qatonadec u ehi ni ebenna hewen . Hewimei uqa uteceb wa gab jen .
Uqa wa gab ji hedocob madon , “ Ija hinana kamelha wa adecemin ihoc jecebil gadacna culigen , ” don .
Odocob uqa mahuc bahic wa halonna eu basecdocob dool agena wa gab jec bohna non . Odimei haun guguli ceseli nu wa tutna wa weti ehi bi haun basecdon . Uqa eu odi dih oodon kamel wa ihoc jecebil culen .
Eu oodon Ebraham uqana cabi dana uqa jeca qee mecidudu cisdon , “ Tibud uqa kobol me bahic Ebraham ihacdonafo qeefo ? ” en .
Odocob kamel wa ji hedocobil dana eu uqa dahof oso eu golna mudec umei Rebeka medena men . Uqaha sai lecis eu golna mudec cedalimei Rebeka ebenna men .
Odimei uqa sisildon , “ Hina indec ateg ? Hina memenna jona ege us nijecnu cudun ihocfo ? ” don .
Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija Betuel ateg . Betuel uqa Neho Milkaca melamala .
Egena jona dool us nijecnu gigi galalecca sabca ihoc bilia . Hina us nijecnu cudunha ihoc bilia , ” don .
Odocob dana uqa gob cehimei mahana jogoen . Odimei uqa Tibud binan susuli
maden , “ Tibud binan wasi nuiale . Uqa ijana ben Ebraham uqana Anut . Uqa ijana ben kobol me bahic odudia . Uqa qee qaudol . Uqa ija dado mimiten hu ijana ben uqa waliagna jona caliga , ” en .
Odocob caja eu uqa guguli limei uqa anagna jona calimei uqana tal ceteteh eunu maaden .
Odocob Rebeka uqa cebinag Leban je eu madudu bilei dahofca saica ihacdocob fen . Odocob Leban uqa guguli cali limei wa tutna nuen . Odimei uqa dana eu ono kamel gami tatawegin fimei

madon , “ Ijaca belowa . Anut hina eelheia . Hina maha gemo odi cain tawagaun . Ija jo wele saciaduga . Hinana kamel agena cudunha wele saciaduga , ” don .
Eunu Leban uqa dana eu ehudi jona len . Odimei uqa uqana ud kamel homoganadec cedi mahana men . Odocob uqa gigi galalecca sabca kamel agena ahu aden . Odimei uqa dana euca leih uqa gami hoin euca jaimiga cusuqagannu wa ahu aden .
Odocob sab jecnu ahu mitoin . Mitocobil uqa maaden , “ Ija sab mahuc qee jigaun qa je maadigen huga eu casac maadi hedumig ija sab jigen , ” aden . Odocob Leban uqa madon , “ Cois , magaga , ” don .
Odocob uqa maaden , “ Ija Ebrahamna cabi dana .
Tibud uqa ijana ben Ebraham ben bahic eeldon . Eunu uqa cehewanca bahic calen . Uqa sipsip amca meme amca bulmakau amca silwaca golca cabi danaca cabi cajaca kamelca ceselca uton .
Aria Sera ijana ben uqa aideg ijana ben mel oso basiton . Euqa toia cocobi lili basiton . Odocob ceteteh cunug Ebraham uqa melah Aisak muguh eu uton .
Aria ijana ben oditeceb uqana je toodugennu qel qetec jena madem . Uqa maten , ‘ Hina ija melaminu Kenan hatunadec caja oso cain u togaun .
Qa nuimeg ija mei uqana jobon medeh uqana sihulnadec caja oso ija melami aideg biligiannu u ahu toga , ’ ten .
Odocob ija ijana ben sisildom , ‘ Caja ija qee tootecebfi ija eeta odigen ? ’ dom .
Odocob uqa jejeni hewi maten , ‘ Ijana Tibud , uqa amegna ija cobigina uqa uqana ensel suldocob hina cesulheceb cabi eu ocom ihoc ligian . Odocob hina ija melami uqana caja eu ija meina jobon medehnadec euqa uqana sihul eundec oso ahu togan .
Hina eu odi oodom ijana sihul gulucadecem age caja eu qee ihecebilfi jic eu himec qel qetec je eu qee migian , ’ ten .
Eunu ija qila wa tutna humig edi inondudu madiga , ‘ O Tibud Anut , hina ijana ben Ebraham uqana Anut , cabi i odocomin tutuc caligiannu cesultaga .
