Faga . Ija wa tut gesacna tawigina . Caja taula oso wa wetigiannu hohob ija madugen , ‘ Wa nag hinana halonnadec gab jigennu coisfo ? ’ dugen .
Odocomin uqa edi matecebfi , ‘ Cois wa gab jejem ija hinana kamelha wa adigen , ’ tecebfi caja eu ijana ben Ebraham melahnu nesilia ija dugen , ’ iga .
Odimig ija wawina inondudu qee hedudugin Rebeka uqa wa halon qatona gahidumei hoia . Odimei uqa wa tutna wa wetecnu noia . Odocob ija maduga , ‘ Hina wa gab itecem jecnu coisfo ? ’ duga .
Odocomin uqa mahucwe bahic wa halonca qatonadec u ehi ni ebenna hehewi bili mateia , ‘ Gad gab jaga . Oodom ija hinana kamelha wa adigen , ’ teia . Eunu ija wa gab jijigin uqa kamel wa adeia .
Odocob ija sisilduga , ‘ Hina indec ateg ? ’ duga . Odocob uqa mateia , ‘ Ija Betuel ateg . Betuel uqa Neho Milkaca ale melamala , ’ teia . Odocob ija dahof oso medena miga . Odimig sai lecis ebenna miga .
Odimig ija gob cehimig jogoi bilig Tibud binan susuli ijana ben Ebraham uqana Tibud Anut eeldoc je maduga . Uqa ija jic tutucna dado miteceb ijana ben uqana sihulnadec age ataga oso uqa melah aidegnu gulucduga .
Eunu age je madiga inu , ‘ Coisfo qeefo ? ’ teiga . Age ijana ben kobol me bahic ihacdodoig jic tutucna cesuldoqaganfo qeefo ? Tutuc mateiga . Odocobilfi ija aisecnu nuigen eu dugen , ” aden .
Odocob Leban Betuelca jejeg hewi madosin , “ Mele bahic Tibud uqa ene ehihi ahoia . Eunu ege jeca qee .
Rebeka i hen . Uqa umeg nuuga . Odocom uqa hinana ben uqa melah aidegnu biligian eu Tibud uqa ihacheia eu odi culituqale , ” dosin .
Odocobil saen Ebraham uqana cabi dana je eu dah mimei uqa Tibud amegna gob cehi jogoen .
Odimei uqa ceteteh silwaca golna mudec euca lotoc me bahicca cedimei Rebeka uten . Uqa ceteteh qaig bennadec Rebeka cebinagca anagca alen .
Odocob uqaca dana uqaca hoin euca age sabca waca jejeig age witic eu ono us nijein . Cojageceb age qasil cajimeig dana eu maaden , “ Culitecebil ija ijana benca ceseli nuigen , ” aden .
Odocob Rebeka cebinagca anagca ale madosin , “ Caja eu culdecem ege gami deel 7fo 10fo odi bilimeb hinaca belowasan , ” dosin .
Qa uqa maalen , “ Cain cahactecebil daleigaun . Qa qila Tibud uqa cesulteceb ijana cabi me caleia . Eunu sultecebil ijana benca nuigen , ” alen .
Odocob ale jejeg hewi madosin , “ Caja eu utadumeb uqana gale docnu sisildocnu , ” dosin .
Eunu ale Rebeka utadumesi sisildosin , “ Hina dana ica belowasanfo ? ” dosin . Odocob uqa maalen , “ Ija nuigen , ” alen .
Eunu Rebeka suldocobil Ebrahamna cabi dana gami belein . Cabi caja Rebeka uqa simnadec cofdodon ben men euha uqa gami belein .
Bebelegin age Rebeka eeldoc je madudu madein , “ Ege cebinamige , hina mati bahic fulusdogale . Hinana sihul agena cad aqimei lahaadi ititacadeiale , ” doin .
Odocobil Rebeka uqa uqana cabi cajaca age cajimeig agena kamel toboin . Odimeig age dana tooadein . Eunu cabi dana uqa Rebeka umei niji u ceseli nuen .
Aria Aisak uqa “ Oso Cebac Bilina Uqa Mecitina Uqana Wa Tut , ” ceseli hon . Uqa wadau waca qee Kenan ono bilen .
Wesu osona uqa cocobi bili uqa cabina nuen . Odimei uqa ameg suli umei mecien . Euqa uqa kamel hohogin meciaden .
Odocob Rebeka uqaha ameg suli umei meciimei Aisak fen . Odimei uqa kamel ohisdec tonimei
cabi dana sisildon , “ Eu cel dana ege gulucgigiannu cabina cocobi hona ? ” don . Odocob cabi dana uqa madon , “ Uqa ijana ben , ” don . Odocob uqa olanaga jahuldoc lotoc umei ola jahuldon .
Odocob cabi dana uqa ceteteh cunug odon eu Aisak madon .
Odocob Aisak uqa Rebeka uqa aideg biligiannu ehudimei uqa anagna lotoc talah dunuh muden . Uqa Rebekanu ben bahic nalug men . Wele Aisak uqa anag cal men . Eunu uqa waloc don qa qila Rebeka Aisak anagna cudun on . Eunu uqa waug ceelen .
Aria Ebraham uqa caja oso on . Uqa ijan eu Ketura .
Odocob uqa mel i age basaditon . Simran , Joksan , Medan , Midianca Isbak , Suaca .
Joksan uqa Siba Dedanca memela . Dedan melahul age dana sihul i age memega calein . Asur , Letus , Leumca .
Midian uqa melahul eu Efa , Efe , Hanog , Abida , Eldaca . Eu age cunug age Keturana sihul .
Aria Ebraham uqana ceteteh cunug eu Aisak uten .
Qa uqana cabi caja eu uqa aideg cinigwe biloloig eu age melamaga ha Ebraham uqa ceteteh leih loo aden . Odimei uqa suladeceb age Aisak culdimeig maha cam tobi becna isec belein .
Aria Ebraham uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc mahana bilen eu 175 .
Uqa toia men . Uqana cabi gel mati bahic . Odocob uqa kis umei cal men . Uqa asagul cal mein eu agena cudunna nuen .
Odocob uqa melahul Aisak Ismalca ale Makpela eu Mamri cemenug meen hatinna deweg ganac hel cisesin . Makpela eu Efronna cabina nijen . Efron uqa Soha melah uqa dana sihul Hitdec .
Cabi eu Ebraham uqa Hit dana ebeneganadec faji on . Aideg Sera hel ciseinna uqa ono hel cisein .
Ebraham cal meceb Anut uqa melah Aisak eeldon . Aisak uqa “ Oso Cebac Bilina Uqa Mecitina Uqana Wa Tut , ” ono bilen .
Aria je i eu Ismalna je . Ismal uqa Hega melah . Hega Isipdec uqa Serana cabi caja uqa Ismal Ebraham basiton .
Ismal melahul ijanaga i edi . Age ijanaga eu toodocobtoodocob cali hoin eu odi nijen . Nebaiot uqa Ismal melah matu . Uqa melahul leih eu Keda , Atbil , Mipsam ,
Misma , Duma , Masa ,
Hedat , Tema , Jetur , Napis , Kedemaca .
Uqa melahul eu age jobon medeh 12 calein . Uqa melahul 12 age ijanaga eu jobon medeh ijanaga filfil qoin .
Aria Ismal uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc mahana bilen eu 137 . Odocob uqa kis umei cal men . Uqa asagul cal mein agena cudunna nuen .
Odocob uqana sihul age maha Hawiladec nueceb Sur gadac euna niji u coboloig . Sur eu Isip maha cam tobi becna isec eu Asiria jic nuecna nijen . Age maha euna isec cotigcotigca han cacadi niji u coboloig .
Aria je i Ebraham melah Aisak uqana je .
Aisak uqana cabi gel 40na uqa Rebeka on . Rebeka uqa Betuel ateg uqa Leban cebinag . Betuel uqa Aram dana uqa Mesopotemiadec . Leban uqaha Aram dana .
Aria Aisak uqa aidegnu Tibud inondon . Odocob Tibud uqa uqana inondoc eu dah mimei wadacdon . Odocob Rebeka uqa melca men .
Oodon eu mel momodo lecis ale waugna niniji bilesi ale cadecwe mesin . Odocob Rebeka uqa maden , “ Tibud uqa elena inondoc dah menfi celnu i edi oditina ? ” en . Eunu uqa Tibud sisildugia bili len .
Odocob Tibud uqa madon , “ Mel lecis hina wawinna bilesia . Hina basalecem ale fulusdumesi sihul lecisna qatani filigandowasan . Oso uqa gagadicca eu oso wooldugian . Odocob matu eu milumna cabi dana biligian , ” don .
Odocob uqana basec saen hocob uqa mel gahca basalen .
Mel uqa casac cali hon eu bagic cacawac . Bagic eu golca . Eu dool deweg cinigwe . Eunu age ijan Iso qoin .
Uqa cali hocob uqa waliag toodu cali hon . Uqa cali hon eu eben oso Iso jaih bisoc hewimei cali hon . Eunu uqa ijan Jekob qoin . Aisak uqana cabi gel 60na uqa aideg mel eu basalen .
Aria mel lecis ale ben mimesi Iso uqa dool qoc gesis dana calen . Uqa bahu dana , uqa bahu nijoloi . Jekobqa uqa malol dana , uqa jeca qee . Odocob uqa lotoc talahna himec biloloi .
Aria Aisak uqa dool cus Iso qoloi eu jecnu gale doloi . Eunu Isonu nalug moloi . Rebekaqa uqa Jekobnu nalug moloi .
Deel osona Jekob uqa wehuc me bahic cilen . Oodon Iso uqa bahudec hon . Uqa wen geh bahic dodon hon .
Odocob uqa Jekob madon , “ Ija wenene qitina . Mahucwe macin wehuc golca eu itecem jiga , ” don . Eunu age Idom doin .
Qa Jekob uqa madon , “ Hina matu . Casac ceteteh hina mugum mec eu itiga ija ihigen , ” don .
Odocob Iso madon , “ Coiso ! Ija wele cal migen odigina . Eunu matu bilec eu cel me oso oditigian , ” don .
Odocob Jekob jejeg hewi madon , “ Casac ija amina hinana matu bilec eu ija itigannu qel qeti mataga , ” don . Odocob Iso eu odi toodu odon .
Odocob Jekob uqa bretca me macin wehucca Iso uteceb jen . Odimei Iso cajimei nuen . Eunu Iso uqa uqana matu bilec eu ceteh gauc cinigwe qelen .
Aria saen osona cahel saen me qee oso calen . Eu Ebrahamna saenna calen eu odi we haun calen . Eunu Aisak uqa Abimelek Filistia agena king Gera ono bilina uqaca nuen .
Wele Tibud uqa Aisakca camasac mimei madon , “ Hina Isip cain nogaun . Maha ija mahigen euna biliga .
Maha ina nag odi biliga . Odocom ija hinaca biligen . Odimig ija eelhigen . Hinaca hinana sihulca ija maha i cunug adigen . Bal cehec je ija wele Ebrahamca madi cagoh eu ija hinaca ha madi cagowan .
Odimig ija hinana sihul eu odocomin age malaqa saona nijia eu odiwe caloqagan . Odimig hinana sihul eu maha i cunug adigen . Odocomin hatuhatu cunug hinana sihul jabajabna age ha eeldoc oqagan .
Ebraham uqa ijana loo jeca cunug ija madom eu ha uqa toodu odon . Eunu hina eelhigen , ” don .
Odocob Aisak uqa Gera ono bilen .
Saen dana jobon eunadec age uqa aidegnu sisildocobil uqa ija cebinami ec maaden . Rebeka uqa caja jaca bahic . Eunu uqa odi cisdon , “ Dana jobon inadec age Rebekanu ija qagatecebil cal migaun , ” en . Eunu uqa cucuiimei eu odi maaden .
Aisak uqa ono bibilen gieceb saen osona Filistia agena king Abimelek uqa fufu oc cebecna meciimei Aisak uqa Rebeka deweg losdodon fen .
Eunu king Abimelek uqa Aisak utadocob leceb madon , “ Faga . Uqa hina aiden ! Eu adinu hina uqa ija cebinami ec matem ? ” don . Odocob Aisak uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Uqanu ija qagatecebil cal migaun imig odi mahem , ” don .
Odocob Abimelek madon , “ Hina eeta odigiga ? Ijana dana oso hina aidenca nijoubmiqa eu hinanu Anut ege wadacgoub , ” don .
Eunu Abimelek uqa dana cunug je gagadic maaden , “ Dana oso dana ifo uqa aidegfo qudualifei mele bahic qocomun cal migian , ” aden .
Aria Aisak uqa maha euna sab cehen . Odocob Tibud uqa eeldon . Eunu cabi gel euna himec uqa sab eu wal meceb on eu mati bahic on . Uqa aig osol cehen eunadec aig 100 haun on . Eu odiodi on .
Odocob Aisak uqa cabi gaid odi oodon li uqa cehewan eu ben bahic men .
Uqa ceteh mati bahicca . Uqa sipsip , bulmakau , cabi dana amca . Filistia danaqa age uqana cehewan fecebil gale aden .
Eunu Filistia age wa tut hunec uqa memegna cabi dana age Ebrahamna saenna hunein eu age eu cunug maha tacitaci belein .
Odocob Abimelek uqa Aisak madon , “ Hina egena hatu culdimeg nuuga . Hina gagadicca . Hinana gagadic odoc eu egeca ihoc qee , ” don .
Odocob Aisak uqa eunadec cajimei nui Gera maha asouna ono cudun hewen . Odimei uqa ono bilen .
Odocob wa tut uqa memeg Ebrahamna saenna hunadein eu Filistia age tacalein eu Aisak haun hunaden . Odimei wa tut eu uqa memeg Ebraham ijanaga aqaden eu haun ijanaga aqen .
Odocob Aisakna cabi dana age maha asouna wa tut oso hunein . Odimeig age wa fifiji beben gulucdoin .
Eu hunein qa Geradec sipsip cofadec dana age Aisakna sipsip cofadec dana age wa tutnu gonagona mimeig maadein , “ Wa tut eu egena , ” adein . Eunu Aisak uqa wa tut eu ijan “ Gona Gona Mec ” qon .
Odocob Aisakna dool cofadec dana age wa tut oso haun hunein . Odocobil eunu ha age gonagona madein . Eunu uqa eu ijan “ Cadec ” qon .
Odocob Aisak uqa cudun eu culimei ono wa tut oso hunen . Odonqa age wa tut eunu qee gonagona mudelein . Eunu uqa wa tut ijan “ Jeca Qee ” qon . Uqa odi maden , “ Qila Tibud uqa cudun ihoc igia . Eunu ege maha ina danaca doolca cehewanigeca fulusdugian , ” en .
Odocob onodec uqa Biasiba ono ten .
Odocob witic euna Tibud uqaca camasac men . Odimei uqa madon , “ Ija hina memen Ebraham uqana Anut . Cain cucuiagaun . Ija hinaca biligina . Ija eelhimig odocomin hinana sihul fulusdugian . Euqa ijana cabi dana Ebrahamnu cisdumig odigen , ” don .
Eunu Aisak uqa cudun euna ihanec meen cabal oso gualen . Odimei uqa Tibud binan sulen . Odocob uqa ono uqana lotoc talah cecehen uqana cabi dana age wa tut oso hunein .
Odon saen euna Abimelek uqaca uqana cisdoc utec dana Ahusatca uqana han dana ilo , Fikol , uqaca age Gera onodec Aisakca hoin .
Odocobil Aisak uqa sisiladen , “ Age ija me qee oditein . Odimeig agena hatunadec ititactein . Eunu age celnu ijaca hoiga ? ” aden .
Odocob age jejeg madoin , “ Qila ege camasac doqona . Tibud uqa hinaca bilina ege doqona . Eunu ege odi cisdom , ‘ Ege gemo gabandocnu je oso cagu madecnu euqa hinaca egeca gemonu madecnu , ’ om . Qel qeti madecnu eu i edi madecnu .
Hina ege me qee qee odigigaun . Eu odiwe ege hina me qee mihecnu qee odi quduhilom . Egeqa gaid hina me eelhimeb sulhocomun wawin malolca nuem . Qila Tibud hina eelhen eu camasac doqona , ” doin .
Odocob Aisak uqa sab ben cilimei adeceb jein .
Odocobil qasil bahic cajimeig age qel qeti madein eu agedodoc age gemo madocobmadocob imeig Aisak uqa suladeceb wawaga malolca belein .
Aria deel euna himec Aisak uqana cabi dana age humeig wa tut oso hunein eunu madoin , “ Ege wa gulucdoqa , ” doin .
Eunu uqa wa tut eu ijan “ Qel Qetec ” qon . Eunu taun eu ijan Biasiba eu qila saen ina ha odi madegina . Biasiba je eu gug “ Qel Qeti Madec Uqana Wa Tut . ”
Odocob Iso uqana cabi gel 40na uqa caja lecis Hetdec cedalen . Caja oso eu ijan Judit , uqa Beri ateg . Caja oso eu ijan Basemat , uqa Elon ateg .
Iso aidegul lecis ale Aisak Rebekaca wawala dain calec alolosi .
Aria saen Aisak uqa toia memen uqa ameg wa hidon . Oodon uqa tutuc meciecwe qee . Saen euna uqa melah matu Iso utadudu madon , “ Melami , ” don . Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija i hen , ” don .
Odocob Aisak madon , “ Faga . Qila ija toia . Ija ijana cal mec deel eu ija qee dugina .
Qila hina hinana qalica gamedca cedimeg bahu nui dool cus aqi ahutuga .
Dool eu ahumeg wehuc jecnu tinca maga . Euqa ija gale tenana isec maga . Odimeg saciadu ahutecem jimig qee cal mec ninijeb ija eelhigen , ” don .
Saen Aisak uqa melah matu Iso madodon Rebeka uqa dah mudon . Eunu saen Iso bahu dool aqimei jobon hewi hocnu nunuen
Rebeka uqa melah Jekob madon , “ Faga . Ija hina memen uqa walin Iso edi madodon duga .
Dool cus leih aqimeg wehuc jecnu tinca saciadu ahutuga . Odocom ija jimig qee cal mec ninijeb ija Tibud amegna eelhigen ec madodon duga .
Aria melami je ija mahigen . Eu dah mi cuhadumeg eu odi toodu odoga .
Meme amnana bileiga euna limeg meme nag oso jecnu me bahic lecis cedali ahutuga . Odocom ija wehuc jecnu tinca hina memen gale donana isec ija saciadugen .
Odocomin hina memen ehi litocom uqa jimei qee cal mec ninijeb hina eelhigian , ” don .
Odocob Jekob uqa anag jejeg hewi madon , “ Faga . Ija wali Iso uqa bagic cacawac . Ijaqa deweni eu bagicca qee .
Ija mei uqa ija deweni tebandugiaqa ija cahuldugina eu dugian . Ija uqa amegna qauec danawe caligen . Odocob uqa qee eelteiaun . Gelitigian , ” don .
Qa Jekob anag uqa madon , “ Melami gelihec je ihecebfi eu ija ugen . Ija mahiga eu odi dih odoga . Nuimeg ceteteh ija mahiga eu cedi ahutuga , ” don .
Eunu uqa nuimei meme lecis cedalimei ahuton . Odocob uqa anag wehuc jecnu tinca uqa memeg gale donana isec saciadon .
Odimei Rebeka uqa melah matu Isona lotoc me bahic jona bilen eu cedimei uqa melah milum Jekob taciton .
Odimei uqa ebenca du jocosaigca eu meme ganacna jahulduton .
Odimei uqa sab tinca bretca saciadon euha melah Jekob uten .
Odocob Jekob uqa memegca humei madon , “ Mei , ” don . Odocob uqa madon , “ Ija i hen . Melami hina indec ? ” don .
Odocob Jekob jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija Iso , hinana mel matu . Ija hina mataga eu odi odiga . Caji bilimeg dool cus ija aqiga eu jaga . Odimeg hina ija eeltecnu ihoc , ” don .
Odocob Aisak uqa melah sisildon , “ O melami , eu adinu dool cus eu mahuc bahic gulucadaga ? ” don . Odocob Aisak jejeg hewi madon , “ Tibud , hinana Anut , uqa cesultecebnu ija odi mahuc bahic odiga , ” don .
Odocob Aisak uqa Jekob madon , “ O melami cemeni hocom ija dewen tebandugen . Euqa hina ija melami Iso bahicfo qeefo ? ” don .
Eunu Jekob uqa memeg Aisak cemenug len . Odocob uqa deweg tebandumei maden , “ Jejein eu Jekob jejeg qa eben eu Iso eben , ” en .
Odonqa Aisak uqa eu Jekob ec qee dol . Uqa eben eu bagic cacawac euqa uqa waliag Iso eben cinigwe . Eunu uqa eeldoc je utigia bili
uqa sisildon , “ Hina ija melami Iso bahicfo ? ” don . Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ese , ija Iso , ” don .
Eunu Aisak uqa madon , “ Ahutuga . Dool cus hina aqaga eu jimig ija eeldoc je ihigen ihoc , ” don . Odocob Jekob uqa ahutocob uqa jen . Uqa wain leihha ahutocob uqa jen .
Odocob Aisak uqa madon , “ Melami cemeni hocom ija cotahigen , ” don .
Eunu Jekob uqa cemenug leceb uqa cotadon . Oodi bilei uqa uqana lotoc cahug eu don . Eunu uqa eeldudu bilei maden , “ Faga . Melami uqa deweg cahug eu cabi Tibud eeldon eu cahug cinigwe .
Anut hina saonadec coi ihiale . Uqaha sab me bahic mahanadec ihiale . Macinca wainca geh bahic ihiale .
Hatuhatu hina ewel uheheig hinanu jogoeigale . Hina cotinel agena ilo biligale . Hina aninna sihul age hinanu jogoeigale . Oso hina gelihecebfi Anut geludigian . Oso hina eelhecebfi Anut eeldugian , ” en .
Aisak uqa Jekob eeldoc je madu hedocob uqa Aisak olanadec nunuen saen qee giec uqa waliag Iso dool cusnu gumu tonen eu hon .
Uqaha sab jecnu tinca saciadumei memegna hewi ahuton . Odimei uqa memeg madon , “ Mei caji bilimeg dool leih ija quga eu jaga . Odimeg hina eeltec je mataga , ” don .
Odocob Aisak uqa melah Iso sisildon , “ Hina indec ? ” don . Odocob Iso uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija hina melem matu , Iso , ” don .
Odocob Aisak uqa gagadic bahic qeleli maden , “ Indec uqa dool qumei ija ahuteceb jiga ? Ija jimig uqa eeldocomin qila bahic nunuen hina hoga . Euqa uqa eeldoc ugian ijom , ” don .
Saen Iso uqa memegna je eu dah mimei uqa geh bahic gemagna isec qaqaji memeg madon , “ O mei , ija eeltaga . Ijaha eeltaga , ” don .
Odocob Aisak uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Hina walin ijaca humei uqa qauteia . Hinana eelhec je eu wele umei nuia , ” don .
Odocob Iso maden , “ Uqa ijan Jekob eu ihoc bahic qoin . Jekob uqana gug eu qauec . Uqa ija qauti lecis don . Uqa ijana matu bilec eu on . Aria qila uqa ijana eeltec je eu oia , ” en . Odimei uqa sisildon , “ Hina ijanu eeltec je oso culuga biliafo ? ” don .
Qa Aisak uqa Iso jejeg hewi madon , “ Faga . Ija uqa hinana ilo mudiga . Euha uqana cotugul eu uqana cabi dana madiga . Uqanu sabnuca wainnuca ija odi eeldoc je utiga . Uqana sabca wainca geh bahic calimei saen cecelac nijigian . Aria melami hinanu ija cel je oso madigen ? ” don .
Odocob Iso uqa memeg haun sisildon , “ O mei , hina eeldoc je osocafo ? O mei ijaha eeltaga , ” don . Odi madodoi uqa qajen .
Odocob uqa memeg jejeg hewi madon , “ Faga . Coi saonadec hinanu qee neiaun . Hinana cabinadec sab me bahic qee caleiaun .
Hinana bilec eu hina han seibulna cacadi bilegan . Hinaqa walinna cabi dana bilegan . Odeganqa hina fee dadaneesi hina uqa ilo bilecnu qajudogan , ” don .
Odocob Iso uqa Jekobnu gemag ben . Uqa memeg Aisak uqa Jekob eeldoc je uten eunu . Odocob Iso uqa cisdon , “ Ija mei uqana cal mec deel eu dodoldona . Uqa cal meceb ija wali Jekob qocomin cal migian , ” en .
Aria age Iso uqana je eu Rebeka madocobil dah mimei uqa Jekob utadocob hocob madon , “ Hina walin uqa qagaheceb cal megannu cisdocna aisais mimi bilei uqadodoc waug soadudu cobona .
Eunu melami jejeni dah maga . Odimeg mahuc bahic cajimeg busali cebinami Lebanca Haran nuuga .
Odimeg ono uqaca bilecem saen gieiale . Ono bibilem hina walin uqa gemag qee migian .
Uqa hinanu gemag qee meceb hina odudem eunu dahig celeceb ija je suldocomin hina onodec ceseli hogan . Qeefi melamiel ale qocobqocob imesi deel osolna cal mowasindain , ” don .
Odocob Rebeka uqa Aisak madon , “ Isona Hitdec caja eu alenu alal tena . Jekob uqaha Hitdec caja oso uqa aidegnu ocobfi euqa ijana bilec mahana eu ihoc qee caleiaun , ” don .
Odocob Aisak uqa Jekob utadocob hocob eeldudu je gagadic madon , “ Hina Kenandec caja cain ogaun .
Cajimeg Mesopotemia hina asin Betuel uqana guc ono nuimeg hina memen Leban uqa ategul eundec oso hinana cajanu oga .
Anut Gagadicca Bahic hina eelheiale . Odimei uqa odocob hinana sihul eu mati bahic caligian . Hinana sihul hatuhatu mati bahic caloqagan .
Uqa Ebraham eeldon eu odiwe hinaca hinana sihulca eeladigian . Euqa maha i Anut uqa Ebraham uton eu hina biliga eu ogan , ” don .
Odocob Aisak Jekob suldocob uqa Lebanca Mesopotemia onoca nuen . Leban uqa Betuel melah . Ale Aram dana . Leban uqa Rebeka cebinag . Rebeka uqa Jekob Isoca anala .
Aria Iso uqa Aisak Jekob eeldudu je eu madumei caja oso ocnu suldocob Mesopotemia nuen don . Aisak uqa je odi Jekob madon , “ Hina Kenandec caja oso cain ogaun , ” ec madodon Iso uqa don .
Jekob uqa memeg anagca conola toodumei Mesopotemia nuen euha Iso uqa don .
Odocob Iso uqa memeg Aisak Kenandec caja ocnu waug qee nijel eu fen .
Eunu uqa Ebraham melah Ismalca nuimei caja haun oso , ijan Malahat , on . Malahat uqa Nebaiot cebinag . Euqa uqa caja casac cedalen eu qee ititacalel .
Aria Jekob uqa Biasiba culimei Haran isec nuen .
Uqa nunuen cam casi leceb cudun osona witic meceb us nijigiannu bilen . Odocob uqa eunadec meen oso umei ilona tet qumei cosoli nijen .
Odocob uqa us ninijei bebelen . Uqa bebelii edi fen . Wadowad oso naha eu mahana qudoc naha eu ti sao qududoc fen . Wadowad euna Anutna ensel age wadowad eu tobi toni eegin meciaden .
Oodon eu uqa Tibud cemenug tatawen fen . Odocob uqa madon , “ Ija Tibud , ija Ebraham Aisakca alena Anut . Maha hina nijiga eu ija hinaca hinana sihulca adigen .
Hinana sihul euha age mati bahic caloqagan . Age maha bobos cinigwe caloqagan . Odimeig maha hagen cunug ihoc loqagan . Hinaca hinana sihulca agenu dana sihul cunug mahana biluqagan eu eeladec oqagan .
Aria faga . Ana nuegan eu ija hinaca belewan . Bebeleu ija cofhigen . Euha ija maha ina ceseli ahu mihigen . Ija hina qee culihigaun . Ija hinaca bibilig li je cunug mahiga eu odigen , ” don .
Odocob Jekob us nijecnadec seli cajimei maden , “ Mele bahic , Tibud uqa cudun ina bilia eu ija qee dolom , ” en .
Odimei uqa cucuii maden , “ Cain . Cudun i cucuianca bahic . Mele bahic i Anutna jo . I sao cebec , ” en .
Eunu Jekob uqa qasil bahic cajimei meen uqa tet qu nijen eu umei dahig biligiannu gadac cehen . Odimei Anut utecnu mool meen eu tatac basecdon .
Odocob uqa cudun eu ijan Betel qon . Weleca taun oso cemenug nijoloi eu ijan Lus .
Odocob Jekob uqa Anut amegna je cagumei edi madon , “ O Tibud , hinaca belimeu ija jicna cofteteg sab jecnuca lotoc tacecnuca itiga .
Odimeg haun coftetem ija ceseli nui ija meina jona caligen . Hina odi odifeg hina ijana Anut bilegan .
Meen i ija cehiga eu Anutnu cuha fecnu cudun caligian . Ceteteh cunug hina itegan eu ija am 10na ila mimig am osahic eundec ceseli ihigen , ” don .
Odocob Jekob haun caji nuen . Uqa nuimei cam tobi bec dana agena mahana calen .
Uqa ono calimei wa tut oso fen . Wa tut eu cemenug sipsip am ijed wa tut eu gesacna ninijegin meciaden . Age wa tut eunadec wa adecebil joloig . Aria meen wa tut eu cufa qoc eu ben bahic .
Saen sipsip cunug cegulecebil sipsip cofadec age meen wa tut ameg qoc eu qosocdumeig wa adecebil joloig . Odimeig meen eu haun ceseli wa tut ameg qoloig .
Odocob Jekob uqa sisiladen , “ O cotiel age anadec ? ” aden . Odocob age jejeg hewi madoin , “ Ege Harandec , ” doin .
Odocob uqa sisiladen , “ Age Neho asag Leban uqanu doginafo ? ” aden . Odocob age jejeg hewi madoin , “ Ege uqanu doqona , ” doin .
Odocob uqa sisiladen , “ Uqa me biliafo ? ” aden . Odocob age jejeg hewi madoin , “ O uqa me bilia . Faga . Uqa ateg Resel uqana sipsip amca hogina , ” doin .
Odocob uqa maaden , “ Feiga . Qila cahineg eu sipsip gelna madec saen qee . Sipsip wa adimeig ehadi nu gigi jec cudunna madeiga , ” aden .
Odocobqa age jejeg hewi madoin , “ Ege eu odi mahuc odocnu qee nijel . Casac sipsip cunug hu gabandocobil meen wa tut conadec qosocdumeb wa adoqonanu , ” doin .
Uqa je maadi tatawen Resel memegna sipsip amca hoin . Uqaha sipsip cofadec caja .
Odocob Jekob uqa Resel uqa awig Lebanna sipsip amca hocobil fimei uqa limei meen wa tut cona eu qosocdon . Odimei uqa Lebanna sipsip wa aden .
Odocob Jekob uqa Resel cotadudu bilei qaqaji waug ceelen .
Odimei Jekob uqa Resel madon , “ Ija hina memen awig . Ija Rebeka melah , ” don . Odocob Resel uqa guguli limei memeg madon .
Odocob Leban uqa awig Jekob uqa je eu dah mimei uqa mahuc bahic gulucdugia bili guguli len . Odimei uqa cogadudu bili cotadon . Odimei ehudi jona len . Odocob Jekob uqa je cunug Leban sadon .
Odocob Leban uqa madon , “ Mele bahic hina ijanadec bahic . Hina ijana sihulnadec , ” don . Odocob Jekob uqa ono Leban gami jagel osahic eu odi bilein .
Odocob Leban uqa Jekob sisildon , “ Hina ijana sihulnadec eunu hina ijanu gauc cabi ogona eu cois bahic qee . Mataga . Hina cabi ogonanu cel ameg ogannu wawin nijia ? ” don .
Aria Leban uqa ategul lecisca . Matu eu ijan Lia . Milum eu ijan Resel .
Lia uqa ola fecnu me bahic qa Resel uqa olaca deweg cunug fecnu eu jaca .
Odonqa Jekob uqa Reselnu nalug men . Eunu uqa madon , “ Ija hinana cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca cabi ugen . Euqa hina aten milum Reselnu cabi ugenfi , ” don .
Odocob Leban jejeg hewi madon , “ Dana oso utecnu eu me qee qa hina ihecnu eu me bahic . Ene ijaca bilewan , ” don .
Eunu Jekob uqa Lebanna cabi cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca cabi on . Odonqa uqa saen eu cecelac cinigwe qee . Eu deel matica qee cinigwe fen . Uqa Reselnu nalug men eunu .
Aria Jekob uqa Leban madon , “ Saen gadac mitem eu wele qee meia . Ijana caja itiga . Odocom ija uqaca nijewan , ” don .
Eunu Leban uqa uqana jobonnadec dana cunug cedeceb age sab ben hewein .
Aria Leban uqana cabi caja Silfa eu ehudi ehi li Liaca mudon . Odocob wesu saenna Leban uqa ateg Lia ehudi ehi li Jekob uten . Odocob Jekob uqa Liaca nijesin .

Odonqa qasil Jekob uqa caja eu ola eu Lia fen ! Odimei uqa Lebanca limei madon , “ Celnu kobol i oditiga ? Ija Reselnu hina hinana cabi uhem . Celnu qautuga ? ” don .
Qa Leban uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Egena jobon kobol i edi . Mel aid milum eu matu wooldumei uqa casac dana qee ona .
Hina ocobocob ec i uqana ja qoc deel eunu cuha osahic himec bilecem leceb ege Reselha ihecnu . Odocob hina uqanu haun cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca cabi ogan , ” don .
Odocob Jekob uqa je eu toodu odigian ec maden . Uqa ocobocob ec uqana ja qoc euna bibilen li cuha osahic hedon . Odocob Leban uqa ateg Resel uqa aidegnu uten .
Euha Leban uqa uqana cabi caja Bilha ehudi ehi li Reselca mudon .
Eunu Jekob uqa Reselca nijesin . Odonqa uqa Reselnu nalug men eu wooldoc Lianu nalug men . Odocob Jekob uqa Lebanna cabi haun cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca cabi on .
Aria saen euna Tibud uqa Jekob Lianu qee nalug mel eu fen . Eunu uqa Liana mel jool huden . Euqa Reselna mel jool menen . Odocob uqa goud men .
Odocob Lia uqa melca mimei mel oso basen . Uqa maden , “ Tibud uqa ija wawi me qee mec eu fen . Mele bahic qila ija gemuni uqa ijanu naluni migian , ” en . Eunu ijan Ruben qon .
Odocob uqa haun melca mimei mel oso basen . Odimei uqa maden , “ Ija gemuni uqa ijanu qee naluni mena Tibud uqa dah mena . Eunu uqa melami i ha itia , ” en . Eunu uqa mel eu ijan Simion qon .
Odocob uqa haun melca mimei mel oso basen . Odimei uqa maden , “ Ija gemuni uqa mel ijed basitom . Eunu qila uqa ija fagtigian , ” en . Eunu uqa ijan Liwai qon .
Odocob uqa haun melca mimei mel oso basen . Odimei uqa maden , “ Qila ija Tibud binan suligen , ” en . Eunu uqa ijan Juda qon . Odocob uqa mel basec culen .
Aria Resel uqa Jekob mel oso qee basitumeinu uqa caja hiagnu hel men . Odocob uqa Jekob madon , “ Mel leih itiga . Qeefi ija cal migen , ” don .
Odocob Jekob uqa Reselnu gemag ben . Eunu uqa madon , “ Ija Anutfo ? Hina mel basecnu jic menihem , ” don .
Odocob uqa madon , “ Ijana cabi caja Bilha i hen . Uqaca nijimesi ija mel basiteia . Odocob jic ina uqanadec ijaha ijana talca bileqan , ” don .
Eunu Resel uqa Jekob uqana cabi caja Bilha aideg cinigwe uten . Odocob Jekob uqaca nijesin .
Odocob Bilha uqa melca mimei mel oso basen .
Odocob Resel uqa maden , “ Anut uqa tutuc gesilteia . Odimei uqa ija jejeni mele bahic dah mimei mel oso itia , ” en . Eunu uqa mel eu ijan Dan qon .
Odocob Reselna cabi caja Bilha uqa melca mimei mel oso Jekob haun basiton .
Eunu Resel uqa maden , “ Ija caja hica ben bahic licdoh . Odimeu ija wooldom , ” en . Eunu uqa mel eu ijan Naftali qon .
Saen Lia uqa mel basecnu culen eu dumei uqa uqana cabi caja Silpa ehudi ehi li Jekob aideg cinigwe uten .
Odocob Liana cabi caja Silpa Jekob mel oso basiton .
Odocob Lia uqa maden , “ Eu ijanu me bahic , ” en . Eunu uqa ijan Gad qon .
Odocob Liana cabi caja Silpa Jekob mel oso haun basiton .
Odocob Lia maden , “ Ija wawi ceelena . Caja age ija ceelec toqagan , ” en . Eunu uqa ijan Asa qon .
Aria wit qetec saenna Ruben uqa cabina nuen . Odimei uqa na oso ijan mandreik eu uqana bobog ceden . Odimei eu hewadi ahumei anag Lia uten . Odocob Resel uqa Lia madon , “ Hina melemna mandreik bobog eundec oso itigamo , ” don .
Qa uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Hina ija gemuni ija cawaltem eu ihoc qeefo ? Eunu qila hina ija melamina mandreik bobogha cawaldocnu madaganafo ? ” don . Odocob Resel uqa madon , “ Hina melemna mandreik bobog itecemfi Jekob uqa hinaca qila witic nijuwasan , ” don .
Eunu Jekob uqa wesu cabinadec ceseli hohob Lia uqa gulucdugia bili len . Uqa gulucdumei madon , “ Ija wele ija melami uqana mandreik bobogna fajihiga . Eunu hina ijaca nijewan , ” don . Eunu witic euna Jekob uqa Liaca nijesin .
Odocob Anut uqa Liana inonec eu dah men . Eunu Lia uqa melca mimei uqa Jekob melah ebum osahic doc oso basiton .
Odocob Lia uqa maden , “ Anut uqa ija ijana cabi caja ija gemuni utemnu ameg wadac itia , ” en . Eunu uqa mel eu ijan Isaka qon .
Odocob Lia uqa haun melca mimei uqa Jekob mel eben naha gic osahicca doc oso basiton .
Odocob Lia uqa maden , “ Anut uqa ija ceteh me bahic oso itia . Ija uqa melahul eben naha gic osahicca basaditom . Eunu ija gemuni uqa ijaca gaid bilewan , ” en . Eunu uqa mel eu ijan Sebjulan qon .
Odocob hibna uqa mel aid oso basimei ijan Daina qon .
Odocob Anut uqa Reselnu dahig bilen . Uqa Reselna inonec eu dah mimei uqa uqana mel jool huditon .
Eunu uqa melca mimei mel oso basen . Odimei maden , “ Anut uqa ija majani qu qeleia .
Uqa mel oso haun itia , ” en . Eunu mel ijan Josef qon .
Aria Resel uqa Josef baseceb Jekob uqa Leban madon , “ Sultecem nuiga . Ija ijana jobon nuigen . Ijana hatuna nuigen .
Ijana cajaca mel simca agenu cabi om eu itecem nuiga . Ija hinana cabi u cuhadom doga , ” don .
Qa Leban uqa madon , “ Hina gale hecebfi ijaca bilewan . Hinanu himec Tibud uqa ija eelten . Ija jahunec je eunadec duga .
Eunu hina cel ameg ogannu wawin nijia eu matecem ihigen , ” don .
Odocob Jekob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija hinana cabi u cuhadomnu doga . Hinana dool am cofaadigin fulusdoin eu ha dogona .
Saen ija qee hocna hina dool am nag bahic . Qa saen ija hocomin hinana dool eu fulusdu mati bahic doin . Hinana cel cabi oso ija om eu Anut cunug eeldon . Qilaqa ija ijana talnu cabi odi oso ugen , ” don .
Odocob Leban uqa sisildon , “ Ija adi fajihigen ? ” don . Odocob Jekob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Hina ceteh oso cain itigaun . Qa hina ceteh osahic i oditecemfi ija haun hinana dool cofadigen .
Qila ija culitecem hinana sipsipca memeca cunug dewenega tolotoloca eu ija cabi om eunu ameg cedadigen . Sipsip nag dewenega casca euha oso cedadigen .
Odocob hibna hina kobol tutuc ija odom eu dogan . Euqa hina cabi ameg item eu fimeg eunadec meme oso deweg tolotoloca qeefo sipsip nag oso casca qeefo fifeg ija hinanadec heje om ec dogan , ” don .
Odocob Leban uqa madon , “ Cois eu me bahic . Hina je mataga eu odi odowan , ” don .
Odonqa deel euna himec Leban uqa meme cufunec manahalca dewenega tolotolo qoc senenec eu cunug cedaden . Odimei uqa sipsip nag cascaca ha cedaden . Odimei uqa eu cunug melahul cofadecnu ebenegana maden .
Odocob Leban uqa jic oso nuen . Jic eu uqana cecelac eu deel ijed eu odi . Uqa Jekob culdeceb Leban uqana dool am leih eu gigi jejegin cofaden .
Odocob Jekob uqa na sihul filfil ijed eundec batac osolosol qetaden . Na eu ijanaga eu popla , almon , plenca . Odimei uqa na eu age batac obutibit qasaladen . Odocob na caun senenec eu camasac men .
Odimei uqa na batac eu dool wa jegina agena boh cemenug quaden . Euqa dool wa jejegin age tobadoloig . Eunu na batac eu ono quaden .
Odocob meme age na batac cemenug tobadecebil hibna age nag basein eu tolotoloca cascaca basadein .
Odocob Jekob uqa sipsip nagnag eu fil maden . Odimei age olanaga waldocob age Lebanna dool dewenega tolotoloca cascaca meciadein . Eunu uqa jic eu odina Lebanna dool amnadec filiganadimei uqananu ceden .
Saen dool cufunec gagadicca age agena tobec saen caleceb uqa na batac eundec oso umei wa gab jec boh cemenug qudoloi . Age na batac eu cemenug li toboloig .
Qa dool oso uqa gagadicca qeefi uqa na batac eu olana qee qudoloi . Eunu dool gagadicca qee eu Lebanna lein . Odocob dool gagadicca eu Jekobna lein .
Odocob jic eu odina Jekob cehewan benca calen . Odimei uqa dool am mati bahic , cabi dana mati bahic , cabi caja mati bahic , kamel mati bahic , cesel mati bahicca men .
Aria Jekob uqa Leban melahul je edi mamadegin don , “ Jekob uqa ceteteh cunug ege memige uqana ceden . Ege memige uqana ceteteh eu ege memigedec cedimei uqa cehewanca men , ” eegin don .
Odocob eu culecnu . Wele Leban uqa Jekob me oduduloi qa saen ina uqa eu edi haun qee odudel eu uqa fen .
Odocob Tibud uqa Jekob madon , “ Ceseli maha hina memen bilinana nuuga . Hinana sihulca nueiga . Euqa ija hinaca bilewan , ” don .
Eunu Jekob uqa Resel Liaca je sulduali maalen , “ Humesi ijana dool am cabina cobigina euna ale guluctesia , ” alen .
Odocob ale limesi gulucdocobil uqa maalen , “ Ale memela uqa weleca ija me oditoloi qa qila eu odi qee oditina eu ija figina . Euqa ija mei uqana Anut eu ijaca bilina .
Aria ija ale memela ijana gagadic odoc cunugcana cesuldolig ale dosina .
Euqa ale memela eu qautimei ijana cabi ameg eu ibulabaldu 10 don . Uqa eu odi odocna ija wawi tudocnu odonqa Anut uqa Leban culdeceb ija deweni oso qee me qee mudel .
Uqa odi matecebfi , ‘ Dool cunug dewenega tolotoloca basadein dool eundec hinana cabi amegnu cedadegan , ’ tecebfi dool basadein eundec himec . Uqa odi matecebfi , ‘ Dool cunug dewenega gaga eu made gaga obutibit eu hinana cabi amegnu cedadegan , ’ tecebfi dool basadein eundec himec .
Eunu jic i edina Anut uqa ale memela uqana dool amnadec ija cehewanica miten .
Aria dool agena manag hewec saenna ija saen osona bebelimig meme manahal dewenega tolotoloca dewenega made gaga obutibitca age cufunec eu manag hehewadegin eu feciadem .
Odocob Tibudna ensel bebelecna maten , ‘ Jekob , ’ ten . Odocob ija madom , ‘ Ija i hen , ’ dom .
Odocob uqa maten , ‘ Qila amen suli umeg faga . Meme manahal cunug cufunec manag hewadegina eu dewenega tolotolocafo dewenega made gaga obutibitcafo . Leban uqa hina me qee odihen eu ija wele fem . Eunu ceteh fem eu ija odocomin calen .
Ija Anut hina Betel ono fecitem eu . Betel cudunna hina meen cehimeg mool basecdu qom . Cudun euna hina je cagu matem . Aria cajaga . Maha i culuga . Maha hina anin basihen euna ceseli nuuga , ’ ten , ” alen .
Odocob Resel Liaca ale jejeg hewi madosin , “ Qila ele memile uqana ceteteh oso qee owaun .
Uqa ele cele caja cinigwe mecilena . Uqa ele fajilecna ameg on . Qa eu cunug ji hedon .
Mele bahic , ele memile uqana cehewan cunug Anut cawaldon eu eleca elena talca egenacin . Eunu hina Anut adi maheia eu odi toodu odoga , ” dosin .
Eunu Jekob uqana ceteteh cunug cedadi Kenan nuecnu saciadon . Aria Leban uqa uqana sipsip baginiga jehecnu cabina len . Odocob Resel uqa memegna jo gadan tibud eu heje on . Odocob Jekob uqa aidegulca mel simca cedadimei kamel tatacanna maden . Odimei uqa uqana dool am cunug eu suladeceb aquni belein . Eunu uqa ceteteh cunug Mesopotemia ono bibilei ceden eu cedadimei busali memeg Aisakca Kenan hatuna nuen .


Odonqa Jekob uqa Leban ija busali nuigina ec qee madol . Eunu uqa qaududu busali nuen .
Odimei uqa uqana ceteteh cunug cedadimei caji mahuc busali nui Jufretis wa leten . Odimei uqa ameg leceb Giliad hatu aluhcana isec mecidudu nuen .
Aria deel ijed hedocob Leban uqa Jekob busali nuen ec don .
Odocob Leban uqa cotugul cedeceb age Jekob jabi toodoin . Age deel eben naha gic lecisca eu odi jabi toodu belein . Odimeig age Giliad hatu aluhcana ono mecidoin .
Odocobil witic euna Anut uqa bebelecna Leban madon , “ Batut faga ! Jekob cain geuldoc je madogaun . Ceselecnu ha cain cesusdogaun , ” don .
Saen Leban uqa Jekob mecidocob uqa uqana lotoc talah aluh osona cehi bilen . Odocob Leban uqa cotugul gamiha Giliad hatu aluhca ono lotoc talah cehi bilein .
Odocob Leban uqa Jekob gulucdumei madon , “ Hina eu cel kobol odom ? Hina qautimeg ija ateniel lecis eu han cacadi caja cawaladecwe cedali busalem .
Hina celnu busali hom qa ija qee matelem ? Hina celnu ami hewem ? Hina ija matoummi ija wawi ceelecca due sisili casu qududu ceed fulduduca sulhoum .
Eu odom qa hina culitecem ija ateniel asielca cotaadecemin houbda . Hina gad kobol bahic odom .
Ija hina qihecnu gagadic odoccaqa qila witic hina memenna Anut uqa je edi mateia , ‘ Batut faga ! Jekob cain geuldoc je madogaun . Ceselecnu ha cain cesusdogaun , ’ teia .
Hina memen nui fecnu holimeg busali hom eu ija dugina . Qa hina celnu ijana tibud heje cedadem ? ” don .
Odocob Jekob jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija cucuiem . Hina atenel lecis eu cawaltigaun imig eunu odom .
Euqa hina humeg hina cotinel amagaca ceteteh faga . Euna ceteh oso hinana fifeg hina oga . Odocob in oso hinana tibud eu cedadifei uqa qee cebac biliaun , ” don . Qa Jekob uqa Resel tibud cedaden eu qee dol .
Odocob Leban uqa Jekobna lotoc talah dunuh len . Eunadec Liana talah dunuh len . Eunadec cabi caja lecis alena lotoc talah dunuh len . Qa uqa euna tibud eu qee gulucadel . Odocob uqa Reselna lotoc talah dunuh len .
Aria Resel uqa jo tibud eu cedadimei kamel tatacan bilec cabal uqana jool tacen . Odimei jool euna cilehdu bilen . Odocob Leban uqa ceteh cunug lotoc talah dunuh bilein eu cijawi fen qa tibud eu oso qee gulucdol .
Odocob Resel uqa memeg madon , “ Ijana ben , cain gemain beiaun . Ija jagel qitina . Eunu ija hina cemein caji lec ihoc qee , ” don . Eunu Leban uqa cijawi cuhadon qa uqa uqana gadan tibud eu qee gulucadel .
Odocob Jekob uqa gemag beceb Leban je gagadic madudu madon , “ Ija adi cahuldu odihem eu madaga duga ? Ija cel silail odemnu i edi jabitigina ?
Hina qila ijana ceteteh cunug wele cijawi faga . Cel oso eu hinanacin gulucdoga ? Aria ceteh eu hina cotinelca ijana talca ege amigena fecnu i hen ec magaga . Odocom age ija cahuldomfo qee hina cahuldom fo gesiluqagan .
Ija hinaca cabi gel 20 biloh . Qa hinana sipsipca memeca eu cunug age nag qee basec oso qee nijoloig . Euha hinana sipsip manahal amnadec oso ija qee jelem .
Dool cus oso hinana sipsip oso qocobfi eu ija qee ahuholig qa ija ijanadec oso eu cesuldu iholig . Odocob dool oso witicfo qee cahinegfo heje ocobilfi hina ija ebeninadec ameg ogannu matolog .
Ija eu odi oodi bilolig . Cahineg ija cam cijitoloi . Witic ija duan toloi . Odocob ija us me qee nijolig .
Cabi gel 20 euna ija eu odi oodi hinaca bilolou . Hina atenel lecis eunu ija cabi gel 14 cabi om . Odocob hinana dool am cofadecnu ija cabi gel eben naha gic osahicca cabi om . Odocob hina ijana cabi amegha ibulabaldu 10 dom .
Ija asi Ebrahamca Aisak meica alena Anut ijaca qee biloubmi hina ija ebeni tanac gauc sultecem nuoum . Qa Anut uqa ijana culumenca ija cabi gagadic omca eu fen . Eunu uqa qila witic hina je gagadic maheia , ” don .
Odocob Leban uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Caja lecis eu ale ija ateniel . Alena mel sim euha ijana . Dool am i age euha ijana . Ceteh cunug hina fagana eu ijana himec . Qa qila ija ateniel i aleca alena mel simca eu adi haun cedadigen ?
Eunu qila ija hinaca ele gemo bal cehec je oso madewan . Odocob ele bal cehec je mamadi meen am osolnu qelewan , ” don .
Odocob Jekob uqa meen ben tutuc sosoloig cecelacca oso umei mahana cehen .
Odocob Leban uqa cotugul maadeceb age meen cedi ahumeig haudoin . Odimeig age meen eu cemenug sab jein .
Odocob Leban uqa cudun eu ijan Jega-sahaduta qon . Odocob Jekob uqa cudun eu ijan Galed qon .
Odocob Leban uqa Jekob madon , “ Meen am i qila deel ina hina ijaca ele gemo bal cehec je madowa eu uqana gadac , ” don . Eunu age cudun eu Galed doin .
Odimei madon , “ Saen ele filigandu cocobohul Tibud hina ijaca cofleiale , ” don . Eunu cudun eu ijan osoha Mispa doin .
Odocob Leban madon , “ Hina ija ateniel eu me qee odalegaunfo qee hina caja leih haun cedadeganfo , eufi ija qee mecihigaun qa Anut mecihigian doga .
Faga , meen am ica meen tutuc tawec ica ija hinaca ele gemo cehowa ene nijia .
Meen am ica meen tutuc tawec ica eu cadnu gaga cudun biligian . Ija meen am i qee wooldumig hagen ono isec hina qihecnu ligaun . Eu odiwe hinaha meen am ica meen tutuc tawec ica qee wooldumeg hagen ene isec ija qitecnu hogaun .
Ebraham Nehoca alena Anut uqa ele gemo gesilligian , ” don . Odocob Jekob uqa Anut uqa memeg Aisak cucuidona eu amegna Leban je maden eu cunug toodu odigen imei je cagu maden .
Odocob Jekob uqa aluhna dool oso qumei Anut ihandon . Odimei uqa cotugul maadeceb sab jecna lecebil sab jein . Odimeig age witic euna aluhna ono us nijein .
Odocobil qasil bahic Leban uqa cajimei uqa asagul simsimca uqa ategul lecis euca cotaaadi bilei eeldoc je aden . Odimei uqa culadimei ceseli uqana jobon nuen .
Odocob Jekob uqaha uqana jicna nuen . Nunui bili ensel age uqa gulucdoin .
Saen Jekob uqa meciadimei maden , “ I eu Anutna cudun , ” en . Eunu uqa cudun eu ijan Mahanaim qon .
Odocob Jekob uqa dana leih sos suladeceb age uqa waliag Isoca belein . Iso uqa Sia agena mahana bilen . Sia eu Idom hatuna nijen .
Qa casac Jekob uqa sos maaden , “ Age ijana ben Iso je edi madoqagan , ‘ Hinana cabi dana Jekob odi madena , ‘ Ija Lebanca bilolounu qila ceseligina .
Ija bulmakau amca cesel amca sipsip amca meme amca cabi danaca cabi cajaca hoqona . Qila ija je i hina sulduhigina . Hina ijanu wawin me nijigian nu , ’ ec madena , ’ age je i madigina eu odi madoigale , ” aden .
Odocob Jekob uqana sos ceseli hu madoin , “ Ege hina walin Isoca loqa . Odeiaqa uqa hona . Dana 400 eu odi uqaca hogina , ” doin .
Odocob Jekob geh bahic cucuii jaen qon . Eunu Jekob uqa uqana dana cajaca dool amca eu qatanadimei am lecisna maden .
Iso uqa humei han sanan mecebfi am oso eu age busali beloqagan ec odi cisdon .
Odocob Jekob uqa odi inondu madon , “ O ija asi Ebrahamca ija mei Aisakca alena Anut , O Tibud , hina dah mitiga . Hina matem , ‘ Hina ceseli hinana hatunaca hina cotinelca nuuga . Odocom ija odocna hina cehewainca calegan , ’ tem .
Ija hinana cabi dana . Hina hinana kobol me bahic eu ihactem . Hina ijanu cisdom . Qa ija ihoc qee . Weleca ija gotutca himec Jodan wa i letem . Qa qila ija am lecis ica ceseli huga .
Ija wali Iso ebennadec cahahataga . Ija cucuiigina . Uqa humei han sulimei ijaca ijana tal eu qee migigian . Eunu ija cucuiigina .
Qa hina matem , ‘ Ija mele bahic odihecemin hina cehewainca megan . Odocob hinana sihul eu lannadec cesic cinigwe caloqagan . Euqa sicanecwe qee eu odi caloqagan , ’ tem , ” uqa eu odi inondon .
Odimei uqa witic ono us nijen . Odocob uqa waliag Iso loo utigiannu dool leih uqana amnadec nesili cedaden .
Dool cedaden eu i edi . Meme cufunec 200 , meme manahal 20 , sipsip cufunec 200 , sipsip manahal 20 ,
kamel cufunec su ogina eundec 30 agena nagca , bulmakau cufunec 40 , bulmakau manahal 10 , cesel cufunec 20 , cesel manahal 10 .
Odocob uqa dool eu qatanadi am naha maden . Odimei uqa dool am eu age uqana cabi dana ebenegana men . Uqa dool am gug fil eu cabi dana oso ebenna men . Odocob dool am gug fil eu cabi dana oso ebenna men . Uqa dool am gug filfil cabi dana osahicosahic ebenegana men . Odimei uqa maaden , “ Age casac aquni beleiga . Age cain gabandu belowain . Oso nueceb oso toodoia qa big togoctogoc cain belowain , ” aden .
Odocob uqa cabi dana aquni nugian eu madon , “ Saen ija wali Iso uqa guluchimei sisilhecebfi , ‘ Hinana ben eu indec ? Dool i age indecna ? Odeiaqa hina ana nuuguna ? ’ uqa odi sisilhecebfi ,
hina edi madegan , ‘ Dool i age hinana cabi dana Jekobnacin . Euqa uqana ben Isonu loo suldoia . Odeiaqa Jekob uqadodoc hib hona , ’ hina odi madegan , ” don .
Odocob cabi dana leih aquni nuen eu toodoin eu age cunug je eu odi himec madoqagannu maaden , “ Age Iso gulucdodoig je cabi dana aquni nuigiannu maduga eu ageha eu odi madoiga .
Qa je i madocnu dahanaga cain celeiaun . ‘ Hinana cabi dana Jekob uqa hib toogena , ’ doiga , ” aden . Jekob uqa cisdon , “ Ija dool lonu aquni suldugina i uqa waug me nijigian . Odocob hibna uqa gulucdocomin uqa ija me meciitigian , ” ec cisdon .
Eunu Jekob dool waliagna lonu suldon eu casac cedi hewi belein . Qa uqa witic euna cudun euna himec us nijen .
Aria uqa witic euna dih Jekob uqa cajimei aidegul lecisca cabi caja lecisca uqana mel 11ca cedadimei suladeceb Jabok wa letein .
Uqana tal suladeceb letecebil uqana ceteteh cunug hib cabi dana suladeceb cedi ehi lein .
Odimei Jekob uqa cuhanuc ono bilen . Odocob dana oso hocob uqaca hewecebheweceb imesi hahagalesin li cojagen .
Hahagali bilesi dana eu Jekob wooldocnu ihoc qee fimei uqa Jekob cataic tudocob cataic teful falicdon .
Odocob dana eu madon , “ Wele cojagena . Culitecem nuiga , ” don . Qa Jekob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija qee culihecemin nuugaun . Euqa eeltecemfi ija culihigen , ” don .
Odocob dana uqa Jekob sisildon , “ Hina ijain indec ? ” don . Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Jekob , ” don .
Odocob uqa Jekob madon , “ Hina ijain haun Jekob qee howain . Hina Anutca hagalimesi dana cunug wooladaga . Eunu age Isrel hoqagan , ” don .
Odocob Jekob uqa sisildudu madon , “ Hina ijain mataga , ” don . Qa uqa madon , “ Hina celnu ijaninu sisiligana ? ” don . Oodoi uqa ono Jekob eeldon .
Odocob Jekob uqa maden , “ Ija Anut ola figaqa ija qee cal melem , ” en . Eunu Jekob cudun eu ijan Peniel qon .
Aria qasil cam tobi beben uqa Peniel cudun eu culimei len . Euqa uqa cataicnu citogohui cobon .
Aria dana eu uqa Jekob cataic teful eu hiliman tudon . Eunu qila saen ina Isrel dana caja age dool hiliman cataic amegnadec eu qee jegina .
Aria odocob Jekob uqa ameg suli u meciimei Iso dana 400 uqaca hohogin feciaden . Odocob uqa uqana mel sim Liaca Reselca cabi caja lecisca age qatanadi am ijedna maden .
Odimei uqa cabi caja lecis ale alena mel gami aquni maden . Odimei Lia uqa uqana mel gami age gemo maden . Odimei uqa Resel Josefca ale hib malen .
Odocob uqa uqadodoc wooladimei uqa aquni nuen . Odimei uqa waliag dodoldodoi jogoi eben naha gic lecisca don .
Oodon Iso uqa guguli humei Jekob gulucdon . Gulucdumei uqa cogadudu bili cotadon . Odocob ale qajesin .
Odocob Iso uqa ameg suli umei cajaca mel simca meciaden . Odimei sisildon , “ I indec ni hinaca hogina ? ” don . Jekob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ O ijana ben , Anut me bahic eeltiti mel sim i age iten , ” don .
Odocob cabi caja ale alena mel sim gami humeig Iso amegna jogoein .
Odocob Lia uqana mel sim gami humeig Iso amegna jogoein . Odocob Resel Josefca ale humesi Iso amegna jogoesin .
Oodogin Iso uqa sisildon , “ Dool am huhu bilig gulucadiga eu cel gugnu ? ” don . Odocob Jekob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Euqa ijana ben hina wawin me mudecnu faga , ” don .
Qa Iso madon , “ O wali ija ceteteh geh bahicca . Ceteteh hinana eu cois hinanacin biligian , ” don .
Odocob Jekob madon , “ Qee , qila hina ijanu wawin me nijecebfi ceteteh loo ihiga i ebeninadec cedega . Qila hina wawin ceelecna guluctaga . Eunu hina olain figina eu Anut ola fecwe migina .
Anut uqa ija me eelten . Odocob ija ceteteh ihoc . Eunu ceteteh hina loo ihigina eu cedega , ” don . Odimei Jekob uqa cesusdudu li uqa ceteteh loo uten eu cediton .
Odocob Iso madon , “ Cois ege belecnu . Ija aquni nunuemin age hib tooteiga , ” don .
Odocob Jekob madon , “ O ijana ben , ijana mel sim age gagadicca qee hina dogona . Euha sipsip bulmakauca cufunec eu agena nagca eu ija cofadigen ec cisdugina . Age gagadic deel osahicna cobifeig age cunug cal moqagan .
Eunu hina casac aquni nunuem ijaca ijana dool amca ijana simca ege cebitnana hib tooheqan . Ija agena jic lec eu age buluaadi toohi Sia ono guluchigen , ” don .
Odocob Iso madon , “ Cois ija ijana dana leih hinaca culadigen , ” don . Qa Jekob madon , “ Odi cain odagaun . Hina me mitiga eu ihoc , ” don .
Eunu deel euna himec Iso ceseli Sia nuecnu uqa coboc sanan men .
Qa Jekob uqa Sakot isec nuen . Ono uqa uqana jo oso cehen . Odimei uqa dool agena jo ha cehen . Eunu cudun eu ijan Sakot egina .
Aria Jekob uqa Mesopotemiadec humei uqa Sekem taun ono culumenca qee me bahic calen . Sekem eu Kenan hatuna nijia . Uqa taun fecnu ihocna cudun oso hewimei lotoc talah cehi bilen .
Uqa lotoc talah cehenna maha eu 100 silwana faji on . Uqa Hamo melahul ebeneganadec faji on . Hamo uqa Sekem memeg .
Ono uqa ihanec cabal gualimei ijan El qon . “ El ” eu Isrelna Anut uqa ijan .
Aria saen osona Daina , Lia ateg uqa Jekob basiton eu , Kenandec caja feciadecnu nuen .
Aria Hamo , uqa Hiwi dana , uqa maha eu agena ilo bilen . Odocob uqa melah Sekem Daina cocobon fimei uqa caluwandu ehi li hehewen nijesin .
Uqa waug eu Dainanu cal men . Odocob uqanu nalug mimei je bodoecna isec madon .
Odocob Sekem uqa memeg Hamo madon , “ Mel aid haun i ijana cajanu u taga , ” don .
Aria Jekob uqa dana eu uqa ateg Daina me qee mudia ec don . Saen euna uqa melahul age cabina bulmakau cofaadegin je eu don . Eunu uqa je oso qee maadec bibilen age hoin .
Odocob Sekem memeg Hamo uqa Jekob je madugia bili uqa hon .
Ale je mamadesin Jekob melahul age cabinadec ceseli hoin . Odocob age Sekem uqa Jekob ateg heweceb nijesin eu Isrel amagana majanaga hewec kobol odon eu dumeig age filicitimeig gemanaga ben . Kobol eu Isrelna sihul gemo odocnu qee nijel eu odon .
Qa Hamo uqa Jekob madon , “ Ija melami waug eu hina atennu nijia . Hina ocobocob owasannu utuga .
Age ege gami ocobocob eqan . Age atagail ege igeiga . Odimeig ege atigeil age cedadeiga .
Eufi age ege gemo biluqagan . Odocobil maha eu age bilecnu jeca qee . Odocob age ene idadecnuca maha ocnuca ihoc , ” don .
Odocob Sekem uqa Daina memegca cebinagulca maaden , “ Age ijanu wawaga me nijecebfi cel ceteh osonu sisiltoqagaqa eu ija adigen .
Caja fajec ameg ganic mateiga ? Eeta gale adena eu ija adigen . Eu ameg ben bahicfi euha ija fajigen . Qa caja eu iteiga , ” aden .
Aria Sekem uqa Jekob melahul age cebinamaga Daina me qee muden . Eunu age gami qauecna isec Sekem memegca je wadacdu maalein .
Odocob age maalein , “ Ege cebinamige dana oso deweg gaga qee qoc ocnu eu ihoc qee . Eu egena kobol qee . Eufi ege majanige gecna isec odocnu .
Ege jic osahicna himec hina cois hecnu . Jic eu odi . Hinana dana cunug age dewenega gaga qoqagan . Eufi age ege cinigwe caloqagan .
Eu odi odocobilfi ege atigeil eu age adocomun age atagail eu ege iguqagan . Odocobil ege ageca bilecnu . Odimeb dana sihul osahic calecnu .
Qa age dewenega gaga qocnu maadoqa eu qee dah migifeig euqa ege cebinamige eu umeb nuecnu , ” alein .
Hamo melah Sekemca je eu dah mesin eu me bahic .
Odocob uqa Jekob ategnu waug ceelen . Eunu dana haun eu cabi eu odocnu qee daleel . Hamo uqana talna uqa dana ben , uqa binanca biloloi .
Odocob Sekem uqa memeg Hamoca taun uqana gel cebecna humesi dana taunnadec je maadi madesin ,
“ Dana i age egena danah . Eunu culadecebil maha ina idadi biluqagan . Maha i eu ben bahic ihoc . Ege age atagail cedadimeb ocobocob ecnu . Odimeb ege atigeil eu age adecnu .
Euqa age gami bilecnuca dana sihul osahic calecnuca jic osahicna himec odi odocnu cois goqagan . Jic eu odi . Dana cunug ege gemo bilegina eu dana i age cinigwe caloqagan euqa age cunug dewenega gaga qoqagan .
Odocob agena dool cunugca ceteteh cunugca egena qee biliaunfo ? Eunu ege cois adocomun age egeca bileqan , ” esin .
Eunu dana cunug taun gel cebecna lein eu age Hamo melah Sekemca alena je dah mein . Odocobil dana cunug age saen euna dewenega gaga qoin .
Aria deel ijed hedocob saen eu age dain aden ninijegin Jekob melahul lecis , Simion Liwaica , ale Daina cebinagul , ale han cadec sigin cedimesi taun euna hosin . Taun eunadec dana qee dodogin humesi cunug aqecebil cal mein .
Ale Hamo melah Sekemca siginna aqecebil cal mesin . Odimesi Daina Sekemna jonadec ehudi belesin .
Odocobil Jekob melahul cunug age humeig dana cal mein ninijegin taun eu dunuhna ceteteh cunug gogoqi heje cedi ehi nuein . Dana taun eunadec age Jekob melahul cebinamaga me qee mudein , eunu odi odoin .
Odimeig age agena sipsip amca bulmakau amca cesel amca ceteteh cunug agena taun bilein euca cabina bilein euca cunug cedein .
Age cehewanaga cunugca agena cajaca agena mel simca cunug cedimeig belein . Ceteteh cunug jona nijen euha cunug cedein .
Odocob Jekob uqa Simion Liwaica maalen , “ Ale ija deweni jeca mudesia . Ale odocobil dana Kenandec Peresdecca dana cunug maha inadec age ija agena cadwe doqagan . Ege dana matica qee . Age gabandumeig ijaca han sulecebilfi ijaca ijana talca ege qee mecnu , ” alen .
Qa ale madosin , “ Uqa ele cebinamile jicnadec wal caja cinigwe odudecnu ihocfo ? ” dosin .
Odocob Anut uqa Jekob madon , “ Aria cajimeg Betel ono taga . Odimeg ono biliga . Ija Anut eu saen hina walin Iso cemenugnadec bubusalegan uqa hinaca camasac men . Eunu Betel ono hina ihanec meen cabal gualimeg ihantaga , ” don .
Eunu Jekob uqa uqana talca dana caja cunug uqaca bilein eu maaden , “ Cele agena tibud ageca bileiga , eu cunug qeladeiga . Odimeig dewenega eeldumeig lotoc haun tacadeiga .
Odocob hoiga . Ege Betel ono tecnu . Ono ija Anut ihanec cabal oso gualimig ihandugen . Ija anaana cocobilig saen ija culumenca bibilig Anut je madocomin uqa dah mitoloi , ” aden .
Eunu age cele agena tibud agena bilein eu cunug Jekob utein . Odocob dahof age dahinigana tacein euha utein . Odocob Jekob uqa ceteteh eu cedimei Sekem cemenug na ben gugna hel cisaden .
Odocob age bebelegin Anut uqa odocob cucuiec ben oso dana caja taun age aliladi bileinna nen . Odocob age qee tooadelein .
Odocob Jekob uqaca dana caja uqaca belein eu age hu Lus calein . Lus qila eu ijan eu Betel . Eu Kenan mahana .
Odocob uqa cudun euna ihanec cabal oso gualen . Saen uqa waliag Iso cemenugnadec bubusalen Anut uqa ono uqaca camasac men . Eunu cudun eu ijan Betel qon .
Odocob Rebekana cabi caja Debora cal men . Odocob uqa na ben gugna Betel bisalu hel cisein . Eunu cudun eu ijan Qajec Na Ben qoin .
Aria saen Jekob Mesopotemiadec ceseleceb Anut uqaca haun camasac mimei eeldon .
Odimei Anut uqa madon , “ Hina ijain eu Jekob qa hina haun Jekob qee howain . Hina ijain eu Isrel hoqagan , ” don . Eunu Anut uqa ijan Isrel qon .
Odocob Anut uqa je oso ha edi madon , “ Ija Anut Gagadic Bahic . Sihul fulusdumeg mati bahic caloqagan . Ija odihecemin hinana sihul ben oso caligian . Sihulna ilo bilec mati bahic age hinana sihulnadec caloqagan .
Maha ija Ebraham Aisakca alem eu hina ihigen . Odocob hinana sihul hina toohec hibna cali hoqagan euha maha eu adigen , ” don .
Odocob Anut cudun uqa je madon eu culimei sao ohis ti nuen .
Odocob Jekob cudun uqa Anutca je madesin euna meen cecelac oso umei tutuc cehen . Odimei uqa Anut ihandocwe wain meen eu basecdu qon . Eu hedocob uqa meen eu moolha basecdu qon .
Odimei uqa cudun eu ijan Betel qon .
Odocob age Betel culimeig belein . Saen age Efrat qee calec ninijen Resel uqa mel basecnu dain doc sanan men qa uqa ihoc bahic qee .
Uqa dain ben dodon Resel uqana cesuldoc caja eu madon , “ Cain cucuiagaun , Resel . Hina qila mel manahal oso basegan , ” don .
Qa uqa cal migia dodoldodon kis u bilei melah eu ijan Benoni qon . Euqa memeg uqa Benjamin don .
Resel cal meceb uqa jic Efrat nuec eu gesacna hel cisein . Cudun eu qila Betlehem egina .
Odocob Jekob meen oso euna uqana qalqal gadac mec cehen . Euqa qila saen inaha bilia .
Odocob Jekob uqa cocobi nuimei Ede agena han qali jo hagen naha isec uqana lotoc talah cehen .
Odocob Jekob uqa ono maha euna bibilen Ruben uqa limei memegna cabi caja aideg cinigwe biloloi eu Bilhaca uqaca nijesin . Odocob Jekob uqa eu don . Aria Jekob uqa melahul cunug gabandoc eu 12 .
Melahul Lianadec eu ijanaga Ruben , Simion , Liwai , Juda , Isaka , Sebjulanca . Ruben uqa Jekobna mel matu .
Melahul Reselnadec eu ijanala Josef Benjaminca .
Melahul Resel uqana cabi caja Bilhanadec eu ijanala Dan Naftalica .
Melahul Lia uqana cabi caja Silpanadec eu ijanala Gad Aseca . Melahul i age Mesopotemia ono Jekob basaditoin .
Odocob Jekob uqa memeg Aisakca Mamri ono nuen . Mamri eu Hebron cemenug . Cudun euna Ebraham Aisakca bilesin .
Aria Aisak uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 180 .
Odocob Aisak uqa dana toia bahic uqa kis umei cal men . Uqana cabi gel eu mati bahic . Odocob uqa melahul Iso Jekobca ale deweg hel cisesin .
I eu Isona je . Iso ijan oso eu Idom .
Iso uqa caja Kenandec cedaden . Eu ijanaga Ada , Oholibama , Basematca . Ada uqa Elon ateg , uqa Het dana . Oholibama uqa Ana ateg . Ana memeg eu Sibion , uqa Hiwi dana . Basemat uqa Ismal ateg , uqa cebinag eu Nebaiot .

Odocob Ada uqa Iso Elifas basiton . Odocob Basemat uqa Iso Reuel basiton .
Odocob Oholibama uqa Iso Jeus , Jalam , Koraca basaditon . Mel i age eu Iso melahul , age Kenan ono basaditoin .
Odocob Iso uqa aidegulca uqana mel simca uqana cabi danaca dool manan amca cehewanca Kenan ono bibili ceden eu cunug cedimei waliag Jekob cemenugdec qisacdu fil aluhna Sia ono nuen .
Alena cehewanala eu ben bahic . Alena dool am eu ben bahic . Eunu ale gabandu bilecwe qee . Maha ale osoben bilesin eu ale lecisnu ihoc qee .
Eunu Iso uqa Sia maha aluhca ono bilen .
Iso uqa Idom sihul eundec agena memega calen . Iso uqana sihul age Sia maha aluhca ono bilein .
Aria Iso aideg Ada uqa Iso mel osahic basiton , ijan eu Elifas . Odocob Elifas aideg oso uqa mel ebum oso basaden . Ijanaga eu Teman , Oma , Jefo , Gatam , Kenasca . Odocob Elifas aideg oso , ijan Timna , uqa mel osahic basen , ijan eu Amalek . Aria Iso aideg Basemat uqa mel osahic basen , ijan eu Reuel . Reuel aideg uqa mel wal oso basaden . Ijanaga eu Nahat , Sera , Sama , Misaca .



Aria Iso aideg Oholibama , eu Ana ateg , eu Sibion asag , uqa Iso mel ijed basaditon . Ijanaga eu Jeus , Jalam , Koraca .

Kora , Gatam , Amalekca . Eu age Elifas aideg Ada asagul .
Aria Iso melah Reuel uqa sihul i edi agena ilo bilen . Nahat , Sera , Sama , Misaca . Eu age Iso aideg Basemat asagul .
Aria Iso aideg Oholibama , Ana ateg , uqa sihul i edi agena ilo bilen . Jeus , Jalam , Koraca .
Iso uqa sihul cunug agena ilo bilen .
Sia dana age casac Idom bilein , age Ho sihulnadec . Sia melahul age Idom bilein eu Lotan , Sobal , Sibeon , Ana , Dison , Ese , Disanca . Sia uqa Ho sihul agena ilo bilen .

Odocob Lotan melahul eu Hori Hemanca . Timna uqa Lotan cebinag .
Odocob Sobal melahul eu Alwan , Manahat , Ebal , Sefo , Onamca .
Odocob Sibeon melahul eu Aia Anaca . Ana i maha wadauna saen uqa memeg Sibionna cesel cofaadi bilei uqa wa fifiji bec dainca gulucdon .
Odocob Ana melah eu Dison . Ana ateg eu Oholibama .
Odocob Dison melahul eu Hemdan , Esban , Itran , Keranca .
Odocob Ese melahul eu Bilhan , Sawan , Akanca .
Odocob Disan melahul eu Us Aranca .
Aria Ho sihulnadec ilo dana eu Lotan , Sobal , Sibeon , Ana ,
Dison , Ese , Disanca . Eu age Sia mahana agena jobon medeh filfilna ilo dana bilein .
Aria Isrel agena ilo dana qee bilec saenna Idom hatu euna ilo dana age hatu eunu ilo bilein . Age toodocobtoodocob bibilegin nuon .

Aria Husam cal meceb Hadad , uqa Bedad melah , uqa uqana cudun umei hatu ilo dana bilen . Bedad uqa Midian dana eu aqen , eu Moab hatuna . Hadad uqana taun eu Awit .

Aria Iso uqa Idom sihul cunug agena ilo bilen , uqa Idom asag . Idom agena sihul age jobon medeh filfil bilein . Ijanaga eu Timna , Alwa , Jetet , Oholibama , Ela , Pinon , Kenas , Teman , Mibsa , Magdiel , Iramca .



Aria Jekob uqa maha memeg bilenna eu Kenan ono bilen .
Jekobna je eu odi . Aria Josef uqa mel haun uqana cabi gel 17 saen euna uqa waliagul , eu Jekob aidegul lecis Bilha Silpaca melemegail , gami dool cofadein . Qa Josef uqa waliagul kobol me qee leih odoin eu hu memeg sadon .
Aria Jekob uqa toia bibilen Josef uqa cali hon . Eunu uqa Josefnu ben bahic nalug men . Odocob memeg uqa lotoc deweg cunug jahuldocnu gaga mati bahicca muditon .
Odocob Josef waliagul age memega Josefnu nalug ben bahic men eu fimeig age uqanu gemanaga ben . Eunu age je me bahic madocnu eu wawaga qee nijoloi .
Aria witic osona Josef uqa bebelen . Odocob bebelec eu uqa waliagul saadeceb age uqanu gemanaga ben bahic ben .
Uqa maaden , “ Bebelec ija bebeliga i dah meiga .
Ege wit gug cabina sog cecedoqon ijana sog eu caji tutuc taweia . Odocob agena sog eu ijana eu talildu tawimeig ijana sog amegna jogoeiga , ” aden .
Odocob waliagul age madoin , “ Hina egena ilo bileganfo ? Hina egena cofgec bileganfo ? ” doin . Eu odi maadeceb casac gemanaga ben eu wooldoc gemanaga ben .
Odocob Josef uqa bebelec osoha bebelen eu saaden , “ Dah meiga . Ija bebelec osoha bebelem eu odi , camca jagelca malaqa 11ca age ija amina jogoeiga , ” aden .
Odocob uqa bebelec eu uqa memegha sadon . Odocob memeg uqa galac mumudi madon , “ Eu cel bebelec bahic ? Ijaca hina aninca hina walinelca ege mele bahic hinaca humeb hina amenna jogoecnufo ? ” don .
Odon waliagul age uqanu gonagona mein . Qa memeg eu je maden eu cunug uqana cisdocna men .
Aria Josef waliagul age memegana dool am cofadoqaga bili Sekem ono belein .
Odocob Jekob uqa Josef madon , “ Hina walinel age Sekem ono dool am cofadegina . Ija sulhecemin nuegan , ” don . Odocob Josef madon , “ Cois , eu ihoc , ” don .
Odocob Jekob uqa madon , “ Hina nuimeg walinel dool amca me bileigafo feciadegan . Odimeg ceseli hu mataga , ” don . Eunu uqa Josef suldocob Hebron maha asounadec Sekem ono nuen . Nuimei Sekem calen .
Odocob uqa ono cabina calimei wawaladi cocobon dana oso gulucdumei sisildon , “ Hina celnu fecii cobogona ? ” don .
Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija walielnu feciigina . Ana dool am cofadegina eu hina matecnu ihocfo ? ” don .
Odocob dana eu madon , “ Age enedec wele beleiga . Age odi mamadegin duga , ‘ Gec , ege Dotan beloqa , ’ eegin duga , ” don . Eunu Josef uqa waliagul tooadi nuimei Dotan ono gulucaden .
Qa uqa filec hohon fimeig age cemenega qee lec ninijen age qocobil cal migiannu je madi cagoin .
Odocob age madocobmadocob ein , “ Bebelec dana i hec hona .
Gec hoiga , ege qagadumeb wa hel maha dunuh qelecnu . Odimeb ege madecnu , ‘ Dool hanca oso qu jeia , ’ ecnu . Odocob uqana bebelec eu mele caligianfo qeefo ege fecnu , ” ein .
Qa Ruben uqa je eu dah mimei uqa Josef cal mecnadec cahahadon . Odocob uqa maaden , “ Ege uqa cain qocomun cal meiaun .
Ege uqa golac cain basecdoqaun . Wa hel wadauna nijia ina helocomun nugian . Qa uqa deweg oso cain tudowain , ” aden . Ruben uqa je eu odi maaden eu uqa waliag cal mecnadec cahahadumei ceseli memegca ehudi ligiannu ec cisdon .
Eunu Josef uqa waliagul cemenega leceb uqana lotoc gaga mati bahic eu hulitumeig
ehudi li wa helna helecebil non . Aria wa hel euna waca qee , eu galalec nijen .
Odocob age sab joqaga bili bibilegin dana Ismal sihuldec age Giliaddec agena kamel mati bahic big togoctogoc hohogin feciadein . Agena kamel euna sabca cilecebil tinca mecnu euca gilic dedemanca ceteteh eundec gahidu age Isip noin .
Odocob Juda uqa waliagul maaden , “ Ege walinige qagadumeb je jahunifeb ege eunadec cel ameg oso ocnu ?
Gec hoiga , ege uqa Ismal dana ebenegana idadocnu . Qa ege uqa deweg oso cain tudoqaun . Naha , uqa ege walinige ege golanige osol , ” aden . Odocob Juda waliagul age je eu dah mimeig eu odi odocnu ein .
Odocob Midiandec idadec dana age cemenega hohogin Josef waliagul age Josef helnadec didocobil cali ben . Odocob age Josef Ismal ebenegana mimi meen qaig silwa 20 oin . Odocobil Ismal dana Josef ehudi Isip noin .
Saen leih leceb Ruben haun ceseli Josef figiannu wa helna len qa Josef uqa ono qee bilel . Eunu uqa uqana lotoc baladon .
Odimei uqa waliagul ceseli nui maaden , “ Mel eu ono qee bilel . Qila ija adi odigen ? ” aden .
Eunu Josefna lotoc umeig meme oso qocobil cal meceb uqana golac euna age Josefna lotoc eu cumdoiga .
Odocobil age lotoc gaga mati eu umeig memegaca ehi belein . Odimeig madoin , “ Ege lotoc gulucdoqa . Faga , eu hina melem uqana lotocfo qeefo ? ” doin .
Odocob eu fimei uqa maden , “ O ija melami uqana lotoc . Dool cus oso uqa jeudia . Mele bahic Josef tatali calcaldoia , ” en .
Eunu Jekob uqa uqana lotoc baladon . Odimei uqa gehel lotoc u tacen . Odimei uqa melahnu deel mati bahic qada qaqaji bilen .
Uqa qaqajen melahul ategulca age wahohogdoqagannu caji uqaca lein . Qa age wahohogdocnu eu culen . Odocob uqa maaden , “ Mele bahic ijana qada qajecna himec ija melamica helna nugen , ” aden . Eunu memeg uqanu qaqaji bilen .
Oodon Midian dana age Josef Isip ono ehudi numeig Potifaca idadoin . Potifa uqa Ferona han dana agena ilo .
Aria saen euna Juda uqa waliagul culadimei Adulam ono non . Uqa dana oso , ijan Hiraca , biluwasannu non .
Ono Juda uqa Kenandec caja oso fen . Uqa memeg ijan eu Sua . Odocob uqa caja eu ocob uqaca nijesin .
Odocobil uqa melca mimei mel oso baseceb Juda ijan Er qon .
Odocob uqa haun melca mimei mel oso baseceb uqa ijan Onan qon .
Odocob uqa haun mel oso baseceb uqa ijan Sela qon . Sela uqa Kesib ono basiton .
Odocob Juda uqa melah matu , Er , uqana caja uton . Caja uqa ijan Tema .
Qa Er , Judana mel matu , uqa Tibud amegna eu qisol dana . Eunu Tibud uqa qagadocob uqa cal men .
Odocob Juda uqa Onan madon , “ Hina walin aidegca lecem nijesia . Kobol i eu odi . Hina walin uqa melca qee . Eunu hina walin aideg ocom mel basigian eu hina walin ijan qumeg uqana sihul calitugiannu , ” don .
Qa Onan mel cali hoqagan eu uqana qee eu uqa don . Eunu saen uqa waliag aidegca niniji olosi eu uqa uqana hinih eu gauc mahana basecdoloi . Euqa uqa waliag aideg mel cain baseiaunnu odoloi .
Uqa kobol odon eu Tibud amegna qisol kobol bahic . Eunu Tibud uqa qagadocob uqaha cal men .
Odocob Juda uqa cisdon , “ Sela uqa Er aideg , Tema , aidegnu ocobfi uqa waliagul cal mesin eu odi cal mec dain , ” en . Eunu Juda uqa Tema madon , “ Hina memenca uqana jona ceseli nuuga . Ono caja wij bibilem li ija melami Sela uqa ben migian , ” don . Odocob Tema uqa memegna jona biligiannu nuen .

uqa caja wij agena lotoc eu hulimei caja oso ola ugia bili lotoc nag osona ola jahuldon . Odimei uqa li Enaim gel cebecna bilen . Euqa Timna jic nuecna . Aria Juda melah Sela uqa wele ben men Tema uqa don qa Sela uqa Tema qee ol . Eunu uqa odi odon .
Odocob Juda uqa humei Tema fecidodon uqa ola jahuldon . Eunu caja eu uqa wal caja ec cisdon .
Juda uqa caja eu uqa melah aideg ec qee dol . Eunu uqa uqaca jic gesacna limei madon , “ Hoga , ijaca nijuwa , ” don . Odocob uqa sisildon , “ Hinaca nijifeu hina eeta itegan ? ” don .
Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija meme nag oso ijana amnadec sulduhigen , ” don . Odocob caja uqa madon , “ Euqa cois . Hina qilaqa ceteh oso hina je cagu madaga meme nag oso itegan aga eu uqana gadac cinigwe itiga , ” don .
Odocob uqa sisildon , “ Cel oso gadac cinigwe ihigen ? ” don . Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Hinana golegoleca ijain gaga mudec cetehca hinana gom hewegena euca itadegan , ” don . Eunu uqa ceteteh eu utadeceb uqaca nijesin . Odocob uqa hibna melca men .
Aria Tema uqa Juda culdi limei uqa lotoc ola jahuldon eu cagasi umei caja wij agena lotoc euna haun bala falen .
Odocob Juda uqa limei uqana ceteteh caja uten eu cedigiannu uqana danah Hira uqa meme nagca suldon . Qa uqana danah uqa caja eu qee gulucdol .
Odocob Judana danah eu dana ono bilegina eu sisiladen , “ Wal caja uqa Enaim jic gesacna bilia eu ana bilia ? ” aden . Qa age madoin , “ Wal caja oso ene qee bilinanu , ” doin .
Eunu uqa ceseli Judaca limei madon , “ Ija uqa qee gulucdolom . Euha dana ono bilegina age mateiga , ‘ Wal caja oso ono qee bilinanu , ’ teiga , ” don .
Odocob Juda madon , “ Ceteteh uqa ceden eu hawadoga uqa cois cedeia . Ele ceteteh eu cedecnu haun sisilocohulfi age asalloqagan . Ija meme nag fajudocnu suldugaqa hina qee gulucdolom , ” don .
Aria jagel ijed eu odi hedocob dana oso uqa Juda madon , “ Hina melem aideg , Tema , uqa wal cajawe odoloi . Odocob qila uqa melca men , ” don . Odocob Juda uqa maaden , “ Ehudi ahoiga . Jana manecebil ja cijeceb cal meia , ” aden .
Age ehudi aahogin Tema uqa Judaca je suldudu madon , “ Ceteteh i faga . Dana ija melca miten uqanacin . Gole goleca ijan gaga mudec cetehca gomca faga . Eu inna ? ” don .
Odocob Juda ceteteh eu feciadimei uqana eu don . Uqa maaden , “ Uqa caja ititom bahic . Uqa ija wooltec . Ija melami Sela aidegnu utoum qa qee utelem , ” aden . Odocob uqa haun Temaca qee nijelesin .
Aria Temana mel sim basec saen dodoldodon mel gahca ale waugna ninijesin tebandon .
Odocob uqa mel babasen mel momodo oso eben men . Eunu caja cesuldoin eundec oso uqa golac haluna eben eu qagen . Odimei uqa maden , “ I uqa casac cali hoia , ” en .
Qa uqa eben ceseli ocob uqa waliag cali hon . Odocob uqa maden , “ Hina batawi cali hoga eu odi , ” en . Eunu uqa ijan Peres qon .
Odocob uqa waliag ebenna golac halu eu cali hocob ijan Sera qoin .
Aria Ismal sihuldec dana age Josef ehudi Isip noin . Odocob Potifa uqa Josef Ismal dana ebeneganadec fajudi on . Potifa uqa Isipdec dana ben . Uqa Farona han dana am oso age Ferona jo cofdocnu uqa eu agena ilo .
Odocob Tibud Josefca bilen . Eunu uqa uqana cabi eu cunug me bahic calen . Uqa uqana ben Isipdec eu uqana jona bilen .
Odocob uqana ben Tibud uqa Josefca bilen eu fen . Uqana cabi uqa amegna calen eu me bahic himec euha fen .
Eunu uqana ben uqa Josefnu waug nijen . Odocob uqa Josef uqana cabi dana matu mudon . Odimei uqa uqana joca uqana ceteteh cunugca cofdocnu cabi uten .
Saen eunadec nueceb Tibud Josefnu Potifana ceteteh cunug jona bileiga euca eeldon . Josef uqa jo euna bilen . Eunu Tibud uqa ceteteh cunug jonaca cabinaca eeldon .
Odocob Potifa uqa ceteteh cunug uqana eu Josef ebenna men . Uqa ceteteh cunug cofdocnu qee cisdol . Qa sab jecnu himec eu uqa cofdon . Aria Josef uqa ola eu fecnu galeca . Uqa dewegha fecnu galeca .
Odocob saen leih leceb uqana ben aideg Josefnu ameg qon . Odocob uqa Josef madon , “ Hocom ijaca nijewan , ” don .
Qa uqa madon , “ Cain , ijana ben jo i cofdocnu miten . Uqa ceteh oso jona bilia eunu qee cisdol . Ceteteh cunug uqana eu ija cofdugennu ebenina men .
Dana oso jona ija wooltec qee bilel . Ijana ben uqa jona ceteteh cunug cofdocnu ija iten . Qa hina uqa aideg . Hina cofhecnu qee itel . Qisol kobol i adi odigen ? Odimig Anut amegna silail migennu mataganafo ? ” don .
Odocob uqa deel abesabes cunug Josef uqaca nijuwasannu ninicdon qa Josef uqaca qee nijelesin . Uqa cemenug bilecnu culoloi .
Odocob deel osona Josef uqa cabi ugia bili jo dunuh len . Odonqa saen euna ha cabi dana leih age jo dunuh ono qee cabi oloin .
Odocob Potifa aideg uqa uqana lotoc hewi didumei madon , “ Hoga , ijaca nijuwa , ” don . Qa uqa lotoc ebenna culitotoi busalen . Odimei maha gumu calen .
Uqa lotoc ebenna culitotoi busali maha gumu cali len eu fimei
uqa cabi dana maha gumu eu utaadi maaden , “ Feiga , Hibrudec i ija gemuni jona ehudi ahon eu uqa odigeceb ege majanige geia . Uqa ene hewiteceb ijaca nijewannu hoiaqa ija euiga .
Odocob uqa ija euecemin dah mimei uqa uqana lotoc ija cemeni cuculi busali maha gumu cali leia , ” aden .
Eunu Potifa aideg uqa Josefna lotoc eu men bibilen uqa gemug jona hon .
Odocob uqa gemug je i madon , “ Hibrudec cabi dana hina egena cabi ugiannu fajudi om eu ijaca hamol hoia . Uqa ijaca nijewannu hoia .
Odocob ija euecemin uqa uqana lotoc ija cemeni cuculi busali maha gumu cali leia , ” don .
Odocob Josef uqana ben aideg je eu odi madocob uqa gemag eu ja cinigwe ben .
Odocob Josef uqana ben uqana han dana maadeceb age Josef ehudimeig gihacdoc jona ehi li tacudein . Gihacdoc jo eu Ferona gihacdoc dana bilein euna age Josef tacecebil bilen .
Qa Josef gihacdoc jona bibilen Tibud uqa Josefca bilimei uqa eeldon . Odocob dana gihacdoc jo cofdoc eu Josefnu waug me nijen .
Eunu dana gihacdoc jo cofdoc uqa Josef gihacdoc dana cunug cofadecnu muden . Odimei cabi cunug Josef ebenna men .
Aria Tibud uqa Josefca bilen . Odocob Josef uqa cabi cunug me bahic odon . Eunu dana gihacdoc jo cofdoc eu uqana cabi eunu uqa qee cisdol .
Aria saen leih leceb Ferona wain gabin hewec ilo danaca uqana bret manec ilo danaca ale Fero , uqa Isip agena ilo , odudecebil gemag ben .
Odocob Fero uqa han dana maadeceb age cabi ilo dana i alenu uqa gemag ben eu cedalimeig gihacdoc jona malein . Gihacdoc jo eu han dana ilo uqa cofdoloi . Gihacdoc jo euna Josef uqaha bilen .

Odocob han ilo i uqa Josef madon , “ Hina cabi ilo dana i alena cabi dana bilegan , ” don . Aria age euna bibilegin saen nag leceb
Ferona wain gabin hewec ilo danaca uqana bret manec ilo danaca ale witic osona bebelesin . Qa alena bebelec eu fil . Bebelec lecis alena gug eu fil .
Qasilna Josef uqa humei ale olanala gulu qeeca bibilesin fecialen .
Eunu uqa sisilalen , “ Celnu ale olanala gulu qeeca bilesia ? ” alen .
Odocob ale jejeg hewi madosin , “ Ele lecisca odi bebelowa . Qa dana oso gug sildilecnu qee bilel , ” dosin . Odocob Josef uqa maalen , “ Gug sildec cabi eu Anutna himec . Alena bebelec satesia duga , ” alen .
Odocob wain gabin hewec ilo dana uqa uqana bebelec Josef sadu madon , “ Ijana bebelecna ija wain halu olanina tatawen figa .
Wain halu eu batac ijed . Ija uqana bobog qee cifilicdoc figa . Oodon bobog cifilicdodon figa . Odocob ija aig qumei ben mi wal memen figa .
Odocob Ferona wain gabin eu ija ebenina bibilen ija aig eu cedimig cafdocomin Ferona gabinna noia . Odocob gabin eu uqa ebenna miga . I odi figa , ” don .
Odocob Josef madon , “ Bebelec gug eu i edi . Batac ijed eu deel ijed .
Odocob deel ijed hedocob Fero uqa hina enedec besihi oihimei hinana cabi ilo weledec eu haun ihigian . Odocob hina haun Ferona gabin uqa ebenna megan . Euqa hina wele uqa ebenna wain gabin molog eu odi odegan .
Qa ceteh ija mahiga eu me calecebfi ijanu me cisdogale . Ijanu Fero madoga . Odocob uqa ija gihacdoc cudun inadec besitigian .
Ija qee gale tecna Hibru agena mahanadec ehiti ene ahoin . Odocob ha ija qila gihacdoc jona biliga eu ija ceteh oso qee cahuldolom . Ija gauc bahic ene ahu mitein . Eunu ijanu Fero madoga , ” don .
Oodon bret manec ilo dana uqa Josef bebelec eu uqana gug me bahic dah mimei uqa madon , “ Ijaha bebeliga , ” don . Odocob uqa edi sadu madon , “ Ija ilomina bret galelca ijed bileiga .
Galel tatacan bilia euna Ferona bret gug filfil manec figa . Qa man fufulec age galel ilomina bilia eunadec jejegin meciadiga . Ija odi figa , ” don .
Odocob Josef uqa madon , “ Bebelec gug eu i edi . Galel ijed eu deel ijed .
Deel ijed hedocob Fero uqa enedec besihi oihigian . Odimei uqa hina ben qetigian . Odimei nana dewen cabusihigian . Odocob man fululec age hina cuhunin joqagan , ” don .
Aria hibna deel ijed docna eu Fero uqana basen deel . Eunu uqa sab ben uqana cabi dana iloilo eu ciliaden . Saen euna uqa uqana wain gabin hewec ilo danaca bret manec ilo danaca eu ale gihacdoc jonadec uqana cabi dana iloilo amagana besali cedalen .
Odocob uqa wain gabin hewec ilo dana eu uqana cabi weledec euna haun ehi li muden . Eunu uqa haun wain gabin Fero ebenna miton .
Qa uqa bret manec ilo dana eu nana deweg cabusudoin . Eu Josef maalen eu odi bahic toodu odalein .
Odonqa wain gabin hewec ilo dana uqa Josefnu qee cisdol . Uqa dahig celen .
Aria cabi gel lecis hedocob Fero uqa bebelen . Bebelec eu i edi . Uqa Nail wa ofna tatawen
bulmakau bobogolec eben naha gic lecisca Nail wa dunuhdec cali bein eu uqa feciaden . Age bohboh lec feciaden . Odocob age wa colna gigi jejegin feciaden .
Odocob bulmakau qehemega becca meciadecnu galeca qee age Nail wa dunuhdec cali bein eu feciaden . Odimeig age wa colna bulmakau eben naha gic lecisca age casac cali bein eu cemenega tawein .
Odocob bulmakau qehemega bec age bulmakau bobogolec eu belucadein . Odocob Fero uqa seeli cajen .
Odocob uqa haun us nijen . Odimei haun bebeli lecis dumei uqa macin eben naha gic lecisca me bahic bobogolec age macin gug osolna hanoc tatawegin feciaden .
Odocob haun macin eben naha gic lecisca fufu maha daincanadec welacadec eu cogain aqec age hanoc tatawegin feciaden .
Odocob age tawimeig macin eben naha gic lecisca bobogolec eu belucaadegin feciaden . Odocob Fero uqa seeli cajimei uqa bebelen eu don .
Qasil uqa bebelec eunu jaen qon . Eunu uqa doi mec danaca Isipdec doc danaca je sulduadeceb hocobil Fero uqana bebelec eu saaden . Euqa dana eundec oso age bebelec eu alena gugnu qee fogo dol .
Odocob Fero uqana wain gabin hewec ilo dana uqa Fero madon , “ Qila ija cahuldom eu cisdugina .
Saen osona hina hinana cabi dananu gemain ben . Odocob uqa ija uqana bret manec ilo danaca ele han dana Fero cofdogina eu uqana ilo uqana gihacdoc jona tacilen .
Aria witic osona ele lecisca bebelec filfil bebeloh . Odocob bebelec eu alena gugha osol qee .
Aria Hibrudec dana haun oso uqa ege gami bilom . Uqa hinana han dana uqa cofdoc agena ilo dana eu uqana cabi dana . Odocob ele elena bebelec sadoh . Odocob uqa bebelec eu alena gug filfil eu malen .
Uqa bebelec gug malen eu , eu odi toodu calen . Hina ija gihacdoc jonadec besiti oitimeg ijana cabi weledecna mitem . Odocob dana oso eu age be qetecebil cal men , ” don .
Odocob Fero uqa Josefnu je suldocob age mahucwe bahic Josef gihacdoc jonadec ehudi ahoin . Odocob uqa met qumei lotoc haun tacimei uqa Fero amegna hon .
Odocob Fero uqa Josef madon , “ Ija bebeliga . Qa dana oso uqa bebelec eu gug matecnu ihoc qee . Qa hina bebelec gugnu sildec ihoc ec ija dah miga , ” don .
Odocob Josef uqa madon , “ O ijana ben ija ijadodoc ihoc qee . Qa Anut ija cesulteceb hina sildihecemin wawin me nijigian , ” don .
Odocob Fero uqa Josef madon , “ Ijana bebelecna ija Nail wa ofna tatawigin
wa dunuhdec bulmakau bobogolec eben naha gic lecisca cali beiga . Odimeig age wa colna gigi jejegin feciadiga .
Odocob haun bulmakau eben naha gic lecisca cali beiga . Eu age qehemega bec meciadecnu galeca qee . Bulmakau meciadecnu galeca qee eu Isip mahana oso eu odi qee felem .
Odocob bulmakau qehemega bec age tawimeig bulmakau bobogolec eu belucadeiga .
Euqa age meciadecnu galeca qee eu odi himec . Dana oso uqa meciadifei age bobogolec eu belucadeiga ec qee doiaun . Odocob ija seeli cajiga .
Odocob ija ijana bebelecnaha macin bobogolec eben naha gic lecisca feciadiga . Macin eu gug osolna himec hahanon feciadiga .
Odocob macin eben naha gic lecisca fufu maha daincanadec welacadec eu cogain aqec age cali hohogin feciadiga .
Odocob age cali humeig macin eben naha gic lecisca bobogolec eu belucaadegin feciadiga . Ija bebelec i doi mec dana saadigaqa agena eundec oso uqana bebelec i gug silditecnu ihoc qee , ” don .
Odocob Josef uqa Fero madon , “ Hinana bebelec lecis eu abesabes qee . Uqana gug eu osol . Anut uqa ceteh odigiannu ihacheia .
Bulmakau eben naha gic lecisca bobogolec macin eben naha gic lecisca bobogolecca eu gug osol . Gug eu odi . Lu saen oso caligian . Eu ninijeb li cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca ugian .
Odocob bulmakau qehemega bec macin cogain qocca euha gug osol . Lu saen eu hedocob cahel saen caligian . Euha ninijeb li cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca ugian .
Je ija mahiga eu odiwe , Anut uqa ceteh odigiannu ihacheia .
Faga , sab geh Isip maha cunugna caligiannu uqana saen hona . Eu uqa cali ninijeb li cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca ugian .
Qa eu hedocob cahel saen toodu hugian . Eu cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca nijigian . Euqa cahel saen eu maha me qee mudugian . Eunu sab geh bahic nijigian saen eunu dahanaga celegian .
Cahel saen caligian eu me qee bahic nijigian . Eunu maha ina sab geh bahic ninijeb saen eunu qee cisdowain .
Aria bebelec eu bebeli lecis doga eu uqana gug eu odi . Anut uqa wele eu odi odigen imei odeia . Euqa uqa saen gohicna wele odigian .
Aria eunu Fero , hina dana cisdoc gesilecca oso fimeg Isip maha i cofdocnu mudoum .
Hina sab cofdoc dana Isip hatunadec gesil cedadaga . Lu saen sab cabi gel eben naha gic leciscana nijigian euna sab cofdoc dana eu age sab inadec oc saenna age sab dana ebeneganadec haudumeig ila mecebil am ebum osahic caligian . Odocob am osahic eundec age hina ihuqagan .
Hina maadecem age sab lu saen hona eunadec cunug cedi haudumeig taun benna jona moqagan . Sab eu jona ninijeb eu Fero uqana . Eu hinana han dana cofdoqagan .
Sab i hibna jecnu abes moqagan . Euqa cahel saen Isip hatuna calimei ninijeb li cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca ugian saen euna joqagannu abes moqagan . Isip hatu cunug cahel saenna me qee mudecdainnu eu odi odegan , ” don .
Josef je maden eu Fero uqaca uqana cabi ilo danaca age je dah mein eu me bahic .
Odocob Fero uqa cabi ilo dana maaden , “ Ege dana oso dana i cinigwe Anutna Kis uqaca bilina oso qee gulucdoqaun , ” aden .
Eunu Fero uqa Josef madon , “ Anut hina ceteh inu maheia . Dana oso cisdoc silecca hina cinigwe oso qee bilel .
Hina ijana jonu ilo bilegan . Odocob ijana dana cunug age hina con toodu odoqagan . Ija king eunu ija himec hina woolhec biligen .
Ija qila hina Isip maha cofdocnu ilo mihigina , ” don .
