Odocob Fero uqa ijan gaga mudec eben gicnadec umei Josef eben gicna taciton . Odocob uqa lotoc cecelac me bahic oso umei Josef taciton . Odimei gilolo golna mudec oso umei Josef benna be awiton .
Odocob Fero uqa uqana karis lecis doc eu uteceb euna cobon . Cocobon Fero uqana han cofdoc dana age aquni utai madein , “ Isa qoiga ! Isa qoiga ! ” adein . Eunu uqa Isip maha cunugnu ilo muden .
Odocob Fero uqa Josef madon , “ Ija Fero . Loo oso Isipdec hina qee madec ceteh oso qee odeiaun . Uqa hina sisilhimei himec odigian , ” don .
Odocob Fero uqa Josef Isipdec ijan oso qon . Uqa Safenat-panea don . Odimei uqa caja oso uton . Ijan eu Asenat . Uqa Potifera ateg . Potifera uqa ihanec dana oso Heliopolis bilen . Odocob Josef uqa Isip maha cunugna coboloi .
Aria saen euna Josef uqana cabi gel eu 30 uqa Fero Isipdec king cabi euna muden . Odocob uqa Fero cemenugnadec culimei nui Isip maha cunugna coboloi .
Odocob lu saen cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca euna sab geh bahic maha euna calen .
Odocob Josef uqa sab cunug lu saen cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca eunadec cedi haudumei taun benbenna jona men . Taun cunug agena cabi talildu nijein Josef uqa cabi eundec sab cedimei uqa taun euna men . Uqa taun cunugnu eu odiodi odoloi .
Josef uqa sab geh bahic haudon . Eunu uqa saniadeceb len ihoc qee , mati bahic . Odocobnu uqa saniec culen .
Odocob cahel saen qee hoc ninijen Josef uqa aideg , Asenat , uqa mel lecis basaliton .
Odocob Josef uqa melah matu eu ijan Manasa qon . Uqa maden , “ Anut uqa oditeceb ija ijana culumennuca ija meinuca walielnuca dahini celeia , ” en . Eunu uqa melah ijan eu odi qon .
Odocob uqa maden , “ Anut uqa ija culumenca bilec mahana mel iten , ” en . Eunu melah milum eu ijan Ifrem qon .
Aria odocob lu saen cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca Isip mahana eu cit qon .
Odocob cahel saen cabi gel eben naha gic lecisca eu sanan men . Eu Josef je maden eu odi bahic toodu calen . Odocob cahel saen maha cunug ihoc len qa Isip hatuna eu sabca bilen .
Saen cahel saen eu Isip maha cunug ihoc leceb dana cajaca age wen adec tebandoin . Odocobnu age Fero inoni madoin , “ Sab igiga , ” doin . Odocob Fero dana caja Isipdec maaden , “ Josefca leiga . Uqa cel je oso maadigian eu odi toodu odeiga , ” aden .
Saen cahel eu Isip hatu cunug ihoc leceb Josef uqa sab jo jic hudimei Isipdec dana cajaca idadoqagannu suldoloi . Oodon saen euna Isip mahana cahel eu me qee bahic nijen .
Aria cahel eu hatuhatu cunugna me qee bahic ihoc li nijen . Eunu dana hatu filfilnadec age Isip ono sab Josef ebennadec fajoqagannu holoig .
Aria Jekob Isip ono sabca uqa don . Eunu uqa melahul maaden , “ Age eetanu gauc bilegina ?
Feiga , Isip ono sabca eu ija dah miga . Age ono numeig cudun eunadec egena sab leih fajeiga . Eufi ege cebac bilecnu , ege qee cal moqaun , ” aden .
Odocob Josef waliagul 10 eu age sab Isipdec fajoqagannu ono noin .
Qa Jekob uqa Josef waliag gug , Benjamin , waliagul gami qee suldol . Uqa cisdon , “ Cal mec oso uqaca hocdain , ” en . Eunu uqa Benjamin suldocnu cucuien .
Aria cahel saen calen eu Kenan hatuha on . Eunu Jekob melahul age sab fajoqagannu nonogin age dana leih ageha sab fajoqagannu nonogin eu osoben gabandu noin .
Aria Josef uqa hatu eu ilo bilen . Odocob uqa dana hatu cunug eunadec hocobil sab idadec cabi oloi . Odocob Josef waliagul age humeig uqa amegna jogoi nu maha cotadoin .
Saen Josef uqa waliagul meciadimei uqa wele don qa uqa dana celedec cinigwe ihocon qumei uqa je gagadic sisiladen , “ Age anadec hoiga ? ” aden . Odocob age jejeg hewi madoin , “ Ege Kenan hatunadec sab fajecnu hoqa , ” doin .
Aria Josef uqa Isip je maaden . Je falicdoc dana oso Hibru je falicdon . Eunu Josef uqa waliagul meciaadi uqa don qa uqa waliagul age eu Josef ec qee doloin .
Odocob Josef uqa waliagulnu bebelen eunu cisdon . Odimei maaden , “ Age hannu cijawi coboc dana . Age egena hatu maha qee cofdoc nijia eu foqagannu hoiga , ” aden .
Odocob waliagul age jejeg hewi madoin , “ Qeeo , egena ben . Ege hinana cabi dana . Ege sab fajeqannu hoqa .
Ege dana osahic melahul . Ege hannu cijawi coboc dana qee . Ege je mele madec dana , ” doin .
Qa uqa maaden , “ Qeeo . Age egena maha qee cofdoc nijia eu foqagannu hoiga , ” aden .
Odocob age madoin , “ Egena ben , ege dana osahic melahul . Ege weleca gabandoc cunug eu 12 . Ege Kenan mahana biluqona . Odocob subig eu memigeca bilia qa osahic eu wele cal men , ” doin .
Odocob Josef maaden , “ Ija wele maadiga eu odi himec . Age hannu cijawi coboc dana .
Ija i edi temadigen . Fero amegna je cagu madigina . Waliniga subig eu ene hugian . Qeefi age cudun i qee culimeig belowain .
Age eundec oso suldocobil nui waliniga ehudi ahoia . Cunug age gihacdoc jona biluqagan . Odocob agena je eu melefo qeefo ege fecnu ? Age cahuldufeig mele bahic , Fero amegna , age hannu cijawi coboc dana , ” aden .
Odocob uqa waliagul cunug gihacdoc jona tacadeceb deel ijed bilein .
Aria Josef uqa deel ijed docna maaden , “ Ija Anut amegna cobigina . Eunu ceteh oso odifeig age cebac biluqagan .
Age je madec eu melefo qeefo gesilecnu waliniga oso gihacdoc jona age bileiga euna cuculdeig beleiga . Age cahel saennu agena talnu sab gahidumeig beleiga .
Odimeig waliniga subig eu ijaca ehudi ahoiga . Odocobilfi agena je eu mele eu feqan . Odocob age qee cal mowain , ” aden . Odocob Josef maaden eu age cois ege toodu odeqan ec madoin .
Odocob age madocobmadocob i madein , “ Mele bahic ceteh i egeca calena eu celnu ? Ege Josef odudom eunu odigina . Ege uqana cucuiecca jaen qocca eu fecomun uqa inongigi maden , ‘ Ija cahahateiga , ’ een ege uqa qee dah mudecwe mom . Eunu culumen ben bahic qila egeca hoia , ” ein .
Odocob Ruben maaden , “ Ija mel eu deweg cain tudowainnu maadem qa age ija qee dah mitilein . Eunu qila ege eu odomnu uqana ameg eu ocnu , ” aden .
Odonqa Josef uqa agena jena je madein eu don . Qa waliagul age eunu qee doloin .
Odocob uqa culadi limei qajen . Qa uqa haun maadecnu gagadic mimei ceseli humei Simion ihohdumei uqana han dana maadeceb age Simion umeig age amagana eben libein .
Odocob Josef uqa uqana cabi dana maadeceb age sab agena bekna taciadimeig agena meen qaig silwana mudec haun ceseli tahiadein . Jicna sab jecnu euha adeiga ec maaden . Odocob age eu odi odiadein .
Odocob Josef waliagul age agena sab udca ceselna meadimeig Isip culimeig belein .
Age cudun witic meceb nijein euna calimeig age oso uqa cesel sab utigiannu uqana bek co cufalen . Odimei uqana meen qaig silwana mudec eu bek cona bibilen fen .
Odocob uqa waliagul utaadi maaden , “ Ijana qaig eu ceseli taceiga eu bek cona bibilen figa , ” aden . Odocob age dumanaga culen . Odocob age qeleli bileig madocobmadocob madein , “ Anut uqa i cel kobol ege odigia ? ” ein .
Aria age Kenan hatuna calimeig age memega , Jekobca , hoin . Ceteh cunug ageca calen eu sadudu madoin .
“ Dana oso , uqa hatu eunadec dana ben , uqa ege je gagadic bahic magen . Odimei uqa ege hannu cijawi coboc dana gen .
Qa ege madom , ‘ Ege hannu cijawi coboc dana qee . Ege mele je madec dana .
Ege dana osol melahul . Ege waliagwaliag , cunug gabandoc eu 12 . Oso eu cal men . Subig eu qila ege memigeca ono Kenan mahana bilia , ’ dom .
Odocob dana ben eu magen , ‘ Age mele je madec danafo qeefo eu i edi dugen . Age waliniga oso ene ijaca culdimeig agena cahel saennu sab cedimeig agena talca nueiga .
Qa age waliniga subig eu ehudi ijaca ahoiga . Eufi age hannu cijawi coboc dana qee . Age mele je madec dana eu ija dugen . Odocob ija age waliniga oso i ceseli adigen . Odocob age ene idadecnu hoqagan eu ihoc , ’ gen , ” age memega je odi sadoin .
Aria saen age agena beknadec sab hihidi bileig age cunug agena meen qaig badom eu age abesabes agena sab bekna bibilen fein . Odocob Jekob uqa melahul gami age eu odi fimeig age filiciti cucuiein .
Odocob age memega Jekob uqa maden , “ Age ijana mel Josef cawaltein . Uqa qee bilel . Odocob Simion uqaha qee bilel . Odeiaqa qila age Benjamin cawaltoqagannu mateginafo ? Age culumen i ija itegina , ” aden .
Odocob Ruben uqa memeg madudu maden , “ Benjamin ija ebenina mecem ija cofdodomin belewan . Odocob haun ceseli ahu hinaca mudigen . Ija Benjamin qee ehudi ceseli hocominfi hina ija melamiel lecis eu ale qagaalaga , ” don .
Qa Jekob uqa madon , “ Ija melami uqa hinaca Isip ono qee noiaun . Uqa waliag , Josef , eu wele cal men . Odonnu uqa jaih cuhanuc himec bilina . Saen uqa jicna cocobob cal mec oso uqaca hocobfi euqa colini beceb ija toia migen . Eunu ija wawi cagoc bibili helna nugen , ” don .
Aria cahel saen eu qee qee mel . Eu me qee bahic odi nijen .
Eunu age sab Isipdec ehi bein eu ji qee mudimeig age memega maaden , “ Isip haun belimeig sab leih haun fajadeiga , ” aden .
Qa Juda uqa memeg madon , “ Dana eu je gagadic edi magen , ‘ Age walinigaca qee hocobilfi ija amina haun qee howain , ’ gen .
Hina ege walinige eu uqaca sulgecemfi ege numeb hinana sab fajihecnu .
Qa hina uqaca qee sulgecemfi ege qee noqaun . Dana eu uqa edi magen , ‘ Age walinigaca qee hocobilfi ija amina haun qee howain , ’ gen , ” don .
Odocob Jekob uqa sisiladen , “ Age eetanu dana eu madoin , ‘ Ege walinige oso bilia , ’ ec madoinnu edi me qee bahic oditegina ? ” aden .
Qa age madoin , “ Dana eu uqa egena sihulnu bahic sisilgen . Uqa odi sisilgen , ‘ Age memega cebac biliafo ? Age waliniga osocafo ? ’ gen . Odocob ege uqa sisilec eu jejeg hewom . Qa uqa edi magen , ‘ Age waliniga ene ehudi neiga , ’ gen eu ege adi docnu ? ” doin .
Odocob Juda uqa memeg , Jekob , madon , “ Mel eu egeca osoben sulgaga . Odocob ege qila bahic cajimeb beleqan . Eufi ege qee cal moqaun . Ege cebac bilecnu .
Ija je cagu madigina . Ija uqa ene hina amenna qee ehudi ahufig ija ja eu gahidudu li cal migen .
Ege qee daleoummi ege wele ono numeb ceseli hu lecis doum , ” don .
Odocob Jekob maaden , “ Age eu odi odoqaganfi cois eu odi odoiga . Age hatu inadec ceteteh caunca leih cedimeig agena bekna tacadeiga . Age na gilic moolca dedeman me bahicca cenal cinigwe eundec pistasio almon aigca cedadeiga . Age ceteteh i age eundec nagnag cedadimeig dana eu loo utuqagannu hewi nueiga .
Odocob age meen qaig onodec hewadi ceselein euha cedeiga . Odimeig eu tatac meen qaig haun eu uqana ameg eu casacnadec eu cinigwe eu odi ha cedeiga . Age meen qaig casacnadec bek cona tahein eu haun ceseli adoqagan . Eu cahuldu taheinfa .
Walinigaha ehudi beleiga . Odimeig qilaca caji ceseli dana euca beleiga .
Anut Gagadic Bahic uqa dana eu odudocob uqa agenu waug me nijeceb age amegna tawecebil uqa waliniga euca Benjaminca besali adigia . Qa ijana doc odi ijana mel culdifig cois ija culdigen , ” aden .
Eunu uqa melahul age dana ben eu loo utuqagannu ceteteh euca meen qaig hewi ceselein euca haun hewi nuecnu cedein euca cedadimeig age Benjamin ehudecebil cajimeig Isip ono noin . Odimeig age Josef amegna tawein .
Saen Josef uqa Benjamin ageca fimei uqa uqana sab cofdoc dana eu madon , “ Dana i age ijana jona cedi hewi nuuga . Odimeg dool oso qocom cal meceb jecnu saciadoga . Dana i age qila cahineg age ija gami sab jeqan , ” don .
Odocob sab cofdoc dana eu Josef madon eu odi odon . Uqa Josef waliagul ehadimei Josefna jona ehadi nuen .
Saen Josef waliagul age dana eu Josefna jona ehadi nunuen age ben cucuiein . Age odi cisdoin , “ Saen ege ene hahawan nom euna age egena meen qaig silwana badom eu ege cunug egena bek cona tacigein . Uqa qaignu je euna um qigimeig egena cesel cedimeig ege cahacgi hewigimeig gihacdoc jona tacigimeig cabi gagadic iguqagan . Eunu ege ene ehigia ahona , ” ein .
Eunu age Josefna sab cofdoc dana euca limeig jo cebecna madoin ,
“ O dana ben , saen ege hahawan ene sab fajecnu nom eu
ceseli bebeloqon witic meceb us nijecnu jaen mudom eu ege abesabes egena bek co cufalimeb ege cunug egena qaig cunug bibilen fom . Eunu ege qila haun hewi ceseloqa .
Ege qaig leihha sab fajecnu hewi noqa . Osoqa uqa egena qaig haun ceseli egena beknana tacigen eu qee doqona , ” doin .
Odocob uqa maaden , “ Cain cisdowain . Eunu jeca qee . Cain cucuiowain . Agena Anut , age memegana Anut , uqa age qaig eu agena bekna taciadenfa . Ija agena meen qaig silwana mudec eu om , ” aden . Odimei uqa Simion ageca ehudi ahu muden .
Odocob sab cofdoc dana eu uqa Josef waliagul ehadi Josefna jona len . Odimei uqa jaimiga cusecnu wa adeceb agena cesel sabha aden .
Aria waliagul age cahineg Josefca ono sab joqagan ec doin . Eunu age Josef ceteteh loo utuqagannu saciadoin .
Odocob cahineg Josef uqa jona hocob age ceteteh loo utuqagannu ebenegana hewimeig jo hamol lein . Odimeig age uqa amegna gob cehi bilimeig jogoi nu maha cotadoin .
Odocob uqa sisiladen , “ Age me bileigafo ? Age memeganu madein eu uqa me biliafo ? Uqa cebac biliafo ? ” aden .
Odocob age jejeg hewi madoin , “ O ben , ege memige uqa me bilia . Uqa cebac bilia , ” doin . Odocob age haun uqa amegna jogoein .
Odocob uqa waliag gug Benjamin fifi maaden , “ Age waliniga subig inu ija mateinfo ? ” aden . Odimei uqa Benjamin madon , “ Anut hinanu waug me nijiale , ” don .
Odocob Josef uqa waliagnu waug qocob qajigiannu odon . Eunu uqa mahuc bahic cali len . Odimei uqa qajigiannu cudun walen . Odimei uqa uqana cuamu dunuh euna limei ono qajen .
Eu hedocob uqa ola cusimei cali hon . Uqa cali humei haun qajecdainnu uqadodoc gagadic mimei uqana cabi dana maaden , “ Sab qoiga , ” aden .
Odocob age casac Josefna sab qoin . Odimeig age Josef waliagul agena sab qoin . Odimeig age Isipdec dana ageca sab joqagannu bilein eu agena sab qoin . Qa Isip dana age Hibru dana gami sab gabandu joqagannu qee gale adel . Eunu abes bilein .
Aria age Josef waliagul maadecebil age sab jecnu bilein eu i edi bilein . Waliaga matu uqa casac cali hon eu uqa aquni bilen . Odocob age toodocobtoodocob cali hoin eu odi bibilegin li subig cali honna cit qon . Age eu odi bilein eu fimeig age wawaga qee fogo dol .
Saen cabi dana age sab Josefna sab jec cabalnadec siwiadecebil Benjamin uqa sab leih wooladec on . Uqa sab on eu dana ebum osahic jec ihocwe on . Eunu age cucuiecca qee Josef gami sab jejeig wain jejeig ein .
Aria Josef uqa uqana jo cofdoc dana madon , “ Dana i agena bekna sab tacecebil am beia . Age gahidoc ihoc eu odi taceiga . Odimeig age osahicosahic agena meen qaig eu bek cona taceiga .
Odocob mel subig uqana bekna ijana gabin silwana mudec euca uqana meen qaig sab fajecnu euca bek cona tacitoiga , ” don . Odocob dana eu Josef madon eu odi odon .
Qasil cocojagen Josef uqa suladeceb age agena ceteteh ceselna meadimeig agena jicna cocobi belein .
Odocob age taun ben culdi onoca qee nuec ninijen Josef uqa uqana jo cofdoc dana madon , “ Hina cajimeg dana eu age jabadi tooadi nuuga . Gulucadimeig sisiladaga , ‘ Age celnu kobol mena odadecemin me qeena wadacdoiga ?
Celnu age ijana benna gabin silwana mudec heje oiga ? Gabin i ijana ben uqa euna gab jenanu . Odi ha uqa gabin ina doi menanu . Eu kobol me qee bahic odoiga , ’ adaga , ” don .
Odocob uqa jabadi tooadi nuimei gulucadi je eu odi maaden .
Odocob age jejeg hewi madoin , “ Egena ben , uqa je eu odi celnu madena ? Ege dana ititom . Eu odocnu ihoc qee .
Faga , meen qaig egena bek cona bilen eu ege Kenan mahanadec ceseli ahu hom . Ege silwafo golfo egena benna jonadec adi heje ocnu ?
Ceteh eu ege oso heje ocobfi cois age dana eu qagadocobil cal migian . Odocob egeha cois gihacgoqagan , ” doin .
Eunu uqa maaden , “ Je age madeiga eu odi himec ija odigen . Qa gabin eu in oso uqana bekna gulucdufig dana eu gihacdocnu mudigen . Odocob age cunug age dewenegana jeca qee , ” aden .
Odocob age mahucmahuc agena bek cesel gogodomoganadec cacu ti mahana mimeig bek co huleladein .
Odocob uqa agena bekna cijawec sanan men . Uqa matuna bekna cijawec sanan mimei waliaga subigna bekna cit qon . Uqa cijawimei gabin eu Benjaminna bekna gulucdon .
Odocob waliagul dumanaga culeceb age agena lotoc bahalaadein . Odimeig agena ud haun cedi cesel gogodomogana mimeig ceseli taun benna belein .
Saen Juda uqa waliagul gami Josefna jona hoin eu uqa ono bibilen age hoin . Age uqa amegna calimeig age mahucwe bahic mahana gob cehi bilimeig ubocuboc nijein .
Odocob Josef maaden , “ Age cel kobol oditeiga ? Dana ija edec ija doi mecnu ihoc ec qee doginafo ? ” aden .
Eunu Juda uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ijana ben , eeta higen ? Ege cel je madecnu ? Cahuldoc eu ege qee odolom . Eu adi ihachecnu ? Anut uqa egena cahuldoc camasac meia . Qila hina ege gihacdocna migegan . Dana gabin uqana bekna gulucdoiga euca egeca osoben gihacdocna migegan , ” don .
Qa Josef uqa maaden , “ Ija eu odi odocwe qee qa ijana gabin cel dana uqana bekna gulucdoiga eu himec uqa gihacdoc jona mudigen . Odocob age cunug cois wawaga malolca age memegaca ceseli beloqagan , ” aden .
Odocob Juda uqa Josef cemenug timei madon , “ O ijana ben , hina Feroca ale ihocihoc . Ijanu cain gemain beiaun qa ija culitecem je oso mahiga .
Ijana ben , weleca hina ege sisilgem , ‘ Age memegacafo ? Age waliniga osocafo ? ’ gem .
Odocob ege jejein hewi mahom , ‘ Ege memigeca , uqa toia . Odocob ege walinige subigca uqa ege memige toia bibilen anige basiton . Subig eu uqa waliag wele cal men . Eunu uqa anag mel osahic , uqa jaih cuhanuc . Ege memige uqa uqanu cal mena , ’ hom .
Odocob hina magem , ‘ Ehudi necebil ija amigul figen , ’ gem .
Odocob ege mahom , ‘ Mel eu uqa memeg culdecwe qee . Uqa culdecebfi uqa memeg cal migian , ’ hom .
Qa hina magem , ‘ Age waliniga subig eu uqaca qee nifeig age ija amina haun qee howain , ’ gem .
Eunu , ijana ben , ege ceseli belimeb ege memige hinana je i madom .
Odocob ege memige uqa magen , ‘ Ceseli belimeig sab leih haun fajeiga , ’ gen .
Qa ege madom , ‘ Ege nocwe qee . Ege walinige subig uqacafi nocnu . Ege walinige subig uqaca qee nufeb ege dana eu amegna haun qee loqaun , ’ dom .
Odocob ege memige uqa magen , ‘ Ija aideni , Resel , uqa melamiel lecis basaliten age dogina .
Odocob oso uqa ija culitimei nuen . Odocob ija madem , ‘ Mele bahic , uqa tuqi calcaldoiga , ’ em . Euqa ija haun qee felem .
Odocob age iha ija cemeninadec cocobil cal mec uqaca hocobfi age ija oditecebil wawi me qee mecca helna nugen , ’ uqa odi magen .
Eunu , ijana ben , ege haun ceseli belocomun ege memige uqa walinige subig eu qee fifei uqa cal migian . Uqana cebac bilec eu melah subig euna bilina . Eunu ege memige uqa odidocomun waug me qee mecca helna nugian .

Odenqa ija je wele cagu ijana mei madom . Ija odi madom , ‘ Melem subig eu qee ceseli ehudi ahocominfi ja eu ija dewenina bibileb li cal mec gadacna caligen , ’ dom .
Aria , ijana ben , eunu ija hinana gihacdoc jona bibilemin mel subig eu culdecem waliagul gami ceseli beleiga .
Mel eu ijaca qee belocomunfi ija meica adi ceseli nuigen ? Ija eu odi odifig ija mei uqana waug me qee mec eu adi figen ? ” don .
Odocob Josef qajecnu amulig bi cit qon . Odocob uqa dana amagana gagadic mecwe qeenu uqa qagai maaden , “ Dana cunug age ija aminadec cali li beleiga , ” aden . Eunu dana cunug age calecebil Josef uqa waliagulca himec bilimeig uqa ija age waliniga ec qasali maaden .
Odocob Josef uqa co suli umei geh bahic qaqajen Isip dana onodec calein eu age dah mudein . Odocob Fero uqaca uqana talca ageha Josef qajeianu je eu doin .
Aria Josef uqa waliagul maaden , “ Ija Josef . Ija mei uqa cebac biliafo ? ” aden . Qa age filiciteeig culunuga cacu teceb jeca qee qeleli tawein .
Odocob uqa maaden , “ Ija cemeni hoiga , ” aden . Age eu odi odocobil uqa maaden , “ Ija age waliniga Josef age Isip dana ebenegana idadoin .
Qa age qila eu odi odoinnu cain jaen aqeiaun . Age dana enedecca idadteinnu cain cisdowain . Anut uqa ene sulten . Anut uqa age qee hoc ninijen dana qee cal mowainnu ija aquniadi sulten .
Cahel eu maha ina cabi gel lecis docna himec ninijen hoia . Odocob cabi gel ebum osahic eu qee hedoc nijia . Saen euna sab cehecnuca ocnuca qee nijiaun .
Qa Anut ageca agena sihulca qee cal mowainnuca cal mecnadec cahahaadigiannuca uqa ija aquniadi sulten .
Eunu age ene ija qee sultelein qa Anut uqa ija ene sulten . Uqa ija Ferona cisdoc dana miten . Ferona dana cunug ija cofadigina . Isip hatu cunug ija ilo biligina .
Eunu mahuc bahic ija meica ceseli timeig madoiga , ‘ Hina melem , Josef , edi madeia , ‘ Anut uqa ija Isip hatu cunugnu ilo miten . Mahuc ijaca hoga . Cain daleagaun .
Hina Gosen mahana bilegan . Euqa hina ija cemeni bilegan . Hinaca hinana mel simca hina asinelca age cunug Gosen mahana biluqagan . Agena sipsip amca meme amca bulmakau amca ceteteh cunug hinana euca age ono biluqagan .
Age ono bilecebilfi ija cesuladigen . Cahel saen cabi gel ebum osahic eu hugian . Gad gad hinaca hinana talca age sawen bilimeig cal mowain , ’ Josef eu odi madeia , ’ doiga .
Feiga , agegul amagana mecitegina . Odocob ija wali Benjaminha uqagul amegna mecitina . Ija Josef , ija himec je maadigina .
Ija ene Isip hatuna dana ben , ijanica biliga eunu madoiga . Ceteh cunug ene wele feiga eunu ha madoiga . Odocob age mahucwe ija mei ene ehudi ahoiga , ” aden .
Odocob uqa eben qelalimei waliag Benjamin colowandumei qajen . Odocob Benjamin uqaha Josef cogadudu bili qajen .
Odocob uqa waliagul cunug cotaadimei agenu qajen . Eu cunug hedocob uqa waliagul age uqaca je madein .
Aria Fero uqa Josef waliagul uqaca hoiga ec don saen euna uqaca uqana dana iloiloca age wawaga ceelen .
Odocob Fero uqa Josef madon , “ Hina waliniel edi maadaga , ‘ Agena cesel cunug jajadumeig ceseli Kenan mahana beleiga .
Odimeig age memegaca agena talca cedadimeig ehadi ijaca ahoiga . Odocobil ija Isip hatuna maha me bahic oso , maha cunug wooladec , oso adigen . Odocob age sab me bahic hatu eunadec joqagan , ’ adaga .
Je ha maadaga , ‘ Karis leih ene Isipdec cedimeig nui ono age aidagailca agena mel simca tacadi ahoiga . Age memegaha ehudi ahoiga .
Agena ceteteh culecnu cain cisdowain . Isip hatunadec ceteh cauncaca eu adigen , ’ eu odi maadaga , ” don .
Odocob Jekob melahul age Fero maaden eu odi odoin . Josef uqa Ferona je toodumei waliagul karis leih aden . Odimei sab jicna joqagannu ha aden .
Uqa waliagwaliag cunug lotoc haunhaun aden . Qa Benjaminnu eu uqa lotoc haunhaun ebum osahic utaden . Odimei uqa meen qaig silwana mudec eu 300 eu odi uten .
Odocob uqa memegna ceteteh Isip hatunadec ceteteh cauncaun eu cesel 10 age gahidoin euca sab uqa memeg saen uqa jicna cocobi bilei jigiannuca eu cesel 10 age gahidoin euca suldon .
Odimei uqa waliagul suladeceb belein . Age bebelegin uqa maaden , “ Age jicna cain fee dadanowain , ” aden .
Odocob age Isipdec Kenan hatuna memega Jekobca bein .
Odocob age Kenan bimeig memega edi madoin , “ Josef qee cal mel . Uqa cebac bilia . Mele bahic uqa Isip hatu cunug eu cofdocnu uqa ilo bilia , ” doin . Odocob Jekob uqa filiciten qa uqa je eunu waug qee meleel .
Odonqa saen age Josefna je eu sadodoig karis uqa tacudi ehudi nocnu Josef suldon eu fimei uqa waug togdon .
Odocob Jekob uqa maden , “ Eu mele bahic ! Ija melami Josef uqa gaid cebac bilia . Ija nui fimig cal migen , ” en .
Eunu Jekob uqa uqana cetetehca Isip nuen . Uqa Biasiba ono calimei uqa memeg Aisakna Anut eu ihandon .
Odocob witicna Anut uqa Jekob ola codocna edi madon , “ Jekob , Jekob , ” don . Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija i hen , ” don .
Odocob Anut uqa madon , “ Ija Anut , ija memenna Anut . Hina Isip nocnu cain cucuiagaun . Ija odocna ono hinana sihul eu mati bahic fulusdoqagan .
Ija hinaca Isip nowan . Odocob mele bahic ija hina haun ceseli ehihi bigen . Odocob hina Josef ebenna cal megan , ” don .
Odocob Jekob uqa Biasiba culdimei nuen . Odocob Jekob melahul age memegaca aidagailca agena mel simca karis Fero memega tacuduqagannu aden euna tacadimeig ehadi belein .
Odocob Jekob uqa uqana sihul cunugca gami noin . Uqana dool mananca ceteteh cunug Kenan mahana ono bibili bilei cedaden eu cunug cedadeceb Isip ono belein .
Uqa melahulca uqa asagul danaca uqa ategulca uqa asagul cajaca uqana sihul cunugca odi cedadimei ehadi uqaca Isip noin .
Aria i eu Jekob uqa melahul ijanaga , euqa Jekob uqa gami Isip ono noin . Ruben uqa Jekob melah matu .
Ruben melahul eu ijanaga Hanok , Palu , Hesron , Kameca .
Simion uqa melahulca eu ijanaga Jemuel , Jamin , Ohad , Jakin , Soha , Saolca . Saol uqa Kenan cajanadec calen .
Liwai uqa melahulca eu ijanaga Geson , Kohaf , Merarica .
Juda uqa melahulca eu ijanaga Er , Onan , Sela , Peres , Sinaca . Aria Er Onanca ale Kenan mahana cal mesin . Odocob Peres uqa melahul eu ijanala Hesron Hamulca .
Isaka uqa melahulca eu ijanaga Tola , Pua , Jasub , Simronca .
Sebjulan uqa melahulca eu ijanaga Seret , Elon , Jalelca .
Lia uqa melahul i age Jekob Mesopotemia ono basaditon . Uqaha ateg oso , Daina , ono basiton . Jekobna mel mel aidca age Lia uqa anaga bilen cunug gabandoc eu 33 .
Aria Gad uqa melahulca eu ijanaga Sifion , Hagi , Suni , Esbon , Eri , Arodi , Arelica .
Ase uqa melahulca eu ijanaga Imna , Iswa , Iswi , Beria , age cebinamaga Seraca . Odocob Beria melahul lecis eu ijanala Hiba Malkielca .
Dana i age eu Silpa melahul . Silpa uqa Liana cabi caja Leban uqa uten . Uqa melahul i age Jekob basaditon eu cunug gabandoc eu 16 .
Aria Jekob aideg Resel uqa mel lecis basaliton . Eu ijanala Josef Benjaminca .
Odocob saen Josef uqa Isip ono bibilen aideg , Asenat , uqa mel lecis Josef basaliton . Eu ijanala Manasa Ifremca . Asenat uqa Potifera ateg . Eu Heliopolis ihanec dana .
Aria Benjamin uqa melahulca eu ijanaga Bela , Beke , Asbel , Gera , Naman , Ehi , Ros , Mupim , Hupim , Adca .
Eunu Jekobna mel age Resel uqa anaga bilen eu cunug gabandoc eu 14 .
Aria Dan melah eu Husim .
Naftali uqa melahulca eu ijanaga Jasel , Guni , Jese , Silemca .
Dana i age eu Bilha melahul . Bilha uqa Reselna cabi caja Leban uqa uten . Uqa melahul i age Jekob basaditon . Eu cunug gabandoc eu eben naha gic lecisca .
Dana cunug Jekob uqana sihul bahic uqa gami Isip belein eu gabandoc 66 . Euqa Jekob melahul aidagailca qee gabandu sicanadec .
Josef aideg mel manahal lecis Isip ono basalen . Eunu Jekobna tal cunug gabandoc Isip noin eu 70 .
Aria Jekob uqa Juda aquni Josefca suldon . Uqa Josef madocob Gosen maha eu ana nijia eu dado mudigiannu suldon .
Odocob age Gosen cacalegin Josef uqa uqana karis saciadumei memeg Jekob gulucdugiannu nuen . Saen Josef uqa memeg gulucdumei uqa eben limei memeg colowandudu saen cecelacca uqanu qajen .
Odocob Jekob uqa Josef madon , “ Qila ija cal mecnu ihoc . Ija ijadodoc hina cebac gaid biliga eu mecihiga , ” don .
Odocob Josef uqa waliagulca memeg uqana talca maaden , “ Ija Feroca timig ija walielca ija mei uqana tal eu Kenan mahana bilegina age ijaca hoiga ec madugen .
Age sipsip cofadec dana . Age dool cofadeginanu . Eunu age agena dool am cunugca agena ceteteh cunugca cedimeig hoiga ec madugen .
Saen Fero uqa utaadeceb uqaca lecebil edi sisiladecebfi , ‘ Age cel cabi oginanu ? ’ adecebfi
age odi jejeg hewi madoqagan , ‘ Egena ben , ege dool simnadec cofaadi ben mom . Ege memigeil odoloig eu odi dih odoqona , ’ doqagan . Age eu odi madocobilfi uqa age Gosen mahana biluqagan eunu cois adigian , ” aden . Aria Isip dana age dool cofadec dananu qee gale adena . Eunu Josef eu odi maaden .
Odocob Josef uqa waliagul ebum oso ehadi li Feroca calimei madon , “ Ija meica ija walielca agena dool amca agena ceteh cunug euca Kenan mahanadec hoiga . Age qila Gosen bileiga , ” don .
Odocob Josef uqa waliagul ebum osahic eu nesili cedadimei Fero amegna ehadi len .
Odocob Fero uqa Josef waliagul sisiladen , “ Age cel cabi oginanu ? ” aden . Odocob age jejeg hewi madoin , “ Egena ben , ege sipsip cofadec dana . Euqa ege memigeil odoloigwe odoqona .
Cahel saen Kenan mahana eu me qee bahic nijia . Odocob egena dool amnu eu sabca qee . Eunu ege qila Gosen ono culigecem bileqannu sisilhoqona , ” doin .
Odocob Fero uqa Josef madon , “ Hina memenca hina walinelca age hinaca hoiga .
Eunu Isip maha eu hina ebenna bilia . Cel maha me bahic oso fimeig memen walinelca euna madaga . Gosen ono madecem biluqagan eu cois . Odocob hina walinel eundec oso uqa dool cofadecnu doc qataneccafi uqa ijana dool cofadigiannu ilo muduga , ” don .
Odocob Josef uqa memeg Jekob Fero amegna ehudi len . Odocob Jekob uqa Fero eeldoc je madon .
Odocob Fero uqa Jekob sisildon , “ Hinana cabi gel ganic ? ” don .
Odocob uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ijana cabi gel eu 130 . Odocob ija maha filfilna geh bahic loldudu cobem . Qa cabi gel eu cecelac qee , eu gohic . Ijana loldudu coboc eu culumen mati bahicca . Ija memiel loldudu coboin eu cabi gel mati bahic . Eu wooldoc ijana cabi gel , ” don .
Odocob Jekob uqa Fero eeldoc je haun madon . Odimei uqa Fero amegnadec cali li nuen .
Eunu Josef uqa memegca uqa waliagulca Isip ono madeceb bilein . Odimei uqa maha eunadec ceteteh cauncaca eu aden . Maha Fero ihacaden eu ijan Rameses .
Odocob Josef uqa memegnuca waliagulnuca memegna talnuca mel simnuca sab ihoc siwiaden .
Odocob cahel eu me qee bahic nijen . Eunu maha cunug sabca qee men . Odocob Isip Kenanca dana age wennu gagadicca qee mein .
Odocob Josef uqa meen qaig sab fajecnu gulucdu haudumei Ferona jona ehi len .
Aria dana cajaca Isipdec Kenandecca agena meen qaig qee meceb Isip dana age humeig Josef madoin , “ Sab igiga . Qee igecemfi ege cal meqan . Cesulgaga . Egena meen qaig ji hedoqa , ” doin .
Odocob Josef uqa maaden , “ Agena dool manan ahoiga . Agena meen qaig eu qee mecebfi ija eu wadacdocnu sab adigen , ” aden .
Eunu age agena hosca sipsipca memeca bulmakauca ceselca Josefca ahocobil uqa eu wadacdocnu sab aden . Odocob Josef uqa cabi gel euna eu odi odon . Agena dool manan cunug ahocobil uqa eu wadacdocnu sab aden .
Odocob cabi gel eu hedocob eu cabi gel haunna uqaca hoin . Odimeig madoin , “ Egena ben , ege hina amenna je mele eu jahunecwe qee . Egena qaig eu qee men . Euqa egena dool manan hina wele ihom . Ege ceteh oso hina ihecnu qee bilel . Qa ege dewenigeca egena mahaca himec bilia .
Cain culigecem cal moqaun . Cain culecem egena maha me qee meiaun . Egeca egena mahaca fajigi oigiga . Odocob egeca egena mahaca eu Ferona bilecnu . Sab aig igecem ege eu cehimeb jiji cebac bilecnu eu odifi ege qee cal moqaun , ” doin .
Eunu Josef uqa Isip maha cunug eu Ferona fajiton . Cahel saen eu ageca me qee bahic nijen . Eunu Isipdec dana cunug age agena maha idadecnu suldoin . Eunu maha cunug eu Fero faji on . Odocob uqa muguh bilen .
Odocob Josef uqa dana cajaca Isip maha gadac osonadec nueceb osona gadac eu age cunug fajadi on .
Odonqa Josef uqa ihanec dana agena maha qee faji ol . Fero uqa meen qaig agenu ihoc bilecnu aden . Eunu ihanec dana age agena maha idadecnu qee suldoloin .
Odocob Josef uqa dana cajaca maaden , “ Aria feiga , qila ija ageca agena mahaca Ferona fajaditom . Eunu agena sab aig i hen . Cedimeig mahana ceheiga .
Odocob sab wal mec saenna age sab cedimeig am ebum osahicna ila mimeig age am eundec oso Fero utuqagan . Odimeig am wal oso eu agena . Euqa agena eu aig cehecnuca sab jecnuca biligian . Aig leih cabina cehoqagan . Leih ageca agena talca joqagan , ” aden .
Odocob age madoin , “ Hina cebac bileqannu cesulgagana . Hina me bahic eelgagana . Eunu ege egena ben Ferona bileqan , ” doin .
Eunu Josef uqa je sab cedimeig am ebum osahicna ila mimeig age am eundec oso age Fero utuqagannu maaden eu gagadic mudeceb loo oso Isipna calen . Loo eu qilaha gaid nijia . Euqa odi sab am eundec oso Fero uteginanu . Ihanec dana agena maha himec eu Ferona qee nijel .
Aria Isrel dana caja age Isip ono Gosen mahana bilein . Odimeig age cehewanagaca mein . Odocob age fulusdumeig mati bahic calein .
Odocob Jekob uqa Isip ono cabi gel 17 bilen . Odocob uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 147 .
Aria Jekob uqa cal migia bili uqana saen dodoldodon uqa melah Josef utadocob hocob madon , “ Hina eben tucumi gemo mimeg je madegan eu cagu madaga , ‘ Ija Isip ene cain hel cisihigaun , ’ aga .
Ija cal mec saenna hina ehiti nui ija asiel nijeigana ono hel cisitiga , ” don . Odocob Josef uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Hina madaga eu odi odigen , ” don .
Odocob Jekob madon , “ Cois je cagu madaga , ” don . Odocob Josef uqa odi odigiannu je cagu madon . Odocob Jekob uqa uqana cabalna bilimei inondocna Anut hetaga don .
Aria ceteh i hedocob saen leih leceb age Josef madoin , “ Hina memen uqa hag nijia , ” doin . Eunu uqa melahul lecis Manasa Ifremca ehaleceb lein .
Saen Jekob uqa edi madocobil , “ Hina melem Josef uqa hinaca hoia , ” docobil uqa gagadic mimei caji cabalna bilen .
Odocob uqa Josef madon , “ Anut Gagadic Odocca uqa Kenan mahana Lus ono ijaca calimei ono uqa eeltiti
je edi maten , ‘ Ija odocna hina fulusdumeg mati bahic calegan . Hina sihul mati calegan . Odocob ija maha i hinana sihul hina toohi cali hoqagan eu adigen . Maha i agena gaid bileceb catanigian , ’ ten .
Aria hina melem lecis ija Isip ene hinaca qee hoc ninijen cali hosin eu ale ijana mel bilesia . Ifrem Manasaca ale ijana mel Ruben Simionca cinigwe calowasan .
Hina melemenel haun melem lecis i ale tooali cali hocobilfi eu age ijana mel qee calowain . Hina melemenel eu age ceteteh age mugumuga mec eu Ifrem Manasacanadec cedoqagan .
Ija Reselnu odi odigina . Ija Mesopotemiadec ceceseligin Resel uqa Efrat cemenug Kenan mahana cal men . Odocob ija uqanu wawi ben me qee men . Eunu ija Efrat ono jic gesacna hel cisem , ” don . Qila Efrat eu Betlehem .
Odocob Jekob uqa Josef melahul lecis eu mecialimei uqa sisildon , “ Mel i ale indec ? ” don .
Odocob Josef uqa memeg jejeg hewi madon , “ Eu ija melamiel lecis Anut uqa Isip ene iten , ” don . Odocob Jekob uqa madon , “ Ehali ijaca hocom eelaligen , ” don .
Aria Jekob uqa toia mennu ameg eu me bahic qee . Uqa mecii cuhadocwe qee . Eunu Josef uqa melahul eu memeg cemenug ehali leceb uqa cotaali cogaalen .
Odocob Jekob uqa Josef madon , “ Ija hina olain haun qee figaun em qa qila Anut odocna ija hina melemenelha meciadigina , ” don .
Odocob Josef uqa melahul eu ale uqa memegna gobnadec cedalen . Odimei uqa du qahi mahana non .
Odocob Josef uqa melahul lecis eu cedalen . Odimei Ifrem Jekob eben ansena isec muden . Odocob Manasa Jekob eben meulana isec muden . Odimei ehali memegca cemenug len .
Odonqa Jekob uqa eben wadacalimei eben meula eu Ifrem ilona men qa Ifrem uqa milum . Odimei uqa eben anse eu Manasa ilona men qa Manasa uqa matu .
Odocob uqa Josef eeldudu je edi maden , “ Anut ija memiel Ebraham Aisakca ale uqa amegna cobosin uqa mel i ale eelaleiale . Anut ija cofteten cocobi hu qila saen ina gadac uqa eelaleiale .
Ensel ija aisais me qeenadec besiti oiten eu uqa mel i ale eelaleiale . Odocob ija ijanica ija memiel ijanagaca eu aleca bileiale . Odocob alena sihul mati bahic fulusdosiale , ” en .
Aria Josef uqa memeg eben meula eu Ifrem ilona memen fimei uqa eu odinu waug qee nijel . Eunu uqa memeg eben eu umei waldu ehi li Manasa ilona mecnu odon .
Odimei Josef uqa madon , “ O mei eu odi qee . I eu uqa matu hina eben meula eu i ilona maga , ” don .
Qa uqa memeg cuculi bili madon , “ O melami , ija dugina , ija dugina . Uqaha uqana sihul hibna sihul ben oso caloqagan . Qa uqa waliag milum eu uqana sihul age benben caloqagan . Euqa uqa matuna sihul wooldoc caloqagan , ” don .
Eunu uqa deel euna eelali maden , “ Isrel age ale ijanalana eel docobdocob oqagan . Age madoqagan , ‘ Anut odocna age Ifrem Manasaca cinigwe caleigale , ’ oqagan , ” en . Eunu Jekob uqa eeldoc je euna Ifrem Manasa aqunitu men .
Odocob Jekob uqa Josef madon , “ Ija cal mige dodoldudugin hina fecitem . Qa Anut uqa hinaca biligian . Odimei ehihi nui hina asinel agena mahana mihigian .
Sekem , maha laloca , ija Amo dana ebeneganadec , sigin qalicana cacadi cawaladem , maha eu hina walinel qee adigaun qa hina ihigina , ” don .
Odocob Jekob melahul cunug utaadeceb hocobil maaden , “ Alilti tawecebil ceteh oso hibna caligian eunu maadigen .
Jekob melahul age , cegulimeig dah meiga . Age memega Isrel dah mudeiga .
Ruben , hina melami matu , hina ijana gagadic odoc . Saen ija dana ibuldom eu hina ijana mel matu calem . Hina ijain eu ben bahic , hina uwein eu gagadic odocca .
Hina wa sil quhulina cinigwe . Qa hina ijana cabi caja , ija aideni cinigwe , euca nijesin . Odocob hina ija majani hewitem . Eunu hina matu cudun qee ogaun .
Simion Liwaica ale waliagwaliag . Alena han sigin eu hannu gelehinca .
Ale gemanala beceb dana leih aqecebil cal mein . Odimesi ale udocnu bulmakau jaimiga qahiqahi belesin . Eunu ija alena je jahuni madecna qee gabanaligaun . Odocob ija alena cegulecna qee biligaun .
Alena gemanala eu gagadic bahic eunu ija geldugina . Ale olohonola eu me qee bahic eunu ija geldugina . Ija odocomin age Isrel mahana qatani bilisadoqagan . Ija odocomin age filigandumeig Isrel dana gami gabandoqagan .
Juda , hina walinel age hina binain suluqagan . Hinana cad benega hewegan . Hina walinel age hina amenna dunuga qahoqagan .
O Juda , hina laion haun cinigwe . Uqa dool qumei uqana cudunna ceselena . Uqa titiqimei nijina . Oso uqa seelecnu qee tulidona .
Juda uqa ilo uqana gom hewigian . Odocob uqana sihul age himec gaidgaid maha ilo biluqagan . Uqa ilo bibileb dana mahamaha cunug agena bagol utecnu hoqagan .
Uqana cesel wain gugna qagigian . Uqana cesel haun wain me bahic batacna qagigian . Uqa uqana lotoc ceteteh wain muhucna cusigian .
Uqa ameg eu gagatucca wain muhuc cinigwe . Uqa aig eu senenec su cinigwe .
Sebjulan uqa macas gesacna biligian . Uqana lanna eu macas tiliec nijigian eu wag benbennu me bahic . Uqana maha gadac eu nui Saidon gadac .
Isaka uqa cesel gagadicca cinigwe . Uqa ud lecis gemo nijina .
Qa uqa jaen mudec cudun me bahic fena . Odocob maha eu fecnu galeca fena . Eunu uqa ud gahidocnu gob qahi biligian . Age madocobil uqa cabi dana meceb cabi gagadic utuqagan .
Dan uqa uqana dana cajaca gesiladigian . Euqa age Isrel jobon medeh leih cinigwe .
Dan uqa man sononec jic gesacna cinigwe caligian . Euqa man sononec aqi jeceb cal meginanu . Uqa hos jaih bisoc qu jenanu . Odocob hos uqa dana qeludeceb ijag tagtag toninanu .
O Tibud , hina ija cahahategannu sumihigina .
Gad uqa heje dana hejenu humeig uqaca han moqagan . Qa uqa waldumei jabadigian .
Ase uqana maha eu sab me bahic caligian . Uqa sab saciadugian eu kingna sab cinigwe .
Naftali uqa dia , uqana gawecna cobona , cinigwe . Uqa dia nag galecaca basadena cinigwe .
Josef uqa cesel cus cinigwe . Uqa hos cus aluh nagna tawena cinigwe .
Uqana cad uqaca han mecnu gagadic hogina . Age olohonogana uqa qocnu qali gusegina .
Qa Jekobna Anut Gagadic Odocca eu uqa gagadic odoc utina . Anut eu uqa Isrel agena cofadec , uqa Isrelna gagadic odoc . Eunu uqana qali eu iilalecca qee tawena . Odocob uqa uwen eu gagadicca .
Hina memen uqana Anut eu cesulhena . Anut Gagadic Odocca uqa eelhena . Uqa edi eelhena . Wa ohisdec ihena . Wa tut maha dunuhdec ihena . Mel sim mati bahic ihena .
Macin bobogca ihena . Aluh ihena . Aluhnadec ceteteh me bahic gaid bileceb catanigian eu ihena . Ceteteh i cunug Josef ilona biliale . Ceteteh i dana uqa waliagul qisacadi bilina eu uqa ilona biliale .
Benjamin uqa qa cus hanca cinigwe . Qasil uqa uqana dool sabnu qon eu jena . Wesu uqa ceteteh hannadec cedena eu ila mena , ” en .
I age eu Isrel agena jobon medeh 12 . Odocob i eu eeldoc je age memega odi maaden . Uqa eeldoc je cunug agenu osahicosahic aden eu agenu ihoc filfil siwiaden .
Odocob Jekob uqa melahul je gatiti edi maaden , “ Ija asiel cal mein eu gami nuecnu saen eu dodoldona . Ija cal mecemin ija asiel gami meen hel Efron Hitdec uqana cabina nijina ono hel cisiteiga .
Meen hel eu Makpela cabina euqa Mamri cemenug Kenan mahana nijia . Meen hel eu Ebraham uqa qalqalnu Efron Hitdec dana ebennadec cabi euca faji on .
Ono Ebraham uqa aideg Saraca hel cisalein . Ono Aisak uqa aideg Rebekaca ale hel cisalein . Ono ija Lia hel cisem .
Cabi meen hel euca Ebraham uqa Hit dana ebeneganadec faji on . Ono ija hel cisiteiga , ” aden .
Aria Jekob uqa je gatiti melahul maadimei uqa jaih mahanadec suli u cabalna men . Odimei uqa siw ehi bi helimei kis on .
Odocob Josef uqa memeg tatacan tonimei qaqaji bili memeg cotadon .
Odocob Josef uqa uqana cabi dana maadeceb age memeg deweg saen cecelac nijigiannu mool joudein .
Odocob dana eu age Josef memeg deweg hel cisecnu saciadodogin deel 40 ihoc len . Deel 40 eu cal mecebil hel cisadecnu dewenega ganac saciadogina uqana gadac bahic . Odocob Isipdec dana age Jekobnu deel 70 qadaca bilein .
Odocob qadaca bilec saen eu hedocob Josef uqa Ferona dana iloilo eu age maaden , “ Ija coni umeig Fero maduteiga .
Edi madoiga , ‘ Saen ija mei uqa cal migia bili bibili bilei uqa oditeceb ija je cagu madem . Ija uqa meen hel uqa saciadon Kenan mahana nijia ono hel cisidugen em . Eunu culitecem ija nuimig ija mei hel cisimig haun ceseli hugen , ’ doiga , ” aden .
Odocob Fero uqa wadacdoc je ceseli suldumei madon , “ Hina memen odi odiheceb je cagu madem eu odi odoga . Timeg memen hel cisiga , ” don .
Eunu Josef uqa memeg hel cisigiannu ten . Odocob Ferona dana iloilo cunugca uqana jonadec dana matu cunugca Isipdec dana benben cunugca age Josef gami belein .
Uqana talca uqa waliagulca uqa memegna talca eu cunug uqaca belein . Agena mel simca sipsipca memeca bulmakauca age himec Gosen ono bilein .
Dana karisnaca hos guhadoin ageha uqa gami belein . Euqa dana am ben bahic belein .
Belimeig age wit tudoc cudun , Atad eu Jodan cemenug , ono calimeig age ono haun conoga suli umeig qada ben bahic qajein . Odocob Josef uqa ono deel eben naha gic lecisca haun qada qaqaji gehel bilen .
Aria dana cajaca Kenan mahanadec age wit tudoc cudun , Atad , ono qada qaqajegin meciadimeig age madein , “ I eu Isip agena gehel ben , ” ein . Eunu cudun eu Jodan cemenug eu ijan Abel-Misraim qoin .
Eunu Jekob melahul age uqa maaden eu odi odoin .
Age gahidu ehi belimeig Kenan mahana meen hatin Makpela cabina nijia , eu Mamri cemenug , ono hel cisein . Meen hatin euca cabica osoben Ebraham uqa qalqalnu Efron Hit dana ebennadec faji cedalen .
Odocob Josef uqa memeg hel cisi hedumei uqa waliagulca dana cunug uqaca memeg hel cisuqagannu tein eu gami age haun ceseli Isip noin .
Aria Josef waliagul age memega cal meceb fimeig age madein , “ Adi Josef uqa egenu gaid gemag benafa . Ege me qee odudom . Eunu wadacdugianfa ? ” ein .
Eunu age Josef je edi suldutumeig madoin , “ Ege memige uqa qee cal mec bibili bilei
hina mahecnu magen . Uqa edi magen , ‘ Hina walinel me qee odihein eu dahin celeiale . Hina silail eu cagasiadagale , ’ gen . Eunu hina qila ege , hina memen uqana Anutna cabi dana , ege me qee odihom eu cagasigiga , ” doin . Saen Josef uqa je suldoin eu dah mimi uqa qajen .
Odocob uqa waliagul age agedodoc hu mahana bilimeig dunuga qaqahi madoin , “ Ege hinana cabi dana , ” doin .
Qa Josef uqa maaden , “ Cain cucuiowain . Ija Anutwe uqana cudunna qee tawigaun .
Age me qee oditecnu odoin qa Anut uqa odocob ija me bilem . Euqa ija dana ben miten . Eunu ija dana cajaca mati bahic cal mecnadec cahahaadecnu ihoc .
Eunu cain cucuiowain . Ija ageca agena mel simca cofadigen , ” aden . Odimei uqa cesuladecnu je me me maaden .
Odocob Josef uqa Isip ono memegna talca bilein . Uqa cebac bilen eu uqana cabi gel cunug gabandoc eu 110 .
Uqa cebac bibili bilei uqa dodigul , euqa Efraim uqana mel , agena mel , eu meciaden . Uqa melah , Manasa , uqana mel , Makia , euqa uqa dodigul euha uqa cebac bibili bilei cedadeceb age ijanaga eu uqana tal ijanagaca gabandoc tawen .
Odocob Josef uqa waliagul maaden , “ Ijana cal mec dodoldona qa Anut uqa cofadimei maha inadec ehadi nui maha uqa Ebraham , Aisak , Jekobca adigiannu je cagu maaden ono madigian , ” aden .
Odocob Josef uqa Isrel melahul maadeceb age je edi cagu madein , “ Anut uqa maha inadec ehigi nuigian saen euna ege hina tefulinha osoben hewi beleqan , ” ein .
Eunu Josef uqa Isip ono cal men . Uqana cabi gel 110na cal men . Odocob age deweg saen cecelac nijigiannu mool joudimeig deweg ganac eu cudaug dunuh tacein .
Jaqec je i Jisas Krais uqana sihul ijanaganu je . Jisas uqa Dewid sihulnadec , odocob Dewid uqa Ebraham sihulnadec .
Ebraham uqa Aisak memeg . Odocob Aisak uqa Jekob memeg . Odocob Jekob uqa Juda waliagulca memega .
Odocob Juda uqa Peres Seraca memela . Ale anala eu Tema . Odocob Peres uqa Hesron memeg . Odocob Hesron uqa Ram memeg .
Odocob Ram uqa Aminadab memeg . Odocob Aminadab uqa Nason memeg . Odocob Nason uqa Salmon memeg .
Odocob Salmon uqa Boas memeg . Uqa anag eu Rehab . Odocob Boas uqa Obed memeg . Uqa anag eu Rut . Odocob Obed uqa Jesi memeg .
Odocob Jesi uqa King Dewid memeg .
Odocob Solomon uqa Riaboam memeg . Odocob Riaboam uqa Abaisa memeg . Odocob Abaisa uqa Esa memeg .
Odocob Esa uqa Jehosafat memeg . Odocob Jehosafat uqa Joram memeg . Odocob Joram uqa Usia memeg .
Odocob Usia uqa Jotam memeg . Odocob Jotam uqa Ehas memeg . Odocob Ehas uqa Hesekias memeg .
Odocob Hesekias uqa Manasa memeg . Odocob Manasa uqa Emos memeg . Odocob Emos uqa Josaia memeg .
Odocob Josaia uqa Jekonaia waliagulca memega . Saen euna Isrel dana cajaca age Babilon ono belimeig gihacdoc bilein .
Age Babilon ono gihacdoc bibileig Jekonaia uqa Sialtiel memeg . Odocob Sialtiel uqa Serababel memeg .
Odocob Serababel uqa Abiut memeg . Odocob Abiut uqa Elaiakim memeg . Odocob Elaiakim uqa Eso memeg .
Odocob Eso uqa Sedok memeg . Odocob Sedok uqa Ekim memeg . Odocob Ekim uqa Elaiat memeg .
Odocob Elaiat uqa Eleasa memeg . Odocob Eleasa uqa Matan memeg . Odocob Matan uqa Jekob memeg .
Odocob Jekob uqa Josef memeg .
Eunu sihul cunug eu Ebrahamnadec leceb Dewid calen eu sihul 14 . Odocob sihul cunug eu Dewidnadec leceb Isrel dana cajaca age Babilon ono belimeig gihacdoc bilein saenna calen eu sihul 14 . Odocob sihul cunug eu Isrel age Babilon ono gihacdoc bilein saennadec leceb Krais calen euha sihul 14 .
Jisas cali honnu je eu odi nijia . Jisas anag Maria uqa Josef col codoc bibili uqa qee ocna Kis Gun odocna waugca men .
Uqana dana , Josef , uqa Anut amegna tutuc coboloi . Odimei uqa Maria waugca ec dumei uqa culdigen ec cisdon . Euqa uqa Marianu cewudec je uqa dewegna cain hoiaunnu naha jahuni culdigen ec cisdon .
Odi cisdudu cocobon Tibudna ensel Josef witic us ninijen bebelecna camas mimei madon , “ O Josef , hina Dewid sihulnadec , hina aiden Maria ocnu cain cucuiagaun . Faga , uqa melca eu Kis Gunnadec .
Uqa mel baseceb uqa uqana dana cajaca agena silailnu fadalowainnu cahahaadigian , eunu hina uqa ijan Jisas qogan , ” don .
Eu Tibudna je uqa je hahun madec dana cona maden eu ihoc ligiannu ceteh eu calen . Je hahun madec dana uqa wele odi maden :
“ Feiga , mel aid taula oso waugca mimei mel basigian . Odocob age mel eu ijan Emanjuel qoqagan , ” en . Je eu Anutna jaqec je tawena . ( Ijan Emanjuel eu uqana gug eu , “ Anut egeca biluquna . ” )
Odocob Josef uqa us niji cajimei Tibudna ensel maden eu odi toodu uqana caja , Maria , ehuden .
Euqa Josef uqa Maria mel qee basec ninijen uqaca qee niji lesin . Mel baseceb uqa ijan Jisas qon .
Maria uqa Jisas Betlehem jobon ono Judia hatuna baseceb Herod uqa king bilen . Saen euna haiden agena doc silecca dana age cam tobi becnadec Jerusalem jobon cali humeig
dana sisiladi maadein , “ Mel sim haun uqa Juda agena king cali hon eu ana bilia ? Ege uqana malaqa ono cam tobi becna isec camas meceb fimeb ege amegna gob cehimeb uqanu cuha feqannu hoqa , ” adein .
Odocob King Herod je eu madecebil dah mimei geh cisdon , odocob Jerusalem dana cajaca cunugha eunu geh cisdoin .
Odocobil Herod uqa ihanec dana benbenca loo je iwaladec danaca utaadeceb cegulecebil uqa sisiladi maaden , “ Krais i Anut uqa suldocob uqa Anutna dana cajaca cahahaadecnu hugian eu cel jobon cali hugian ? ” aden .
Odocob age madoin , “ Uqa Betlehem jobon Judia hatuna cali hugian . Je hahun madec dana agena je odi jaqec wele nijia :
‘ O Betlehem , Judia hatuna , king uqa Isrel dana cajaca cofadigiannu eu Betlehem ono cali hugian . Eunu Juda jobon benben age hina qee woolhegina , ’ jaqec je taweia , ” doin .
Odocobil Herod uqa doc silecca dana jahuni utaadeceb hocobil uqa malaqa cel saen cali hon eunu sisiladen .
Age silditocobil dumei Betlehem jobon belecnu dado madimei maaden , “ Ijaha nui mel eunu cuha figennu age uqanu megi cuhadoigale . Odocob age eu gulucdu fimeig hu sateigale , ” aden .
Odocob age kingna je dumeig Betlehem jobon beloqagannu belein . Odocob malaqa wele cam tobi becna isec fein eu aquniaadi , jo mel bilen eu ohis cehi qudu tawen .
Age malaqa fimeig age wawaga gehca ceelen .
Odocob age jona limeig melca uqa anag Maria ha fecialimeig age mel amegna gob cehi jogoimeig uqanu cuha fein . Odimeig agena bokis qosocdumeig goldca , gilic ja manecebil dedeman meca , gilic dedeman meca umeig age toinanaga osoosoca Jisas utein .
Odocob Anut uqa age bebelecna maadi maaden , “ Herod cemenug haun ceseli cain belowain , ” aden . Maadeceb dumeig age jic osona agena hatuna ceseli belein .
Doc silecca dana age wele belecebil Tibudna ensel Josef us ninijen bebelecna camas mimei madon , “ Faga , Herod uqa mel wawali li qocnu madena . Eunu hina caji mel anagca cedalimeg busali Isip hatuna nui biliga . Ija mahecemin haun ceseli ene hogan , ” don .
Odocob Josef uqa witic cajimei mel anagca cedalimei Isip hatuna nui bilein .
Odimeig age Isip hatuna bibilegin li Herod uqa cal men . Saen euna Tibudna je hahun madec dana uqana je ihoc ligiannu ceteh eu calen . Je hahun madec dana uqa wele odi maden : “ Ija melami Isip ono bibilen utadocomin Isipnadec cali hon , ” en .
Herod uqa doc silecca dana age ija uhultiti woolti belein imei gemag ben bahic ben . Odimei uqa han dana suladeceb age mel manahal age cabi gel lecis qee wooladec eundec cunug age Betlehem jobonca hatu cemenugca ono bilein eu aqi hedoin . Uqa doc silecca dana malaqa cel saen wasen sisiladeceb madocobil don eu toodu mel aqeceb cal mein .
Eu odocna je hahun madec dana Jeremaia uqana je ihoc len . Uqa wele odi jaqen :
“ Rama jobonna qajec ben bahic dah mein . Qada qajec ben bahic onodec hon . Resel uqana melnu qada qajena . Mel cal mein eunu qada qajena . Age wahohog je madocobil dah mecnu culen , ” en .
Herod cal meceb Isip hatu ono Tibudna ensel bebelecna Josefca camas mimei
madon , “ Dana age madi , mel qoqan , ein age wele cal mein . Eunu cajimeg mel anagca cedalecem ceseli Isrel hatuna beleiga , ” don .
Odocob Josef cajimei mel anagca cedaleceb ceseli Isrel hatuna hoin .
Humeig Herod melah Akeleas memeg hehuldi king bibilen eu madocobil dumei uqa Judia hatuna bilecnu cucuien . Anut uqa Josef bebelecna dado mudeceb Galili hatuna nuimeig
Nasaret jobon ono bilein . Je hahun madec dana age wele odi madein , “ Age uqa Nasaretdec doqagan , ” ein . Eunu je hahun madec dana agena je oso ihoc ligiannu age Nasaret jobon ono bilein .
Saen euna Jon , wa joadec dana , cajimei Judia hatuna wadau ono cocobi me je qasali maaden .
Uqa maaden , “ Sao cul jobon eu age cemenega hona . Eunu agena silailnu tului falicdoigale , ” aden .
Ge , Jon uqa dana eu Anut uqa je hahun madec dana , Aisaia , cona eunu maden . Uqa wele odi maden : “ Dana jejeg oso uqa wadauna bibili utai maadena , ‘ Tibudna jic saciadoiga . Uqana jic tutuc mudeiga , ’ adena , ” en .
Jon uqa kamel bagicna lotoc mudec tacoloi , odimei uqa wailohna dool ganacna oologam mudec taqoloi , odimei uqa sisca mehud uqana waca joloi .
Saen euna dana cajaca age Jerusalem bileginaca , dana cajaca age Judia hatu cunugna bileginaca , dana cajaca age jobonjobon Jodan Wa cemenug bileginaca age Jonca lein .
Limeig age agena silailnu je qasali madocobil Jon uqa Jodan Wana wa joaden .
Odocob Jon uqa Farisi Sadjusica mati age uqa wa joadigiannu uqaca hohogin feciadimei maaden , “ Age man sononec nag me qee ! In madeianu age Anutna gemag bec jawe hugia odona euna busalecnu age ihoc , egina ?
Agena silailnu mele bahic culimeig tului falicdumeig Anutna je qee tefacdoginanufi me odoc oso odoiga eu ihacteiga .
Euqa ija mele maadigina , Anut uqa meen ene nijegina eu cedimei Ebraham talacul euna madecnu ihoc . Eunu age cain cisdudu madowain , ‘ Ebraham ege asige . Eunu Anutna gemag bec egeca qee hoiaun , ’ owain .
Sapol na gug qetecnu wele taweia . Na cunug aig me qee qona uqa qetimei jana heligian , ” aden .
“ Ija age agena silailnu wele tului falicdoinnu wana wa joadigina qa oso hib tooti hona , uqana gagadic odoc ijana gagadic odoc wooldona . Uqa dana meca bahic . Ijaqa dana meca qee . Ija uqana cabi dana me bahic ihoc qee , ija uqana jaih tacec hewecwe qee . Uqa age Kis Gunna janaca wa joadigian .
Uqa sawolca hona . Sawol euna wit aig cunug eeldocnuca , wit aig uqana jo bisna mecnuca hona . Odimei uqa witna tetec ja qee cafulina euna manigian , ” aden .
Saen euna Jisas Galilidec Jodan Wana len . Uqa Jon uqa wa joudigiannu Jonca limei
madon , “ Ijaha wa joitigale , ” don . Odocob Jon uqa cahacdudu madon , “ Hina ija wa joitegan eu me bahic . Hina eetanu ija hina wa joihecnu matagana ? ” don .
Odocob Jisas Jon jejeg hewi madon , “ Anut madena eu cunug toodu odocnu eu tutuc . Eunu qila culimeg gad wa joitigale , ” don . Odi madocob Jon cois imei wa jouden .
Jisas wa joc umei uqa mahucwe wa ocna ti tatawen sao ohis jic cebec hudeceb uqa Anutna Kis cuhudid cinigwe ni uqaca bilen fen .
Odocob sao ohisdec ha jejeg oso camas mi maden , “ Ija melami nelugca ihen . Ija uqanu wawi ben ceelena , ” en .
Saen euna Seten uqa Jisas temdu figiannu Kis Gun uqa Jisas iwaldocob wadauna nuen .
Uqa deel 40 cahineg witicca sab qee jec bilen . Saen hedocob wen don .
Wen dodon temgec eu uqaca limei madon , “ Hina Anut Melahfi meen i maadecem sab ibuldocob jaga , ” don .
Euqa Jisas uqa Seten jejeg hewi madon , “ Anutna jaqec je eu odi madena : ‘ Sab jec himec dana cebac bilec qee adena qa je cunug Anut conadec cali hona eu dana cebac bilec adena , ’ ena , ” don .
Odocob Seten uqa Jisas ehudimei jobon gunna ehi ti tempel qab tatacanna muden .
Mudimei madon , “ Anutna jaqec je eu odi madena : ‘ Anut uqana ensel maadeceb hina jaim meenna qee tudoiaunnu age hina ebenegana hewihi ehi ni mihuqagan , ’ ena . Eunu hina Anut Melahfi busali tonoga , ” don .
Jisas Seten jejeg hewi madon , “ Anutna jaqec je osoha madena : ‘ Tibud , hinana Anut , eu cain temdu fagaun , ’ ena , ” don .
Odocob Seten uqa haun Jisas ehudi aluh benna ehi ti muden . Mudimei mahamaha cul cunug agena tumutum cahulecca ihacdudu madon ,
“ Faga , hina amina gob cehi ijanu cuha fecemfi fagana eu cunug culihigen , ” don .
Odocob Jisas Seten jejeg hewi madon , “ Anutna jaqec je odi madena : ‘ Tibud uqa hinana Anut uqanu cuha faga , uqa himec cewel utugale ! ’ ena , Eunu Seten , cuculti nuuga , ” don .
Odocob Seten uqa Jisas cuculdi nueceb ensel age hu Jisas cewel utoin .
Aria , Jisas uqa age Jon hewimeig gihacdoc jona mudein ec dumei uqa Galili hatu ono nuen .
Odimei uqa Nasaret culimei Kapaneam jobon nui bilen . Kapaneam jobon eu Galili wa gad cagocna isec nijina , eu Sebjulan sihulca Naftali sihulca agena hatu gadac nijina .
Je hahun madec dana , Aisaia , je oso wele maden eu ihoc ligiannu odi odon . Uqa odi jaqen :
“ Sebjulan sihulca , Naftali sihulca , alena hatu eu Galili wa gad cagocna isec nijia , Jodan Wa ono isec , Galili hatu Juda dana qee eundec agena ,
hatu euna dana cajaca age tuna biloloig eu fulacdoc ben oso fein , dana cajaca age cal mec hatuna tuna biloloig , eu fulacdoc ben oso iletaden , ” Aisaia odi jaqen .
Saen ina Jisas uqa dana cajaca je qasali maadi sanan mimei maaden , “ Sao cul jobon eu age cemenega hona . Eunu agena silailnu tului falicdoigale , ” aden .
Jisas uqa Galili wa gad cagocna cocobi dana oso waliagca fecialen , eu Saimon , age Pita egina , uqa waliag Andruca . Ale cimec ben wana hehelesin fen . Ge , age cul dool cedec dana .
Odocob Jisas maalen , “ Hu tootecebil ija odalecemin ale dana cajaca cedadowasan , ” alen .
Maaleceb mahuc bahic alena cimec ben cuculesi uqa toodu belesin .
Uqa nag bahic onoca limei dana oso waliagca fil fecialen , eu Jems , uqa Sebedi melah , uqa waliag Jonca . Ale memela , Sebedica , agena wagna bibileig cimec ben tatalec eu haun wewegi bilein . Odocob Jisas utaalen .
Mahuc bahic ale wag memelaca cuculadi limesi Jisas toodu belesin .
Jisas uqa Galili hatu cunug cocobi nuen . Uqa Juda agena cuha jonana limei dana cajaca iwaladen . Odimei uqa sao cul jobonnu me je qasali maaden . Odimei uqa dana cajaca agena hag filfilca age dewenega laleg mein eundec filfilca me maden .
Age uqa hutannu je saec eu Siria hatu cunugna ihoc len . Odocob age dana cajaca hag gug filfil me qee maden eundecca , dain ben aden eundecca , buga me qee hewadein eundecca , dana caja titi hudec hagca age gaid dewenega qeleceb toni mahulegina eundecca , dana tefulunuga laleg mi cal mein eundecca cedadi Jisasca ahocobil Jisas uqa me maden .
Dana cajaca am ben age Galili hatunadecca , Dekapolis hatunadecca , Jerusalemdecca , Judia hatunadecca , Jodan Wa ono isec hatunadecca age toodu belein .
Jisas uqa dana cajaca mati bahic uqaca hohogin feciadimei uqa aluh osona ti bibilen uqana malogom uqaca hoin .
Odocobil uqa uqana malogom iwalaadi maaden :
“ Dana age Anutnu doc dumanaga ihoc qee eunu dogina eundec saona gun cul eu agena . Eunu age eeladecca bilegina .
Dana age qada qajegina eundec Anut age wahohogadigian . Eunu age eeladecca bilegina .
Dana age gemanaga jocosaigca eundec mahamaha cunug eu age mugumuga oqagan . Eunu age eeladecca bilegina .
Dana age tutuc odoc ihoc ligiannuca , agedodoc agena odoc tutuc migiannuca odogina eu odi sab wen adenaweca , wa gab adenaweca eundec Anut uqa cesuladeceb age ihoc oqagan . Eunu age eeladecca bilegina .
Dana age cotogail walocca bibilegin feciadimeig wawaga qocob me madegina eundec age saen osona walocca bibilebil Anut feciadimei waug qocob me madigian . Eunu age eeladecca bilegina .
Dana age wawaga cataniec eundec age Anut ola foqagan . Eunu age eeladecca bilegina .
Dana age maul qetegina eundec age ijanaga Anut melahul oqagan . Eunu age eeladecca bilegina .
Dana age tutuc odoginanu aaqati tootooadec gahidogina eundec saona gun cul eu agena . Eunu age eeladecca bilegina , ” aden .
“ Dana mahanadec eundec age , age ijana bilegina eunu cewadimeig aaqati tootooadimeig age agenu je me qee uhulaadi madegina saen euna age eeladecca bilegina .
Odi bahic ha dana age je hahun madec dana wele biloloig eu aaqati tootooadoloig . Age sao jobonna ameg me bahic oqagan . Eunu age wawaga me meceb ceeli bileigale , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Age odi mahamahanu macas bilegina . Euqa macas uqana mug qah becebfi adi haun mugca migian ? Macas qah bec eu ceteh osonu qee ihoc lena . Age dana lahacluhucdoqagannu helegina , ” aden .
“ Age odi mahamahanu fulacdoc bilegina . Jobon ben aluhna cehein nijia eu jahunec nijecnu qee nijel .
Dana age gowoc oso madacdumeig hal dunuh qee tacena qa age gowoc ohisna caqusegina . Odocobil jona bilegina eundec cunug fulacadena .
Dana age agena me odoc eu fimeig age Memega sao jobon bilia uqa binan suluqagannu age eu odiwe agena gowoc madacdocobil eu dana fulacadeiale , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Ija mele maadigina , sao mahaca qee mudigian deel qee cali hoc ninijeb loo je jaqec naha nag osolha qee fadaleiaun . Loo je ninijeb li ceteh cunug ihoc ligian . Eunu age ijanu uqa Mosesna loo jeca je hahun madec dana agena iwaladec jeca bebesi qee mudigiannu hon odi cain cisdowain . Qeeo , ija loo jeca agena iwaladec jeca qee mudigennu qee holom qa ija loo jeca agena iwaladec jeca toodu bahic ihoc ligiannu hom .

Ija maadigina , agena tutuc odoc eu Farisica loo je iwaladecca agena tutuc odoc qee wooldocobfi ageha saona gun culna qee lowain . Eunu dana oso loo je nag odi besimei dana odi ha toodu odocnu iwaladena eu uqanu saona gun culna age uqa caunca qee oqagan . Osoqa loo je toodu odimei dana ha odi odocnu iwaladena eu saona gun culna ijan meca ugian , ” aden .

Jisas je haun maaden , “ Loo je age jajanagail wele oin eu age dogina eu odi madena : ‘ Hina oso cain qocom cal meiaun . Oso qocob cal meceb eu uqa gesilec jona ligian , ’ ena ec je nijia .
Ijaqa maadigina , oso uqa cotignu gemag bena eu gesilec jona ligian . Odocob oso uqa cotig cewudec je me qee madona eu Juda dana matu agena cegulec age dana eu gesildocnu ihoc . Odocob oso uqa cotig madona , ‘ Hina dana gad , ’ dona eu oloqanih jana lecnu ihoc , ” aden .
“ Eunu hina ihanec cabalna tatawi hinana ceteh ihandoga bibili hina cotin hina dewennu je hewihewi cobona eunu dahin fogo docobfi
hina casac hinana ceteteh ihanec cabalna ninijeb cuculi cotinca li je tutuc mudesiale . Odimeg hu hinana ceteteh ihandogale , ” aden .
“ Dana oso hina dewennu um qocobfi hinana cad gesilec dana ben uqa ebenna mihiaunnu , odocob gesilec dana ben uqa gesilec jona cofadec dana ebenna miheceb uqa gihacdoc jona tacihiaunnu eunu hina hinana cadca gesilec jona bebelesi jicna uqaca tanawecnu wawin nijiale .
Ija mele mahigina , hina meen qaig ihoc lec qee helecemfi qee bahic besihuwain , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Age jajanagail wele loo je oso oin eu ageha dogina je eu odi madena : ‘ Hina dana cajaca alena sisi jelalec cain wagalagaun , ’ ena ec je nijia .
Ijaqa maadigina , oso dana osona caja fimei nenehegdudu hewoum ena eu uqa wele waug dunuhna cajaca wal kobol odosin , ” aden .
“ Hina amen meula isec eu silail mecnu faninhigia odocobfi selimeg helagale . Hina dewen cunug oloqanih jana helowaindainnu hina dewen naha culimeg silail qee moum eu me .
Hina eben meula isec eu silail mecnu faninhigia odocobfi qeti helagale . Hina dewen cunug oloqanih jana helowaindainnu hina dewen naha culimeg silail qee moum eu me , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Wele age odi madoloig : ‘ Oso uqa aideg culdina eu uqa sisi jelec cufalec jaqec je utigian , ’ oloig ec je nijia .
Ijaqa maadigina , dana oso uqa aideg dana osoca qee leceb nijelesin euqa gauc dana caja sisi jelec cagumei caja culdina eu uqa aideg odudeceb aideg wal kobol odona . Eetanu ? Uqa aideg dana oso ocob ale wal kobol odosina . Odocob dana oso uqa caja gemug culden eu ona uqaha dana caja sisi jelec cufalimei wal kobol odona , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Ageha age jajanagail je oso oin eu mamadegin odi doin , ‘ Hina Tibud amegna ceteh oso odigen ec je cagoc oso madecemfi hina je cagoc eu cain dahin celeiaun . Hina Tibud amegna je madem eu cisdudu toodu odogale , ’ madegina ec je nijia .
Ijaqa maadigina , Tibudca ceteh osoca amegna madigina odi cain bahic owain . Odocob sao eu Anutna bilec bahim . Eunu sao amegna madigina cain owain .
Odocob maha eu bahim Anut uqa jaih tatacan mudina . Eunu maha amegna madigina cain owain . Odocob Jerusalem eu King Ben uqana jobon . Eunu Jerusalem amegna madigina cain owain .
Hinaha hina gosin osol cas lec eu senenec ibuldocwe qee , odocob hina gosin osol senenec eu cas lec ibuldocwe qee . Eunu hina ija ilomina je tutuc madigina cain agaun .
Age sisiladecebil eu melefi age ‘ Ese ’ ec dih madeigale . Qeefi , age ‘ Qee ’ ec dih madeigale . Age je eu je oso tubdufeig Setenna je ec madoqagan , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Age je oso odi madoloig ec doin : ‘ Oso uqa cotigna ameg me qee mudecebfi ageha uqa ameg me qee mudeigale . Oso uqa cotigna maih me qee mudecebfi ageha uqa maih me qee mudeigale , ’ oloig ec je odi doin .
Ijaqa maadigina , qisol mec dana age , age dewenega me qee mudegina eundec age ameg me qee wadac cain adowain . Oso hina sihom oso naha qahecebfi hina naha ha ihacdogale .
Oso hinaca cetehnu tutuac cacadesi hinana siot cawalihecebfi hinana lotoc meca ha culitogale .
Oso uqaca nuecnu kilomita osol ihoc lecnu ninichecebfi hina kilomita leciscadoc belesiale .
Oso ninihecebfi eu ceteh utugale . Oso cesultagale hecebfi cain hibemdogaun , cesuldogale , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Age je oso odi madoloig ec doin , ‘ Hina hina utuqain bilec eundecnu nalunuga magale . Hinana cad sagagadagale , ’ oloig ec je odi doin .
Ijaqa maadigina , age , dana age agenu nalunuga megina eundec himec nalunuga meginafi Anut cel ameg me adigian ? Takis cedec dana eu ageha odi odogina . Odocob age agena danah eundec himec feele ec maadeginafi age in wooldu odogina . Haiden ageha odi odogina . Euqa Memega Anut uqa me odoc eundecca me qee odoc eundecca cam sulduadena . Uqa tutuc coboginaca tutuc qee coboginaca osobennu waha sulduadena . Eunu age Memega sao jobon bilia eu age uqa melahul bilegina eu camas moqagannu age agena cadnu nalunuga meigale . Aaqati tootooadegina eundecnu Anut waug qugiannu inondoigale .



Age Memega sao jobon bilia eu uqa odoc me ihoc lec bilina . Eunu ageha agena odoc me ihoc lec bileigale , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Batut feigale . Age dana egena Anut cewel utoc foqagan imeig odocobilfi age Memega sao jobon bilia eu ameg me uqa qee adeiaun . Eunu age Anut cewel utoc eu ege odocomun dana age meciguqagan cain owain , ” aden .
“ Me hihili coboc dana age Juda agena cuha jonaca jicnaca ege binanige suluqagan imeig sawen dana loo siwiadoqa bili aquniaadi taul fuldogina . Eunu hina me hihili coboc dana eundec odi odogina cain odogaun . Ija mele maadigina , dana eundec age agena ameg oc eu wele oin .
Euqa hina wawin qocca loo siwiadec eu jahunec biligiannu hina sawen dana eundec loo siwiadecem eben meulana isec odona eu eben ansena isec cain doiaun . Odocob Memen uqa ceteh jahunecna bilia eu fena uqa ameg me ihigian , ” aden .

Jisas je haun maaden , “ Me hihili coboc dana age dana ege Anut inondocomun meciguqagan imeig Juda age cuha jonaca jicnaca tatawi Anut inondogina eunu gale ben adena . Eunu hina me hihili coboc dana Anut inondoginawe odi cain inondogaun . Ija mele maadigina , dana eundec age agena ameg oc wele oin .
Euqa hina Memen inondoga bili hina jo hamol limeg jic cebec menimeg Memen uqa jahunecna bilia eu inondoga . Odocob Memen uqa ceteh jahunecna bilia eu fena uqa ameg me ihigian , ” aden .
“ Haiden age madegina , ‘ Ege egena tibud je mati bahic madocomunfi jejenige toodu odigian , ’ egina . Eunu age inondudu je gauc madegina eu odi haiden odoginawe cain madowain .
Age Memega qee madoc ninijeb uqa agena wawaga hoolecca agena togo nijigiannu madegina eu wele dona . Eunu age haiden odogina odiwe cain odowain , ” aden .
“ Eunu age odi inondoigale : ‘ O ege Memige , hina sao jobon biligina , hina ijain gun biliale .
Hinana cul egeca hoiale . Hina con toodu odoc sao jobon ihoc lenawe odi mahana ha ihoc leiale .
Sab jecnu ba i ihoc igigale .
Dana age ege me qee odigeinnu ege dahinige celenwe hinaha egena me qee odadec eunu dahin celeiale ,
Hina ege temgecna cain ehi li migigaun . Euqa qisol mec kobol eu cagasigagale , ’ doigale , ” aden .
“ Ge , age dana age me qee odadein eu agena silail dahiniga celecebfi Memega sao jobon bilia uqaha agena silail dahig celigian .
Euqa age dana age me qee odadegina eu agena silail qee dahiniga celecebfi Memega uqa agena silailha dahig qee celeiaun , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Me hihili coboc dana eu age ege sabnu qagu biluquna eu meciguqagan imeig olanaga jugu qocca cobogina . Euqa age sabnu qagu bilecnu bibileig olanaga jugu qoc me hihili coboc dana eu odi odoginawe cain cobowain . Ija mele maadigina , dana eundec age agena ameg oc eu wele oin .
Euqa dana hina sabnu qagu biligina eu cain fecihuwainnuqa Memen jahunecna bilia eu mecihigiannu hina sabnu qagu bilecnu bibili gosin cilihdumeg olain wasacudagale . Odocob Memen uqa ceteh jahunecna bilia eu fena uqa ameg me ihigian , ” aden .

Jisas je haun maaden , “ Hina toinain haudoc nijina eunu hina wawin cisdocha nijina . Mahana cehewan eu cumucumca tontonca hewi me qee mudina , odocob heje dana ceteh euha heje ocna cawaladoqagan . Eunu age mahana cehewan meca agedodocnu haudocnu cain cabi owain . Euqa sao jobonna cehewan eu tontonca qee hewena , eu susul me qee mudecwe qee , odocob heje oc dana euha heje ocna cawaladecwe qee . Eunu age sao jobonnu age cehewanaga meca haudocnu cabi oigale , ” aden .


Jisas je haun maaden , “ Dewenna fulacdoc eu hina amen . Eunu hina amen me nijinafi hina dewen cunug fulacdocca nijina .
Euqa hina amen galuc mecebfi dewen cunug tu migian . Eunu fulacdoc eu wawinna bilia eu cafulecebfi wawin eu gagatucna bahic bilina ! ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Cabi dana oso uqa dana ben lecis alena cabi ocwe qee . Ge , uqa oso sagagduduqa osonu nalug migian . Qeefi , uqa osonu waug nijigian qa oso cewudigian . Odiwe ha age Anutca maha cehewanagaca agena tibud mumudi osoben cabi u calecnu qee nijel , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Eunu ija age maadigina , age mahana cebac bilecnu cain jaen aqeiaun . Eeta sab jeqan , eeta gab jeqan , cain owain . Age deweneganu ha cain jaen aqeiaun . Eeta taceqan cain owain . Agena cebac bilec eu sab jec wooldona . Dewenega eu lotoc wooldona .
Man fululec sao bisilag cobogina eu meciadeigale . Age ceteteh qee cehegina . Ageha wal meceb ceteteh jo bisna qee tacegina . Euqa age Memega sao jobon bilia uqa moot madena . Age agena fajec eu man fululec agena fajec wooldoc bahic bilegina !
Age info uqa uqana cebac bilecnu jaen qonana uqa uqana maha bilec saen nag cecelacca mudecnu ihoc ? ” aden .
“ Age eetanu lotoc tacecnu jaen ben aqena ? Age ceteh sal qoc wasena eu feiga . Age cabi qee ogina , agena lotocha qee mudegina .
Euqa ija odi maadigina , Solomon uqa lotoc tumutumca bahic taci tawen eu sal qoc bahunadec tawena i oso qee wooldol .
Euqa Anut uqa ceteh gigisac gami tacec balaca adena , ceteh eu qila tawena uqadec jana helecebil cijina . O age wawaga meleec meca qee , age dogina , Anut uqa age gigisac wooldudu tacecnu adigian .
Haiden age ceteh eu cunugnu jaen aqena . Odocob age Memega sao jobon bilia uqa age ceteh euca qeefi age maha ina bilecwe qee eu uqa dona . Eunu age jaen aqeceb eeta sab jeqan , eeta gab jeqan , cel cetehna dewenige taceqan eu cain madowain .

Euqa age casac age Anut mudecebil uqa agena king biliale , odocob age uqana tutuc coboc umeig toodoigale . Oodobil ceteh mahanadec eu toodu ageca hugian .
Deel uqadec uqadodoc jaen qocca cisdugian . Eunu age deel uqadec uqana gihacadec eunu cain jaen aqeiaun . Deel abesabes gihacadec gahidocnu ihoc gulucdoigale , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Eetanu hina cotin amegna hilican nag eu fagana qa hinadodoc amenna fan ben nijina eu qee fagana ? Qeefi , hina adi cotin madogana , ‘ Coti , cultecem hilican nag amenna nijia eu u helihigen , ’ dogana qa hina amenna fan ben nijina ? Hina me hihili coboc dana ! Casac fan ben eu hina amenna fagdoc nijia eu cagati helagale . Odocob hilican nag cotin amegna nijia eu u helecnu ihoc fegan . Gesilec age osonu je madegina gesilec euna Anut uqa age gesiladigian . Age ihoc mec dana ihoc miadegina ihoc mec euna ha Anut u hewi age ihoc miadigian . Eunu Anut age gesiladimei camasac mimi cewadeiaunnu age dana osona kobol gesildumeig cain camasac mimi cewudec je madowain , ” aden .




“ Qa age falicdu age tataladowainnu age ceteh Anutnu gun bahic nijia eu qa cain culiadowain . Ho age gilolo eu lahacluhucdowainnu agena gilolo me eu ho amagana cain helowain , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Cunug age cetehnu Anut sisildogina eu ceteh ogina . Odocobil oso ceteh walena eu ceteh gulucdona . Odocob oso jic cebec gohugohudona eu Anut huditugian . Eunu Age Anut cetetehnu inondocobil ceteh eu adigian , odocobil age wawali cobimeig ceteh walegina eu gulucdoqagan , jic cebec gohugohudocobil Anut hudiadigian .

Qeefi , age gemona dana oso uqana mel uqa memeg sab itiga jiga docobfi memeg uqa sab qee utina qa meen utinafo ?
Qeefi , age gemona dana oso uqana mel uqa memeg cul dool itiga jiga docobfi memeg uqa cul dool qee utina qa man sononec utinafo ?
Feiga , age dana gug me qee qa age agena mel ceteh me adecnu dogina . Eunu age mele dogina , Memega sao jobon bilia eu uqa age sisildogina eundec ceteh me bahic adigian !
Eunu dana filfil age agenu odadecebil gale adenawe eu odi age dana filfilnu ha odadeigale . Ge , Mosesna loo jeca je hahun madec dana agena iwaladec jeha madein agena je eu uqana caun ihen , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Fadalecna calecnu jic cebec eu bagalan , jic euha bagalan . Toodocnu eu hetec . Odocob jic cebec euna mati bahic limeig jic euna cobogina . Euqa cebac bilec catanec euna calecnu jic cebec eu sosog , odocob jic euha cacanigca . Odocob dana cajaca mati bahic jic eu gulucdumeig qee toodogina . Eunu age cebac bilec catanec euna loqaga bili jic cebec sosogna leigale , ” aden .

Jisas je haun maaden , “ Age uhulec je hahun madec dana age sipsip ganac tacimeig eu age qee waadecnu odi ageca hogina . Euqa wawaga dunuhna age qa cus olohonogaca odi nijia , age me qee bahic odadoqagan . Eunu ageca hu qauadowainnu batut feigale .
Age agena odoc aig qocnana cisadi feigale . Qam aig gagalit na mogi jecnu nijiafo ? Dan aig momos na mogi jecnu nijiafo ?
Eu odi cehelo gug me eu aig me qona , odocob na gug me qee uqa aig me qee qona .
Cehelo gug me uqa aig me qee qocwe qee , odocob na gug me qee eu uqa cehelo aig me qocwe qee .
Na uqa aig me qee qona eu codocobil toneceb cedimeig jana manegina .
Eu odiwe age uhulec je hahun madec dana agena odoc aig qocna cisadi feigale , ” aden .
“ Dana cajaca age ija ‘ Tibud , Tibud , ’ tegina eu cunug sao cul jobon dunuh qee lowain . Euqa Mei sao jobon bilia eu madena eu toodu odogina age himec loqagan .
Deel cit qoc euna mati odi matoqagan , ‘ Tibud , Tibud , ege hina ijainna je hahun madeginawe odi qee madolomfo ? Ege hina ijain hewi buga me qee eundec qee ititacadolomfo ? Ege hina ijainna kobolkobol qee odolomfo ? ’ toqagan .
Odi matecebil ija maadigen , ‘ Ija age , age ijana eu qee feciadelem . Age qisol mec kobol odogina cuculti beleiga , ’ adigen , ” aden .
Jisas je haun maaden , “ Eunu oso , ijana je dah mimei eu toodu odona , eu dana cisdoc silecca cinigwe . Dana eu uqa uqana jo maha gagadic meencana cehen .
Odocob wa ben neceb wa cue ha humei jona leceb gugula ha hu jo eu heweceb qa jo eu uqana nah maha gagadicna cehen tawennu jo qee cabatel .
Osoqa uqa ijana je dah mimei eu toodu qee odona eu uqa dana gad oso odi , uqa uqana jo wa gon esicna cehen .
Odocob wa ben neceb wa cue humei jona leceb gugula ha hu jo heweceb jo eu cabaten . Odimei jo cabati nui me qee bahic muden , ” aden .
Jisas uqa Juda agena loo je iwaladec dana oso cunug maadeinwe odi qee maadel qa uqa je Tibud gagadic odocca iwalaadi maaden . Eunu uqa je eu maadi mamaden dana cajaca age wawaga cacaden bilein , uqana iwaladec je eu wawaga qon .

Jisas uqa aluh culimei toni nuen . Toni nunuen dana cajaca am ben bahic toodu belein .
Jisas nunuen hag dana oso deweg lepraca uqa Jisas fimei uqa limei Jisas olana gob cecehi Jisasnu cuha fefei cesusdu madon , “ O Tibud , hina ija me mitiga hecebfi hina me mitecem ijana hag culteceb ija Anut amegna cataniec bilecnu ihoc , ” don .
Odocob Jisas eben huleldumei deweg qududodoi madon , “ Ija me mihiga tena . Me maga ! ” don . Saen eunadih lepra hag eu uqa dewegna culdeceb deweg hul hon .
Odocob Jisas cahacdu madon , “ Dah maga , ceteh inu oso cain sadudu cobogaun . Euqa li nawel tawec ihanec dana eu hina dewen ihacdocom maleldugian . Odimeg Moses loo je wele maden eu toodumeg hina qila me biliga dana cajaca cunug ihacadecnu Anut ihandogale , ” don .
Jisas uqa Kapaneam jobon dunuh lelen Rom agena han ilo dana 100 cofadec oso ono uqaca hu ninidudu madon ,
“ O Tibud , ijana cabi dana ijana jona hag nijia . Uqa laleg men deweg geh dain dona , ” don .
Odocob Jisas uqa jejeg hewi madon , “ Ija hinaca belimeu me mudihigen , ” don .
Euqa Rom agena han ilo dana 100 cofadec uqa madon , “ O Tibud , hina ijana jo dunuh lecnu eu ija dana me bahic ihoc qee . Faga , ijaha ijadodoc han dana ilo oso bisalu biligina . Odocob ijaha han dana leih ija bisalu bilegina . Ija oso nuuga ecemin nuina . Ija oso hoga ecemin hona . Odocob ija ijana cabi bega meh dana odi odoga ecemin uqa coni toodu odona . Eunu hina je osol madecem ijana cabi dana hag medugian , ” don .

Jisas uqa Rom agena han ilo dana 100 cofadec je eu madeceb dah mimei tumatumai toodoin eundec maaden , “ Ija mele maadigina , ija waug meleec uqana bilina cinigwe Isrel gemona oso qee gulucdolom ! ” aden .
“ Ija age maadigina , cam tobi becnadecca cam toni nocnadec ha mati hoqagan . Age Ebrahamca , Aisakca , Jekobca gami sao cul jobon ono sab jecnu biluqagan .
Age odi bibilegin Isrel dana cajaca Anut uqa age sao cul jobon bilecnu nesili ehaden eundecqa Anut ititacadeceb jobon hahagum limeig tu gagatuccana biluqagan . Ono dana age qada qaqaji maimaga kicodudu biluqagan , ” aden .
Odimei uqa Rom agena han ilo dana 100 cofadec madon , “ Wawin meleec eu toodu odihiale . Hina gad nuuga , ” don . Madodon euna bahic Rom agena han ilo dana 100 cofadec uqana cabi dana hag medon .
Odocob Jisas uqa Pitana jona limei uqa Pita momoig hag deweg daincaca hulec ninijen fen .
Odimei uqa hagca caja eu eben qududocob uqana hag culden . Odocob uqa cajimei sab jec saciadumei Jisas cewel uten .
Odocob wesu meceb dana age cotogail mati dewenega buga me qee hewadein eundec cedadecebil Jisasca ahoin . Odocob Jisas uqa buga me qee je maadeceb dana deweneganadec cali hu belein . Odimei dana cajaca cunug age hagca me maden .
Uqa je hahun madec dana , Aisaia , uqana jaqec je ihoc ligiannu odi odon . Jaqec je eu wele odi maden , “ Uqa egena hag filfil cedi gahidu nuen , ” en .
Odocob Jisas uqa dana cajaca am ben bahic talildu tatawegin fimei uqana malogom maaden , “ Ege wa gad cagoc cool ono isec beleqan , ” aden .
Odocob loo je iwaladec dana oso Jisasca humei madon , “ Iwalgec , hina anaana nunuem ija toohigen , ” don .
Odocob Jisas jejeg hewi madon , “ Qa cus agena helona nijegina , odocob man fululec agena teicna nijegina . Euqa Dana Melah uqa us nijec cudunca qee , ” don .
Odocob malogom oso uqa Jisas madon , “ O Tibud , cultecem ija casac ceseli nuimig mei heel cisigen , ” don .
Odocob Jisas jejeg hewi madon , “ Cal mec dana culadecem cal mec eundec agena heel ciseigale . Hinaqa ija tootaga , ” don .
Jisas uqa wag osona tobocob uqana malogom toodu toboin .
Age nunuegin ququlubadecwe gugula ben neceb macas me qee meceb caji qahi wag dunuh qelen . Euqa Jisas uqa us nijen .
Odocob malogom age li Jisas tulidudu madoin , “ Tibud , ege fadalecnu odoqona . Cahahagagale ! ” doin .
Odocobil uqa maaden , “ Oe age wawaga meleec meca qee . Eetanu cucuiegina ? ” aden . Odimei uqa caji gugula macasca cahacaali maaleceb manin tilien .
Dana age eu oodon fimeig tumatumai madein , “ Uqa cel dana fufuca macas qahecca uqa co toodu odosina ? ” ein .
Odocob age nui Gadara agena hatuna calein , eu Galili wa oc naha isec . Odocob dana lecis buga me qee hewalein eu ale qalqal hatinnadec cajimesi Jisas gulucdosin . Ale cus bahic . Eunu dana age jic euna nuecwe qee .
Odocob ale jejenela suli u madosin , “ O Anut Melah , hina ege eeta odigegan ? Saen qee calel hina ege me qee odigecnu hogafo ? ” dosin .
Aria , ho am ben oso ono isec sab jiji coboin .
Odocob buga me qee age Jisas ninidudu madoin , “ Hina ititacgifeg ho am euna sulgecem age dewenegana leqan , ” doin .
Odocobil Jisas maaden , “ Beleiga , ” aden . Odocob age dana lecis cuculaleig ho dewenegana lein . Odocobil ho cunugca aluh qeihqeih guguli nu Galili wa gad cagoc dunuh gotoimeig cunugca odi wa jimeig cal mein .
Odocobil dana ho cofadoloig eu age fimeig busali belein . Age taun ben limeig ceteh cunug calennu dana cajaca maadein . Age ceteh dana lecis buga me qee hewalein aleca calen eunu saadein .
Odocob dana cajaca cunug age taun euna bilein eu age limeig Jisas gulucdoin . Odimeig age Jisas fimeig dana Gadara agena hatunadec cunug Jisas cuculadi nuigiannu ninidoin .
Jisas uqa wagna tobimei wa gad cagoc leti hagen naha isec nuen . Odimei uqa uqana jobon calen .
Odocob dana leih age dana laleg hagca oso gabagabna ninijen Jisasca hehewi ehudi ahoin . Saen Jisas agena wawaga meleec eu ben bahic fimei dana laleg eu madon , “ Melami , hinana silail cagasihiga qee meia eunu wawin toogdoiale , ” don .
Odocob loo je iwaladec dana leih age togodudu madein , “ Dana eu uqa Anut cewudec je madeia , ” ein .
Euqa Jisas uqa agena cisdoc dumei maaden , “ Age wawagana cisdoc qisol je eetanu madegina ?
Cel je madec cacanigca qee ija madigen ? Ija madigen , ‘ Hinana silail cagasihiga qee meia , ’ ecfo , qee ‘ Cajimeg coboga , ’ ec madigenfo ?
Euqa Dana Melah mahana silail cagasiadecnu gagadic odoc ebenna nijia eu doqagannu ihacadigen , ” aden . Odimei uqa dana laleg hagca madon , “ Cajimeg hinana gabagab eu qahimeg hewi hinana jobon nuuga , ” don .
Odocob dana eu cajimei uqana jobon nuen .
Odocob dana ono cegulein age odi oodon fimeig cucuiein . Odimeig Anut uqa gagadic odoc eundec dana aden eu binan sulein .
Jisas uqa jobon eu culimei uqa cali li dana oso , ijan Matju , uqa takis cedec jona bibilen fen . Fimei madon , “ Tootaga , ” don . Odocob uqa cajimei Jisas toodu nuen .
Odocob hibna Jisas uqa jo euna sab jejei bilen . Bibilen takis cedec danaca , silail danaca mati hocobil age Jisas uqana malogomca gami sab jein .
Odocob Farisi age Jisas odi oodon fimeig Jisasna malogom maadein , “ Eetanu agena iwaladec uqa takis cedecca silail danaca eundec gami sab jegina ? ” adein .
